¶ begynneth lyf ſaint katherin ſenis bleſſid virgin ¶ audi filia et vide doughter ſee fructuous example vertuous liuinge edyfycaciō thy ſowle cō forte encreſe thy goſtly labour werkis pyte truſte gracious yeftes oure lorde jheſu thy wyll ſette pleſe hym hym ſecuyce holy excerciſe vertue obedyence vnder counſeyll techinge thy goſtely gouernours moche fele longe experyens inward affeccions inclynyng wyth pyte comforte haue nede bothe lyuyng dede therfore ſtrengthe cōforte thy wil al thi goſtely ſuſterē whiche lord▪ hath graciouſly choſe ſerue hym nyght day prayer meditaciō laboure bodely tyme nede ſocour helpe ſeke poure purpos lordis mercy worſhyppe wyth truſte grace leue helpe prayer tranſlate englyſſhe tongue legende bleſſid lyf holy mayde virgyn whiche callyd katheryn ſene legende compyled worſhypfull clerke fryer reymond ordre ſaynt domynik doctor deuynyte cō feſſour holy virgyn tranſlacion leue two prologue whiche begynnyng ſame clerke made latyn whiche paſſeth vnderſtondyng touche alle mater longeth lernyng cauſe moche maner vertuous lyuyng ſhall reherſyd eſpecial chapytres boke whiche generall wordes toucheth ſhortely prologue leue alſo poyntes diuynyte whiche paſſeth vnderſton dyng touche mater yt longeth lernyng thā ſayde begynning doughter ſee thou hereſt redeſt holy mayde vyrgyn thou yeue full credence ſhal wryte veryte may preuyd wythout ony feynyng biſcryptures confeſſours verefyeng creature whiche late lyued erthe alſo vytnes purpoſe put ende eche chapytre worſhypfull clerke dide whiche compyled boke latyn therfore werke begynne perfourmed name holy trynyte boke ſhall deuyded thre partyes eche parte boke ſhal departed diuerſe chapyters whiche chapyters compyled gyder begynnyng manere kalendre ye mowe redely fynde matere boke ye deſyre rede ¶ fyrſt parte boke ſhal byrth holy werkis mayde chyldhode tendre age time ſhe ſpouſed merueylouſly gracyouſly lord▪ ¶ ſeconde parte conteyneth maner conuerſacion tyme deſpouſacion lord lord wrought tyme yt ſhe paſſyd world ¶ thyrde parte ſhall ſhewe paſſyng world ſame mayde myracles whiche lord wrought lyf thus bi mercy graunt lord almyghty werke ſhall termynyd lawde holy trynyte honour glorye euer wythout ende amen capitulum j fyrſte chapytre fyrſte parte forſayde bleſſyd mayde virgyn katheryn treteth progenyte mater whiche byfyll touchyng ſhe wē te openly abrode fader moder wedded man wedded ſhe neuer wolde c iiij ¶ item feruour deuocyon wythdrawe whiche lord ſuffred encrece grace folowyng ſtronge pacience wyth whiche pacience ſhe ſuffred faders hous many iniuryes c v ¶ aboute delyueraunce whiche acombred vexed wyth fendes c x ¶ item yefte prophecye yefte ſhe delyuerd many mē wymmen fro perylles bothe body ſowle c xj ¶ item myracles whiche oure lorde wrought holy mayde vyrgyn herbes breed wyne thinges hadde none lyf c xij item ofte reſceyuynge holy ſacrament aulter myracles whiche oure lorde dyde hyr touching holy ſacrament holy relyques ſaintes ca xiij begynneth thyrde parte wherin reherſyd capitulum j deyeng holy mayde vyrgyn myracles ſhewed deth fyrſt wytneſſes whiche preſent hyr paſſyng enfourmed auctur boke whiche cap ij ¶ item merueylous thynges whiche befyll yere half fore deth holy mayde vyrgyn martyrdome ſhe ſuffred bodely wycked fendes wherof ye laſte ſhe hadde bodely dethe c iij ¶ item holy mayde vyrgyn deſyred vnbounde body wyth cryſt preuyd deuoute prayer whiche ſhe made put ende another boke whiche ſhe made boke generally ſhortely wryten boke wyth ſame oryſon c iiij ¶ item time ſhe paſſed whan ſhe paſſed worlde ſermō whiche ſhe made goſtely dyſcyples ſuſteren tofore paſſyng ſhe informed generall ſpeciall ſhold gouerne theym whan ſhe go • vyſyon whiche ſhewed matrone houre paſſyng ca v ¶ item token myracles whiche oure lorde wrought hyr dethe holy mayde vyrgyn bothe tofore beryeng ſaye myracles whiche knowe many knowe cap vj ¶ item myghty ſtronge paciens whiche mayde vyrgyn ſhewed openly fyrſt age yonge deth whiche vertu clerly preuyd ryghtfull ſhe worthy haue name holyneſſe goddes chirche erthe▪ whan ſhe made ſo fayre gloryous goddes chirche heuen chapytre recapitulacion ſayd fore worthynes alſo werynes reders alſo yf eche man may haue al thys legende may haue ſubſtaunce martyr tofore compendyouſly reherſyd laſt chapytre ¶ fyrſt chapytre fyrſt parte progenye holy mayde vyrgyn gloryous ſaint katheryn ſene mater whiche befyll touchyng ſhe went openly abrode fader moder condycions theym capitulū primū cite geene italye prouynce tuſkane ther man name janes jacob fader callyd comyn ſpeche ye contree beuencaſa james ſymple vertuous wythout fraude deceyte ony man dredynge god fleyng alle euyll deth fader moder toke wyf ſame cyte name lapa woman wythout ſuche malyce vſed amonge men ben tyme ſhe full beſy aboute longeth houſhold meynye ſeruauntes knowen openly knewe whyle ſhe liued erthe whan bothe ioyned gyder matrymonye lyuyd vertuouſly ſymplycite ſuffycient habondaunce hadde temperall godes bothe gentyll commendable byrthe reuerende lorde bleſſyd lapa graciouſly fulfylled hyr plentuouſly wyth birthe chyldren habondaunt vyne hous jacob whiche huſbond eche yere almoſt ſhe conceyued bare ſone doughter ofte fythes ij ſones two doughters tyme jacob paſſeth worlde lapa wyf ſynguler laude commendacion reherſyd ſaide mayſter reymonde confeſſour holy mayde vyrgyn glorious martyr katheryn ſhe euer ſoo lyke dyſpoſycion ſoo moderate worde occacion euer came trouble trybulacion exceded neuer ſpeche haſty ne angrye worde whan ſaw ony meyny greued herd hem ſpeke angerly bytter wordes anon comforted eche theym wyth glad • ſayde ye maner contree brother good day troubled ſpeke ſuche wordes falleth ne ſemeth v ſpeke ¶ ſpeciall lapa wyf wherſeth whan tyme one neybours dyſeſyd hym wrongfully aſked hym grete ſom̄e monye whiche owed none reaſon▪ ſoo moche vexed hym ſymple mā wyth might frendes ſupplanted hym wyth grete wronges brought hym loſſe alle godes alle tyme good man myght neuer ſuffre preſence man curſe hym wronge ne ſpeke hym harme noo wyſe ſoo moche blamed wyf lapa wyth ſofte wordes ſayd ſuffre dere wyf ye good day lord ſhall ſhewe hym therrour ſhall oure defendour whiche wordes founde ſouthe afterward veryte ſhewed openly lyke myracle payne hadde conſcyence delyuerd agayne moche hadde errid wrongfull perſecucion good man jacob thyſe wordes ſayde lapa mayſter reymonde who wordes yaue full truſte knowe knewe ſhe ſoo moche ſympleneſſe age xxiiij yere though ſhe wold haue lyed ſhe •• wde haue feyned ſuche leſyng ſoo commyn teſtymonye alle tho knewe huſbonde jacob man ful ſymple innocencye ryghtfull alwaye fleyng euyll alſo good mannys ſoftenes ſpeche ſoo vertuous alle meyny namely wymmen dame ſels taught ſoole myght ſpeke ne noo worde ſemely dyſhoneſte ſo moche one doughter whiche callyd bonauentura wedded yonge man whiche callyd nycolas ſame cyte wyth whome conuerſaunt many yong men hys age cauſe hadde nother fader ne moder thyſe men wythout ony refreynynge tongue ſpake eche other▪ wyth wyth hym foule wordes dyſhoneſte mater bonauentura att laſte toke therof ſoo grete heuynes ſhe fyll ſuche ſykenes fro day daye ſhe waxed lene vanyſſhed almoſt awaye ryght feble huſbonde ſawe aſked hyr cauſe heuyneſſe ſekeneſſe ſhe anſwerd ſayde noryſſhed myn faders hour neuer wonte ſuche wordes euery daye ſo neuer taught fader moder wherfor knowe ſothe diſhoneſte ſpeche bee avoyded fro hous wythin ſhorte tyme ye ſhall ſee deed whan huſbond herde bothe avoyded vngoodly langage▪ felawſhyppe therwyth edefyed moche euer before▪ well vertues lyuinge fader moder doughter wyf anone forbode felawes neuer ſpeke ſuche maner wordes preſens nomore dede ſoo ſoftenes honeſte jacob hous amendyd moderaunce dyſhoneſte nycolas hous whiche hadde weddyd jacob doughter ¶ ferthermore ye ſhall vnderſtonde ye jacob vſed crafte makyng colour wherwyth wollen wolle clothes ben dyed crafte vſed bothe ſonys contree ben called dyer wherfore full wonderfully god ordeyned dyer doughter ſhol made ſpouſe emperour heuen ye ſhall ſee goddes grace boke somme haue ſhewed chapytre knowe parte cyte ſom̄e confeſſour ſayd mayde katheryn moder many relygyous perſons ſeculers whiche neybours kynrede ſame jacob wyf ¶ byrthe merueylous werkinge whiche lord wrought ſhewed chylhode holy vyrgyn mayde capitulū ij whan forſayd lapa whiche lyke fructuous vyne fulfyllyng wyne jacob huſbonde bryngyng forth full ofte bothe ſones doughters befyll aboute laſte tyme berynge chyldren ordynaunce dy ſpoſycyon lordis mercy ſhe conceyued brought forth two doughters freell febyll nature moche freell bodely ſtrengthe ſemed outward▪ ſtrengthe ſtabylneſſe hadde ſyght god ¶ whan lapa moder beſely behelde theym ſhe thought well ſhe ſuffyſed nought nouryſſhe bothe forthe wyth owne mylke wherfore good auyſement ſhe commytted one smother noryſe ſhe wythhelde kepte ſtylle noryſſhed forth wyth owne mylke ſoo befyll ordynaunce lorde ſhe choſed doughter owne kepyng▪ whiche lord euerlaſtynge tyme hadde choſe vnto ſpouſe bothe reſceyued grace baptyſme nombre goddes choſe chyldren yet forſayd mayde called katheryn called johan later ſuſter whan ſhe hadde receiued grace baptyſme ſame grace ſhe went forth heuen ſhort tyme ſhe paſſed worlde katheryne abode ſtylle ſukkyng moders breſtes goddes ordynaunce ſhe ſhold drawe heuen longe cheyn • ſoulis moche lapa ye moder conſyderyd katheryn abode deed nouryſſhed dyligently hopyng ſhe choſe abyde goddes chyld ofte ſythes moder lapa wolde ſaye maiſter reymond confeſſour holy mayde ſhe louyd katheryn paſſyngly aboue alle ſones doughters euer ſhe hadde ſayde vnto hym alſo ſhe conceyued ſoo ofte ſhe myght neuer nouryſſhe ony chylde wyth owne mylke ¶ katheryn ſhe nouryſſhed forth ye ende tyme yt ſhe neded vnder nouryſſhe alle tyme ſhe conceyued ſemed oure lorde doughter hadde graunted tyme reſte traueylyng byrthe chyldren token ſhe myght come ende conceyuyng byrthe doughter whiche ſholde ateyne gete ende alle perfection ¶ yet moder lapa nouryſſyng katheryn▪ one ſhe conceyued bare doughter whiche called johan ſhe made ende beryng chyldren ſhe hadde bo • en xxv chyldren whan mayde thus broughte forth halowed god whan ſhe hadde lefte mylke toke ete brede whyle ſhe wente aboute alone began ſoo acceptable ſoo byloued tho ſawe ſoo wyſe wonderfull wordes ſhe ſpake vnnethes moder myght holde owne hous eche man aboute neybours kynrede lad home wyth theym glad myght haue wyſe ſpeche myght haue felawſhyp gladeneſſe yonge mayde soo maner gladdeneſſe paſſyng ſolace called owne ryght name katheryn eufroſyna meued calle ſoo wyſt theym ſelf ſhe afterward ſomme tyme wolde ſaye ſuppoſe myſtery cauſe ſhe purpoſed folowe ſaynt eufroſyne lyuyng confeſſour wrote legende ſuppoſed yonge mayde chyldis ſpeche vſed ſomme maner ſownynge nyghed acorded n • eufroſyne ſoo maner wolde reherce wordes called ſoo name neuertheles euer appieryd ſhe burgenyd chilhode tree ony ſuche ſhewyng fruyt brought forth afterward olde age wyſdome prudence ſpeche connyng ſweteneſſe holy conuerſacion myght reherſed wyth tongue lygthly wryte wyth penne theym knewe veryte thys whiche hadde experyence hadde alſo inward werkynge whyche ſhewed well▪ ſpeche cō uerſacion wher thorugh many mennys ſowlis drawe god hadde thorugh grace grete lykyng ſauour god ſomoche heuyneſſes excluded mennys hertes whiche conuerſaunt wyth her▪ thinges noyed ſowle put awaye alſo remembraunce eche noye angwyſſhe take awaye folowed eche man ſoo grete reſte ſtabylneſſe ſowle whiche hadde byfore euery man woundred theym ſelf made joye wyth newe maner gladdeneſſe eche man owne ſowle cryed ſayde good v be▪ make thre tabernacle dwellyng place none woūder douiles▪ hydde inuyſybly breſte ſpouſe whiche tranſfygured hylle ſaynt peter ſayde appoſtles ¶ ferthermore purpos choſen mayde full tender age ſoone began waxe cōforted wyth holy ghoſt token ſhe ſholde ſoone fulfylled wyth dyuyne wyſdome aboute age fyue yere whan ſhe taught ſaye ſalutacion aungell aue maria recordyd beſely ſayde full ofte whan ſhe coude ſaye ſhe enſpired frō heuen began grete oure lady goyng vpward ſtayere comynge doūward ſame ſtayere eche grees ſtayere worſhyppe lady wyth aue maria ſhe tolde confeſſour afterward ſecret •• eſſe confeſſion ye maye ſ • e ſhe fyrſt begynnynge ſhewed forth fyrſt pleſyng acceptable wordes men yonge age ſhe began ſtye vp thynges inuyſyble ¶ holy begynnyng encreſed euery daye▪ pleaſyd lord vyſe • ed wyth gracyous wounderfull vyſyon ſtere ſhewe hyr gyftes grace holy ghooſt ſhewe lytyll plante ſhold brought forthe ſoo nouryſſhed tree cidre moyſter holy goſt ¶ aboute age vj yere befyll choſen mayde wyth brother steuen ſomme elder ſhe wente ſuſter bonauentura whiche ſuſter made mencion byfore perauentur ſomeuer ende loke ſhe ferde maner frendes kynrede ſoo doo whan ſhe hadde doo bode doo goyng homward agayn waye whiche called tongue wallis piacta holy may lyfte vp eyen agaynſte ouer chirche freer prechours ſhe ſawe ayer full fayre chambre ryally aparayed wyth ryches honeſte oure lorde iheſu cryſte trone imperyall clothed wyth pontyfycall veſture hauyng hede myter papall wyth hym ſaynt peter ſaynt poule ſaynt johan euan gelyſt whan ſhe behelde alle thys ſhe fyrſt ſtonyd vyſement ſtably ſhe ſtode ſtyll wyth louyngyng herte deuoutly ſhe loked ſauyour bothe wyth bodely goſtely eyen anone lorde drewe loue hym mercy fully ſette e • en mageſte vpon graiouſly louyngly wyth manneuer ſmylyng chere reched ryght arme toward ouer her▪ gaue bleſſyng wyth token holy croſſe maner byſſhoppes prelate ¶ grace gyfte god ſpedfull ſoo effectuouſly putte anon ſhe tranſformed rauyſſhed ſpyryte vnto oure lord whome ſhe ſawe behylde wyth ſoo greate goſtely lykynge gooyng waye mynde fully ſhe hadde forgoten ſelfe ofte wente waye beſyde men beſtes nature dredfull ſholde chylde euer eyen hede vpward abydyng vppon blyſfull vyſyon none doughte ſoo ſhe wolde haue abyde ſhe hadde touched take awaye ſomme body longe vyſyon endured ¶ laſ • e whyles thys ſhewed mayde▪ steuen broder helde forthe waye paſſed greate ſpace wenyng ſhe folowed hym whan tourned hym ſawe folowe tourned agayn ſawe ſuſter fer • e hynde ſtondyng ſtyll waye loke vp fyrmament ¶ thenne cryed wyth alowde voys called ſhe anſwerde take none hede thenne wente nere cryeng afterher voys helped ¶ woundred wente thenne drewe honde ſayde dooſt thou comeſt thou forthr ſhe anon caſt doune lytyll eyen ſhe hadde awaked heuy ſlepe ſayde yf thou ſawe ſawe thou woldeſt haue lette holy vyſyon anone ſhe ſaid •• ▪o wordes lyft vp eyen agayne holde vp ſhe hadde ſeen vyſyon alle wythdrawe ceſyd wyll whiche aperyd fore myght ſhe bere wythout ſharpe ſtroke ſorowe anone ſhe vengyd ſelf wyth ſore wepynge ſorowe ſhe caſte doune eyen tyme houre yonge mayde vyrgyn ſaint katheryn began waxe olde vertues ſadneſſe maners haue wounderfull witte felyng body bot • e grace nature ſoo moche dedes • chyldyſſhe ne yonge woman ſemed rather alle men came wyſedom greate worſhypfull age soo anone ſhewed fyre dyuyne loue kyndeled herte whiche vertu intellection made clere wyll feruent memorye comforted alle outward werkyng ſhewed alle thynges rewle goddes lawe ¶ ſhe ſayd confeſſyon hyrconfeſſour full mekely lowely ſhe lerned knewe tyme wyth techyng ony body ony redynge heryng onely • nfuſyon holy ghooſe leuyng maners foly faders egypte lyuyng many sayntes ſpecyally lyfe saynt domynyk▪ ¶ hadde ſoo grete deſyre folowe lyuyng holy fadres sayntes ſhe myghte noo thynge ellys thynke howe ſhe myght come therto ¶ cauſe many newe thynges beganne holy mayde hyr holy lyuyng dedes broughte men wonder tyme ſhe ſought oute ſhe myght haue pryue place abyde preuely whanne ſhe wolde vſe bodely afflyccyons whanne ſhe wolde occupye hyr prayer holy medytacyons▪ ¶ place certeyne tymes ſhe ſcourged hyr lytell tender body wyth lytell ſcourge lefte maner pleye • dyſportes beſely gafe hyr prayer medytacyons full ſtylle ſhe gaf alle ſcylence euery day ageynſte condy cyon chyldren laſſe bodely mete ſhe toke thenne ſhe wonte fore wonte falle chyldren wexynge exemplum exſaumple thys yonge mayde many damſe •• y dwellyng nye hyr age ſteryd god grace gadred hyr holy gracyous wordys power folowe hyr holy werkys thorugh fyll alle tho chyldren att certeyne tymes • amen gyder preuy place hir hows ſhe dwellyd ſhe hadde choſen fore hyr ſelf alle ſcour gyd hem ſelfe ſhe dyde eche ſayde certeyne pater noſter aue maria katheryne bad h • ſaye ¶ alle theſe werkyngee tokenys gretter meruaylles ſholde folowe ¶ hyr moder tolde full ofte mayſter reymond ¶ ſhe whan aſked hyr myghte denye hyt full ofte goyng vpward dounward grees hyr faders hows vyſybly alle ſyghte ſawe hyr swyf •• ly ſhe wente ayre touched noo grees wyth fete thys fylle namely whanne ſhe wolde flee waye another place ¶ forthermore moche ſhe knowynge lyfe holy faders egypte reuelacyon therfore wyth alle ſtrengthes ſhe ſteryd gretely folow hem ¶ ſo moche ye yong tender age full feruentely ſhe deſyred wylderneſſe holy faders olde tyme ſhe myghte thynke hyr maner waye ſhe myght perfourme hyr deſyre cauſe ordeyned god ſhe ſholde dwell ſoo ſolytary place oure lorde ſuffred hyr ſtonde wytte hir proper nature ſhe myght nomore knowe ſhe ſholde doo touchyng purpoſe hyr owne chyldes wytte wolde ſhewe hyr ryght ſo befyll ſhe wyth hyr feruent wyll purpoſe ſhe ouercame tendreneſſe frealte hyr age yet hadde ſhe parfyte vyctorye erly morowty de ſhe thought go deſerte ellys wylderneſſe abyde ſolytary place wherefor chyldys prouydence ſhe purueyed lofe brede forthe ſhe wente toward hyr ſuſters hows wedded whyche hows faſte gate clepyd gate ſaynt anſanye paſſyd hyr ſuſtrer hows forthe ſhe wente gate ſo dyd ſhe neuer afore ſoo paſſyd forthe tyll ſhe came waye cyte ſhe ſaw noo hows ſtonde nyghe ſhe dyde cyte thenne ſhe thought wel ſhe nyghe deſerte yet wente ſhe ſomwhat forther laſte ſhe founde lytel caue vnder banke whyche pleſyd hyr well▪ forth ſhe wente glad herte wenyng hyr ſhe hadde fonde wylderneſſe whyche ſhe hadde deſyred ſhe yet lorde almyghty god whome ſhe behelde long fore receyned hys holy blyſſyng whyche gladly acceptyth holy deſyres alle lord hadde dyſpoſed hys ſpouſe haue manere lyuyng yet wolde ſuffre dede ſhe dyde good deſyre paſſe awaye wyth token ſheweher ſhe dyd acceptable pleſyng hym anone ſhe began praye feruently ſhe lyfte vp lytell lytell erthe body wente vp hyghe height caue wolde ſuffre ſo ſhe ſtode prayer fro morow none thys mayde perceyued welle ſhe areryd erthe tyme ſhe wende ben wor • hyng hyr enemye whyche wold wyth hys fraudes dyſceytes lette hyr prayer deſyre ſhe deſerte cauſe ſhe beſyed hir enforced hyr ſtablye feruently praye laſte aboute houre day whan lord paſſy croſſe take doun fro croſſe ſhe deſcendyd lytell lytell ſhe aſcendyd inſpyracion lord ſhe hadde vnderſtondyng knowyng tyme yet come ſhe ſholde putte hyr body ſuche afflyccyon lorde ne ſhe ſholde leue faders hows ſuche maner wherefor ſhe torned ſhe came whan ſhe wente ſawe ſhe allone behelde gate cytee longe full fe • age feblyneſſe dredynge alſo hyr fader moder ſhold wene ſhe loſte coude beganne praye commytted hyr fully god anone ſhorte whyle ordynaunce myght lorde ſhe borne vp eyre ſette gate cytee wyth ony harme anone ſhe wente home alle haſt ſhe myght coude thys ſhe tolde coſyne here whyche callyd laxa hyr fader moder alle thys hydde vnknowen tyll ſhe came elder age wende ſhe hadde come fro hyr ſuſters hows wedded thys ſhewed thys chapytre ſomme partye lapa hir moder tolde mayſter reymond whyche hyr laſt confeſſoure ſomme partye ſelf ſomme laxa hyr coſyne wythſtondyng hadde grete ſweteneſſe alle wrytton ſayd fore saue laſte bothe hyr fyrſt confeſſour whyche nouryſſhed hyr faders hows many worſhypfull trewe matro • neyghbours nyghe beſyde nygh hyr fader moder hyr ¶ hyr vowe made virgynyte vertuous liuynge meruaylles whyche fyll tyll ſhe came age abylytee wedded man wedded ſhe ne neuer wolde capitulū iij moche vertue grace vyſyon whyche reherſyd nexte • hapytle fore worldly loue affeccyon wyth drawen herte thys holy yonge mayde onely holy loue goddys ſone gloryous mayde moder lord iheſu cryſte ſtylly ſtedfaſtly prented hyr herte▪ wherfore ſhe ſette alle thynge noughte ſoo ſhe myght ouely wynne lord hyr ſauyour anone ſhe clere vnderſtondyng techyng holy ghooſt full ſemyng accordyng lorde maker nought ſerued wyth alle purytee • lenues bothe body ſowle wherfore ſhe deſyred fully haue kepe clenneſſe virgynytee ſhe thought well knowynge hyr techynge god bleſſyd lady goddys moder fyrſte founde lyf virgynytee wherefor thys mayde conceyued hyr herte vp mater ſhe wolde haue recourſe lady helpe counſeyll whan ſhe came ſeuen yere age ſhe took grete auyſemente though ſhe hadde ſadneſſe xx yere age contynuelly ſhe prayed lady quene aungels virgynes ſhe wolde woucheſauf helpe hyr gete hyr lord parfyte waye techynge holy ghooſt ſhe myght doo mooſt pleſynge god moſte ſpedefulle helthe hyr ſowle eche prayer euer ſhe ſhewed hyr deſyre lady ſore ſhe deſyred lyue aungelslyf lyf virgynytee alle thys tyme loue euerlaſtyng ſpouſe feruent fro day day thys maydens herte whyche loue ſteryd alle hyr ſowle wyth oute ony ceſſyng vnto heuenly liuynge whan thys wyſe mayde ſawe feruent ſpyryte deſyre cauſe ſhe wolde quenche ſpiryte whiche freely gracyouſly hadde graunted ſhe aſked hote kyndelyng deſyre vpon day thanne ſhe choſe hyr preuy place noo body myght hyr ſhe myght ſpeke alle lowde wyth hygh voys euer ſhe wolde ſaye wyth lowneſſe body ſowle thus ſpak ſhe lady ſayde mooſt blyſſedfull lady mooſt holy vitgyne whyche fyrſte amonge alle wymmen thou halowedeſt euer thy virgynytee lord wyth makyng hym vowe whome thou made moder hys onely ſone thy pyte whyche may ſpoke ne tolde tongue lowely beſeche praye none merytes notwythſtondyng myn vnworthyneſſe woucheſ auf gracyous lady ſo moche grace thou ſpouſe hym onely whome deſyred wyth ſtrengthes ſowle thyn holy ſone lord iheſu cryſte make hym fulle promyſſe ſhall neuer take ſpouſe ſhall kepe hym virgynyte vndefowled myghte poure loo maydens rede thys loo vere ye may ſe ordynatly alle yeftes vertuous werkyng dedys thys holy mayde dyſpoſed ordeyned euerlaſtyng wyſdome whyche myghtely dyſpoſeth alle thynges ſoftnes age ſyy yere ſhe ſawe hir ſpouſe wyth hyr bodely eye took hym hys blyſſynge age ſeuen yere ſhe made vowe virgynyte taketh hede alſo auyſement ordre ſhe kepte makyng hyr auowe ¶ fyrſte ſhe deſyred aſkyd haue hym hyr ſpouſe whome hyr ſowle louyd deſyre aſkyng ſhe forſoke euery maner ſpouſe behotyng hym trouth feyth euer laſtynge thys petycyon myght denyed taketh hede alſo whome ſhe prayeth ſhe prayed ſhe prayeth fyrſte ſhe prayeth lady whyche hath properly inacte lyberalytee fredome alle grace euer graunte yeue grace man neuer ſo fowle ſynne ſhe holdeth hyr ſelfe dettour alle bothe wyſe vnwyſe deſpyſeth none ſhe opened hande eche man hath nede ſtretched hyr pawmes eche poure man ſheweth hyr ſelf folke well neuer faylled ſholde gracyous lady lytell mayde ſo innocent feruent whyche puttyth awaye hyr grace ſynfull men woman elder age ſholde gloryous lady receyue purpoſe virgynyte holy mayde whyche gracyouſly fyrſte amonge men founde holy clene lif virgynytee ſholde mercyfull pyteuous lady denye thys lytell mayde hyr ſone whyche drewe hym heuen erthe ſholde gyue alle belyued hym ye haue ſeen thys mayde prayed sithe praye thou ſhe prayed aſkyd ſame whiche ſelf taughte aſke whyche aſked ſought ſame whyche byddeth alle men ſeke ſhall ſought hym ſelf ſhalle ſought may put awaye ne put petycyon ſuche thynge muſt nedys haue graū te lordes promyſe ſayde aſkyth ye ſhall haue speketh ye ſhall fynde ſayde alſo another place fyrſte ſekyth kyngdome god hys ryghtwyſneſſe therefore whanne thys mayde ſo beſely ſought ſoo tymely ſo tender chyldys age ſone god whyche hym ſelfe kyngdome god manere myght ſhe ſholde fynde ſhe ſoughte haue ſhe aſkyd ferthermore ſeeth manere ſhe prayed aſked ſhe deſyred ye ſhalle clerely ſee hyr prayer myghte doon awaye ne voydyd dyſpoſed hyr ſelfe receyue ſhe aſkyd onely tyme alle tyme come remeuyd alle hyr obſtacles ſhe clothed hyr wyth pleſable clothynge pouerte hym euer whome ſhe aſkyd hyr deſyre bonde hyrſelf oblyſſhed hyr wyth ſolempne vowe fore god ſoo ſtraytely reſtrayned hyr ſelfe neuer world ne fende ſholde lette hyr dyſpoſycyon alle thys tyme ther faylled hyr condycyons whyche prayer ſholde haue prayer muſte nede herde ſhe aſked hyr ſelf ſhe aſked fulle mekely helthefull alle helthe feythfully ſhe ſtood ſtedfaſtely repreſente hyr perſeueraū ce made perpetuell vowe ſhe remeuyd alle ſhold obſtacle hyr petycyon may ye ſekerly conclude nedys ſhe moſte herde lord thynketh thenne ſekerly ſhe aſked ſoo ſhe reſceyued lorde took hyr lorde hyr loue hyr euerlaſtyng ſpouſe hys blyſfulle moder ſhe deſyred bi helpe gloryous lady ſhe coupled euer hyr dere ſone perpetuell vowe virgynyte ſhall proued wyth helpe lord clere token laſt chapytre fyrſt partye ferthyrmore ye ſhall knowe thys vowe thys mayde began euery day wexe holy holy tender age ſhe began take batayll wyth hyr fleſſhe whyche yet began neuer rebell ſhe purpoſed take waye hyr fleſſhe fleſſhly mete moche ſhe myghte wherfore whanne fleſſhe leyde hyr fylle ofte eyther ſhe leyde stephen hyr brothyr preuely lytyll lytyll ſhe voyded body ſholde perceyue contynued alwaye hyr dyſplyens whyche ſpake fore encreſed hem ſharpely eyther allone hyr ſelf wyth yonge maydens alſo grete wele othyr ſowles helthe began kyndelyd hyr wonderfull ſuche chyldes herte ſyngulerly ſhe loued tho ſayntes whiche laboured ſpecyally boute helthe mannes ſowle hadde alſo knowyng onely techynge god saynt domynyk ordeyned ordre frere prechours loue feythe holy chyrche helthe mannes ſowle wherfore ſhe ordre ſo moche reuerence whan ſhe ſawe frerys ordre paſſyng forth waye hir faders ſe ſhe marked wel wente paſſyd fulle mekely deuoutely ſhe kyſſed ſteppes theyr fete tyme forward wext grete deſyre hyr ſowle go vnto ordre ſhe myght profyte man ne ſowle wyth brethern ordre cauſe ſhe ſawe grete obſtacle ſhe woman therfore ſhe thought folowe saynt eufroſyen mē clepyd hir childhode wōderfully pronoſtycacion ryght ſaynt eufroſyen feyned hyr man went monaſtery monkes ſame manere thys mayde purpoſed ſeyne hyr man go ferre contree ſhe knowe take abyte ordre frere prechours ſhe myght helpe ſowles ſaue peryſſhyng yet wytfſtondyng ſame thought purpoſe abode longe hyr mynde lord ſuffred thought perfourmed dedene brought execucyon ye loue put hyr mynde another ende lord wolde alſo another maner fulfyll hyr deſyre thys tyme thys mayde wexte faſt body encreced age moche hyr ſowle encreced vertue mekenes wext faſt deuocyon encreced feyth clere hope gretely ſtrengthed charyte multyplyed hyr feruour thys vertues gendryd vertuous worſhypfull ſadnes maneres relygyous putte ſyght al men whyche conſydered hyr dedys fader moder aſtonyed brethern ſuſteren wondred gretely alle meyne hyr faders hows meruaylled beholdyng perceyuynge ſoo hygh wyſdome ſoo tendyr age amonge many notable wyſe wordes dedys one wylle ſhewe cōmendacyon mayde ¶ hyt befylle tyme ſeuen yere fore ten yere age deuocyon hyr moder hadde ſaynt anthonye wolde haue maſſe ſayde worſhyppe ſame saynt wherefor ſhe clepyd katheryne hir doughter took hyr certeyne candelles certeyne ſyluer ſayde goo doughter paryſſhe chyrche praye oure paryſſhe preeſt ſyng ſynge maſſe worſhyp ſaynte anthonye offer thyſe candelles thys money vp awtre ¶ thys mayde gladde doo alle thynge myght torne worſhyp god anone ſhe wente chyrche performed hyr moders byddyng deuocyon ſhe hadde maſſe ſhe abode ſtylle ende maſſe whan alle ſhe wente home ageyn hyr moder wende ſhe wolde comen anone ageyn anone ſhe made oblacyon preeſt ¶ moche doughter taryed ſo longe hir ſemyng whan ſhe ſawe ſhe come ſhe thought blame hyr doughter ſayd curſyd wycked tōgues ſayd thou ſholdeſte nomore come ageyne thys manere ſomme men ſaye langage name taryed longe thys mayde thenne grete wyſdome herde hyr moder ſayde helde hyr ſtylle whyle ſpake noo worde ageyne good ſpace thys mayde drewe hir modre fyde wyth grete ſadnes hyr mekely ſpak hir modre ſeyde ¶ lady modre euer treſpas agaſt youre biddyng bete ye wyth rodde thynketh beſt ware another time worthy ryght full ye ſo thyng praye defautes curſeth neuer good man ne badde ſemyng degree full grete affliccion̄ herte hyr modre herde theſe wordys ſche wondrid gretely merueill lytill doughter teche ſo wyſely enforme hir ſomoche ſhe hadde ſpirite blame hyr tyme wyſdom ſhe ſawe ſo yonge alitill thynge neuer le ſhe wolde hyr doughter hadde knowe therfor ſūwhat ſhe thoughte ſpeke ageyne turned hir doughter ſeyde ſo longe doughter ſeyde mekely ageyne modre herde maſſe yebadde goo whan doone turned home ageyn wythout ony tarieng abode nowhere till come home ageyne thoo modre tho wordis edyfyed ſhe fore went hyr huſbonde ſeyd thus thus hath thi yonge doughter ſpoke good man gafthankynges god bare ſtylle priuely hys herte ſeyde noughte ageyne loo ye mayden̄s rede thys book thys oo poynt yt one leſte yet mowe ye wele perceyue lorde encreceth hys grace weye thys yonge mayde till ſhe come ye yeres abilitee weddyd whyche yeres ye ſhalle ſee next chapytre thys chapitre make ende ¶ yet ye ſhall vnderſtonde thyſe conteyned thys chapytre ſame mayde partye ſomme hadde modre dwellyng hyr fadres hows whyſe ſhe age ¶ hyr feruente deuocyon drawe whyche lord ſuffred encrece grace folowyng hyr ſtronge pacyence wyth whyche pacyens ſhe ſuffred hir fadres hows many iniuryes capitulūq̄rtū wonderfull vertuous cours lyuyng fyrſt yeres thys maydens tender age lordes wyll ſomme lyghte defaute ſuffre hyr fall ſuffred fulle ofte ſomme hys holy ſayntes entent ſholde myghtely aryſe vp ageyne lyue warly ſtrenght hem atteyne ryght waye heythe perfeccyon gloryouſly haue vyctorye fende whyche euer enemye mannes ſowle ¶ theſe wordes ſaye whanne ſhe came age yeres abylyte wedded ſaye twelthe yere hyr age lytel thenne manere contree ſhe abode ſtyll home came hyr fadres hows fader moder thenne hyr frendes kynne cauſe knewe may den purpoſe bethought hem beſyed hem ſeke aboute thys mayden myght worſhypfully parfy tably wedded proſone hyr moder ſuppoſed grete wyſdome hyr doughter ſhe ſholde haue wedded ſomme man grete kyneede ſhe beſyed hir faſt aboute bodely apparayll araye hyr doughter taught hyr waſſhe ofte hyr face kembe ofte hyr hede make hyr fayre voyde alle thynge ſholde dyſhoneſte ſholde make foule hyr face hyr necke whan ony man came aſke hyr maryage ſhe ſholde ſemely fayrer thys holy mayde alle another purpoſe made another vowe alle ſhe ſhewed hyr fader ne moder wherfor vtterly ſhe thoughte noo thynge hyr moder bad hyr touchyng ſuche curyoſyte beſyed wyth alle hyr ſtrengthes pleſe god man wyſe whanne hyr moder hadde aſpyed ſhe wylle maner lyuynge ſhe dyſpleſed clepyd hyr bonauenture hyr doughter whyche late wedded bad hyr trete ſoo hir ſuſter ſhe myght araye hyr bodely apparayll manere wymen contre ſholde maryed doo ſhe hadde bad hyr doo fore hyr moder knewe welle katheryne loued bonauenture fulle tenderly ſuppoſed ſhe ſholde broughte lyghtely hyr ſuggeſtyons thanne ony ſoo ſhe ye ſhalle ſee ſuffraunce oure lorde ſhe broughte ſo inne thorough ſpeche example hyr ſuſter bonauenture many maner wayes laſte ſhe aſſentyd hyr beſyneſſe apparaylle hyr body wylle hyr moder wythſtondynge ſtably ſhe kepte hyr purpoſe neuer haue huſbonde graū te hyr ſuſtre folowed hyr wylle ſuche araye ſhe maad ſoo moche ſorowe whanne ſhe confeſſyd therof wyth terys ſobbyng eche body ſhold ſuppoſe ſhe hadde ſomme greuous ſynne vſed ofte confeſſyd generally alway whā ſhe came ye poynt ſhe accuſed ſelfe full harde wyth wepyng ſore ſobbyng confeſſour alle knewe vertue god lowely ſowles ſee ſelf defaute none lytyll ſemeth hym full grete neuertheleſſe aſmoche ſhe accuſed ſelf demed worthy euerlaſtynge payne ſynne ſauyng mercy god aſked whether ſhe purpoſed wylled tyme agaynſt vowe ſayde nay came neuer herte alſo aſked agayne whether ſhe dyde pleſaunce ony man ſpeciall pleſaunce men anſwerd ſayde ther none ſomoche payne holde men ſeyne men men ſhold fynde wherfore faders men yt lerned dyer crafte faders hous came ony place chambre ſhe ſhe fledde faſte awaye adder hadde come ſoo men wondred wold neuer goo wyndowe ne dore hows ſee men wente waye then̄e ſayd deſerued ye dede whiche bodely ornamente euerlaſtyng payne namely whan apparelle exceſſyuely anſwerd ſayde exceſſyuely ſhe loued ſuſter thought thā god tyme wherfore ſhe wepte wythout remedye dyd harde penaū ce confeſſour wold haue replyed agayne ſayde alle bee ther ſomme maner exceſſe loue lytyll dede ſelf doo noo wycked euyl entencion vayne pleſaunce tyme agaynſte precepte god herde confeſſour replyed ſhe lyft vp eyen god wyth lowde voys cryed ſayde lorde god ghoſtely fader haue nowe whiche excuſeth ſynnes wyth ſore grutchynge agaynſt ſelf ſhe tourned confeſſour ſayde fader thynke ye wretchedfull mooſte vnworthy creature god whiche hath receyued maker nought ſoo many gracyous yeftes wythout labour wythouten ony meryte ſhold occupye ony tyme arraye vayne apparelle roten fleſſhe whiche myght induce dedely ſynne wene ſhe ſayde helle ſuffyſeth punyſſhe hadde pyte god doo gracyouſly mercyfull wyth thyſe wordes confeſſour durſt nomore ſpeke mater beſyed knowe yf bleſſyd ſowle euer lyf kept wythouten ony ſpot • e dedely ſynne soo ſhe hadde kepte fully hole vyrgynyte body ſowle ſynne fleſſhely ſteryng alſo alle maner ſynne ¶ knewe vertuous clene ſowle ſhe hadde wytneſſe recorde bare conuerſacion ſayd wrote coude neuer perceyue ne fynde nother generall confeſſyon ne ſpeciall confeſſyon ofte euer ſhe confeſſyd▪ ryght ofte ſhe hadde offendyd agaynſt precepte lorde yf tolde afore whiche myght ſuppoſe agaynſte byddynge god ne trowed none dyſcrete man wold ſuppoſe alſo ſayde founde euer ſoo clene fro venyall ſynnes vnnethe coude perceyue bi cotydyan confeſſyon ony maner offē ce openly knowen confeſſours knewe conſcyence conuerſaunt▪ neuer ſeldon ſhe offended worde eyther ſhe occupyed tyme prayer contemplacion elli good edyficacion neyghbours tyme ſlepyng vnnethes ſhe wolde grauute quarter houre whan ſhe ſholde ete mete▪ yet may called mete euer ſhe prayed thought holy medytacyons thynkyng thynges ſhe hadde lerned lord ſowle confeſſyon mayſter reymound bereth trewe recorde tyme yt knewe hadde cure conſcience payne ete mete hungry man wythdrawe hys mete grete tourmente body tyme ſhe hadde ete com̄ely fenerous man rennyng offhis feuer one cauſes ſhe wolde ete mete ſhall declared wythin forthe tourmente put payne body maner treſpaas myght ſuche ſowle occupyed alwaye occupyed ſoo wyth lord god yet wythſtondyng ſuche good occupacions accuſed ſelf ſoo ſharpely confeſſion ſoo wyttyngly put ſelfe treſpaas offenſes yf hee cōfeſſour hadde knowe conuerſacyon myght haue ſuppoſed ſhe hadde treſpaſed ſhe treſpaſed rather deſeruyd mede loo ye maydens heren reden boke alle proceſſe thynge ellys ſayde ye perceyuen lytyll defaute whyche holy mayde yelde ſelf ſoo mekely gylty ye maye vnderſtonde therby per feccyon ſheweth therafter gracyous yefte lorde whiche confeſſour reherſeth wyſe bonauentura ryght ſhe beſy afore araye holy mayde worlde aſketh ryght ſoo eftſones ſhe beſyed enduce ſuche araye counſeyll ſame apparaylle myght noo wyſe inclyne may den herte nother generall nother ſpecy ſhe ſholde ſhewe bodely preſence wylfully ſyghte man entent oonly ſhe ſholde deſyred ſoner wedded though feruour prayer ſweteneſſe medytaciō ſlaked wythdrewē tyme att laſte oure lorde wolde lenger ſuffre hys ſpouſe whiche ſoo ſpecyally choſen ſholde withdrawe taryed hys ſpeciall ſeruyce wythdrewe wyſe tyme whan ſame bonauentura ſuſter holy mayde ſholde brynge forthe chylde ſhe yet yonge nough age bere chyldren take hede maydens therfore ſee thys oure lorde diſpleſed wyth theym ben aboute lette wythdrawe theym wolde ſerue hym ſpecially maydenhode chaſtyte lyuynge thys bonauentura reherſyd alwaye full honeſte maner lyuyng bothe worde dede cauſe ſhe beſyed drawe ſuſter wordly thynges whiche deſyred ſerue lorde ſpecyally ſmyten hym punyſſhed wyth full ſharpe deth neuertheleſſe lord yet wrought full mercyably wyth hyr ſhewed afterward reuelacyon thys holy mayde ſhe purgatory ſuffred many greuous paynes prayer hir ſhe delyuered payne reſtored blyſſe ſhe ſhewed afterward preuely hyr confeſſour ¶ whanne hyr ſuſter bonauenture paſſyd thys worlde thanne thys bleſſyd mayde katheryn clerely perceyued vanyte thys worlde ganne feruentely gredylye trewely torned louely ghoſtly clyppyng hyr endeles ſpouſe jheſu cryſte claymyng accuſynge hyr ſelf gylty wyth marye magdalene fallyng doune full ſtreyte fete oure lorde plenteuouſly ſhedyng terys axynge inwardly hys mercy praynge thynkyng vnceſſably hyr ſynnes ſhe myght deſerue hyr wyth marye magdalene wordes confort lorde ſayde marye thus ¶ remittūtur tibi peccata tua ¶ ſaye doughter thy ſynnes foryeue ſo ſhe beganne haue ſynguler affeccyon mary magdalene thanne tyme ſhe enforſed hyrſelf wyth alle hyr myghtys conferme hyr marye magdalene haue grace forgyuenes hyr ſynnes therfore afterward encrece deuocyon thys folow therof lord god ſpouſe holy ſowles hys bleſſyd moder lady saynt marye gaue mary magdalene thys blyſſyd mayde mayſtreſſe moder ſhall declared openly wyth inne forth helpe jheſu ¶ thys fende enemye alle mankynde ſorowyng thus pray wythdrawe delyuerd alle hole hys power whyche lytell lytell enforced drawe hym alſo conſyderynge thys holy mayde encreced renne quyckely tabernacle mercy hyr ſpouſe jheſu thought felly wylely lette hyr hyr ghoſtly purpoſe meyne hyr faders howſholde beſyeng hym aduercytees perſecucyons drawe hyr holy worlde ſhe ſholde occupyed ſuche ghoſtly excercyſe puttyng mynde hir fader moder alſo hyr brethern alle wyſe ſhe ſholde wedded myght ſo hyr mene purchace ſomme manere kynrede aboute thys beſyneſſe fende enduced hem ſo hyely aſmoche one hyr doughters paſſyd thys world ſholde aboute recouer harme hyr dede hyr lyue ferforth aboute ſeke huſbonde thys holy mayde ¶ whan thys mayde perceyued conſydered wyles hyr ghoſtly enemye inſpyracyon lord jheſu none myghtely beſyly ſhe contynued prayer medytacyon excercyſes penaunce haue grace flee conuerſacyon men ſoo ſhewed open tokenys hyr frendes noo wyſe ſhe purpoſe wedded dedely ne corruptyble ſpouſe syth ſo ſhe taken ſo gracyouſly hyr ſpouſe hir yonge tender age vndedely kyng endeles blyſſe whanne fader moder kynne perceyued veryly thys holy may de ſhewed perſeueraūtly bothe token worde ſhe wylled neuer wedded none erthely man thought bowe hyr herte nother mene conſente theyr purpoſe callyd frende therys frere prechour whyche loued ſpecyally prayed hym entyrly wolde goo counſeyll holy mayde ſhe ſholde conſente wylle whome frere anſwerde ſayde wolde myght whan came thys mayde communycacyon founde hyr ſo ſtedfaſt purpoſe maydenhode conſcience ſo enduced gyue hyr holſum counſeylle ſayde syth ſo thou arte dyſpoſed ſerue lorde god maydenhede ageynſt whyche purpoſe thy frendes ben aboute lette shewe ſtedfaſtneſſe thyn holy purpoſe cutte waye alle thyn thy hede peraduenture wold ceſſe purſuyte ſoone thys bleſſyd mayde herdethys hys counſeyll ſhe wrought though ſhe hadde herde god took peyre ſherys anone cutte awaye hir herys whiche ſhe ſuppoſed ſhe ſynned greuouſly ſhe hated ſo moche ſhe cutte awaye ryght gladly faſt de whanne ſhe ſhe couerd hyr hede wyth coyf ſo wente forthe alle ageynſt comyn cuſtome maydens worlde wyth kerchyf hyr hede ye doctryne ſaynt powle whan hyr moder lapa aſpyed thys hyr doughter katheryn vſed thus couer hyr hede cuſtomably aſked hyr ſhe dyd ſo thys mayden gaf none clere anſwer cauſe ſhe wolde nethyr lye ne telle trouthe wyth moder wente thys maydens hede took hyr kerchyfe wyth hyr owne hondys ſo ꝑceyued yt hyr cut awaey thāne moder ſorowfull hyr herte bycauſe hyr fayre cutte awaye waylynge cryenge thys wyſe aa doughter haſte thou doo anone mayde keuered hyr hede efte ſones wente ſyde crye moder came bothe fader chyldren meruayllyng myght whanne knewe cau •• hyr cryeng hugely ameuyd ageynſte maide whiche trouble begonne ſecounde bataylle ageynſt mayde ſharper thēne waſ fyrſt yet thys mayden lord gaff vyctorye thoo thynges whyche ſemed lettyng hyr holy purpoſe hyr grete helpe meruayllouſly knytte hyr lord myghtely therefore purſued hyr openly rebukyng hyr thretyng hyr worde dede ſayeng thus thou wretched creature troweſt thou eſcape thus thou ſhalt fulfyll wylle becauſe thou haſt cutte awaye thyn hyt ſhall growe ageyn wyll thou nyll thou though thyn herte ſholde breſte yet ſhalt yu haue huſbonde thou ſhalt neuer haue reſte vnto tyme thou haſte conſented wylle wyth made ordynaunce katheryne ſhold nomore haue pryue chambre hir ſelf dwelle inne ſholde openly occupyed comyn ſeruyce hows place tyme prayeng vnyeng knyttyng jheſu hir ſpoufe ſholde vtterly wyth drawe hir alſo ſhe ſhold ſee hyr ſelf ſo moche deſpyte ſhe made comyn ſeruaunte thys ordynaunce thys holy mayde putte alle manere fylthe beſyneſſe fowle kechyn suffryng euery day repreues euery day alſo wronges rebukyng dyſpytable wordes multeplyed ageynſt hyr moſte alle ouercomen wymmenys hertys hyt ſuppoſed hyr fader hyr moder brethern hadden fonde yong man who kynrede gretely well apayde therefor ſteryd inpugnyd hyr ſharpely ſhe myght ſonner bowed theyr conſent oure ghoſtly enemye fende who wyckednes tretcherous werkes thyſe thynges wrought doune wende wyth drawe thys mayde hyr clene purpoſe helpe god ſhe made mooſt ſtrengeſt ſhe noo wyſe meuyd ne ſtered alle doone hyr ſhe made hyr pryue chaumbre helpe holy ghooſt hyr owne ſowle fro whyche pryue chaumbre ſhe made ordynaunce hyr ſelf neuer go manere beſyneſſe ſo done dede ſhe whyche fyrſte hadde outward chaumbre aſſygned hyr ſomtyme ſtood wyth ſomtyme wente oute afterwarde whan ſhe made hyr ſelue hyr ſowle pryue chaumbre myght take hyr creature erthe ſhe went neuer thes ben tho heuenly vyctoryes may taken awaye fro cryſtis ſpecyall erthe ouercomynge wyth ony doubte alle ſtylly enemyes holy wrytte ſeyth regnum dei infra no eſt ſaye kyngdome heuen wythin v alſo prophete dauyd ſeyth ioye lordes doughter wythin forthe wythin v wyth ony doubte clere vnderſtondyng fr • wylle retentyf mynde wythin v alſo gracyous infuſyon holy ghooſt whiche maketh perfyte theſe ghooſtly myghtys reherſed afore ouercometh throweth vnder foot alle outward aduerſytres wythin v yf ben trewe vylners vertue dwelleth gheſt whyche ſayde ſeyth confidite ego vici mundum truſteth feythfully ye ſhall ouercome enemyes haue ouercome worlde grete enemye bleſſyd lord thys holy mayde katheryn truſtyd ſo hyghely ſhe made hir wyth inne hyr ſelf chambre hys helpe who loue ſhe charged leſe chambre made mannes handes wythout forth ¶ one thynge ſhall ſaye mayſter reymond confeſ ſour thys holy mayde beryth recorde whan ſholde walke outward cauſe whyle grete outward beſyneſſe occupacyon nedys muſt done thys holy mayde oftymes warned hym ſayde ſhold make wythin hys ſowle pryuee celle whyche pryue cell ſholde neuer goo alle vnderſtonde hyr ſo ouerly ſo lyghtely yet neuertheleſſe afterwarde whan conſydered wyttely hyr wordes wordes saynt johan ſayde goſpell felle hys mynde reherſed cryſtys dyſcyples thys wyſe hoe autem non cognouerunt diſcipuli eius primum sed quando glorificatus eſt iheſus tune recordatiſunt cryſtys dyſcyples knewe alle thynge hym touchyng hys paſſyon fyrſt onely tyme whan reyſen fro deth lyue gloryfyed thanne knewe openly clerely ſoo ſame manere wyſe bothe mayſter reymond hyr confeſ ſour tho conuerſaunt wyth hyr happyd meruayllouſly perceyued openly clerely bothe dedys hyr wordes afterwarde whenne wyth hyr preſently ¶ yette ſhall telle another holy conſeyt bleſſyd ymagynacyon thys holy mayde holy ghooſt taught hyr whyche ſhe ouercome alle wronges deſpytes ſhe tolde pryuely hyr confeſſour axyng hym mekely ſhe myght perfytly gladde amonge ſoo many deſpytes thanne ſhe brake ſayde ſhe hadde ſuche ymagynacyon hyr ſelf hyr fader repreſented lorde iheſu cryſte oure ſauyour hyr moder oure bleſſyd lady saynt marye hyr brethern many houſholde betokeneth holy appoſtles oure lorde dyſcyples hys thys bleſſyd ymagynacyon ſhe ſerued hem alle gladdely ſoo alle meruaylled therof thys bleſſyd ymagynacyon ſhe wan another grete profyte oftr ſhe ſerued made mynyſtracy euer ſhe hadde mynde hyr hyr ſpouſe iheſu cryſte whome hyr thought ſhe ſerued ſoo ſhe beyng bodely kechyn alle waye wyth holy place callyd sanctum ſancto rum ofte ſhe ſerued atte mete ſoo ofte ſhe fedde hyr ſowle wyth preſence oure ſauyour hyghe rycheſſe endeles counſeyll many dyuers meruayllous wayes delyuereſt truſten alle maner dyſeſes bryngeſt hauen endeles reſte delyueryng bothe pytte ſwolowe whan alle thys done thys holy mayde conſyderynge euyr hyr ſowle ye mede rewarde ordeyned hyr holy ghooſt ſuffred gladly nought paynfully alle wronges putte hyr alſo ſhe encreced contynually cours hyr labour ſhe myght haue full ioye hyr ſowle cauſe ſuffred hyr haue chambre hyr ſelf haue hyr chambre openly hadde ¶ therefore holy • uyſement ſhe choſe chambre stephen hyr brother hadde nether wyf ne chyldren dayes tyme whanne abſente ſhe myght allone nyghtes tyme whan ſlepte ſhe prayed hyr deſyre ſoo nyght daye ſhe ſoughte ſee face hyr ſpouſe iheſu cryſte knockyng dore hys ghooſ • ly tabernacle wyth ceſſyng prayed lord vnceſſably wolde wouche ſauf keper hyr virgynytee ſayeng ſyngyng ſowle wyth saynt cecylye thys holy verſe dauyd prophete fiat cor meum domine et corpus meum immaculatum lorde iheſu praye myn herte body kepte clene vnderfowled ſoo ſcylence hope ſhe made ſtronge lord ryght meruayllouſly torment perſecucyon ſhe hadde wyth forth ſhe fulfylled wyth ghooſtly ioyes wythin forth ſoo ferforth hyr brethern perceyueng hir ſtedfaſtneſſe ſayden betwyne ſeluen thus ouer come hyr fader moſt innocente alle conſyderyng pryuely hyr dedes perceyued ſhe ladde euery daye holy ghooſt nought lyghtnes yonthe alle thyſe ben reherſed thys chapytre hyr confeſſour mayſter reymond reuelacyon lapa thys maydens moder lyxa brother wyf alſo hyr faders hows thynges folke myght knowe knewe tellyng thys holy mayde confeſſyon ¶ vyctorye whyche ſhe hadde deſeſed hyr culuer whiche hyr fader ſawe vyſyon • ynt domynyk ca v mene whyle thys holy mayde putte ſuche reproue ſhame happyd vp daye ſhe entred chambre hyr yonge brother stephen prayed deuoutly leuyng dore vnſhett forboden hyr hyr fader moder ſhe ſholde ſhette dore caſuelly thenne happened fader entred chambre ſekynge certeyne thynge hys ſones nede loked aboute ſawe hys doughter goddes doughter thanne hys prayng corner knelyng lytell whyte culuer reſtynge vp hyr hede whyche culuer fledde chambre wyndowe whan fader entred chābre thought anone fader axed doughter culuer myght fledde ſo chambre doughter anſwerd ſayde neuer ſhe ſawe culuer ne byrde chambre thenne hadde fader grete meruaylle kepte thyſe wordes pryuely hys herte fro tyme forwarde beganne gracyouſly encrece holy maydens ſowle holy deſyre whyche neuertheleſſe begonne reherced fore hyr chyldehode afterward renewyd tuycyon dyſeaſe kepyng hyr maydenhode virgynytee deſyre thynge ellys receyue habyte ordre frere prechours whyche ordre saynt domynyk bothe foundour fader ſhe prayed bothe daye nyght lord woucheſauf fulfyll hyr deſyre therto ſhe grete deuocyon saynt domynyk reherſed fore worthy fruytfull louer ſowles almyghty god therefor ſawe wyſely myghtely hys doughter yong knyght faught batayll wyth feruour deuocyon ſhe beſyed hyr pleſe hym wyth alle hyr deſyre wolde wyſe dyſceyue hyr ne defraude hyr hyr holy purpoſe ſekerneſſe comforted hyr wyth ſuche vyſyon ¶ holy mayde tyme vyſyon hir ſlepe ſhe ſawe many holy faders many dyuers foūdours ye ordre ye frere prechours amonges ſhe ſaw ſaynt dominyk ſhe knewe wel holdyng hys honde fayre whyte lylye whyche lylye ſemyng hir fyre ye buſſhe yt moyſes ſaw yet brennyd whan holy faders al general eche ſpeciall gaf hir coūſeyll hir mede yt ſhe ſhold cheſe oo relygion ordynaūce ye whiche relygion ſhe myght yelde due ſeruyce god torned hir ſelf hole ſaynt dominik ſo ſaw ſpyryt yt ye holy fader ſaynt dominyk came hir brought honde habyte ſuſtriſ whyche ſuſters ben called ſuſtres penaunce ſaynt domynyk ye whiche ſuſters ther ne yet lytell nōbre ye cyte senee whan thys holy fader ſaynt domynyk cam mayde cōforted hir ſuche wordes ſayde dought good cōfort drede manere peryll ryght yu haſt deſyred habyte ſhe thought ſhe receyued thankyd almyghty god worthy confeſſour saynt domynyke wyth lytyll gladneſſe wyth ioyefull teres ſoo perfyghtely hadde cō forted ſoo wyth wepyng ſhe awoke reſtoryd bodely wyttes ¶ whan ſhe awaked ſhe caught comforte bodely ſtrength vyſyon toke ſoo grete boldenes truſte ſhe hadde lorde ſame daye ſhe called fader moder bretheren togyders ſayde theym boldely wyſe somtyme ye ſayde vnto tretyd longe tyme therof ſholde bee wedded corruptyble dedely man though hadde abhomynacion ſuche weddyng myn herte ye myght clerly perceyue many dyuerſe tokenes ye hadde wolde yet reuerence ſholde ſhewe fader moder bydyng god vnto tyme excuſed neuer clerly cauſe may noo lenger ſtyl ſhall declare openly myn herte purpoos whiche purpoos conceyued newe chyldhode vnto tyme▪ therfore wyl ye knowe myn chyldhode made avowe virgynyte ſerue oure lorde ſauyour alle worlde bleſſyd moder gloryous vyrgyn marie gloryous lady chyldely wyth ſa • longe avyſement grete cauſe made avowe alſo ſhold neuer take huſbond hym alone therfore ſyth come ſufferaunce oure lord perfyght age knowleche vnderſton dyng wytte wete ye ryght well ſame purpoos whiche ſoo myghty ſtroonge myn ſowle poſſyble hard flynt ſtones rather made neſſhed myn herte ſhold wythdrawe fro holy pnrpos therfore ye laboure aboute thys thynge tyme ye leſe wherfore counſeyll ye leue alle maner ſuche tretyng weddynge touchyng myn perſone therin ſhall neuer fulfylle wyll cauſe ſholde rather obedyent god man therfore yf ye wylle haue ſuche one hous ſerue god purpoos commyn ſeruaunt ſerue redy may doo ſeruyce gladly yf ye wylle receyue cauſe ye wylle putt hous doo well wete noo wyſe myn herte may wythdrawe fro holy purpos ¶ haue huſbond ſpouſe cryſte jheſu ſoo rychely ſoo myghtely yt wyll ſuffre noo wyſe lacke thyng wyll mynyſtre nedeth whan ſhe hadde ſayde alle thyſe wordes alle herde ſpeke fyll wepyng cauſe plentnouſly ſyghynge ſobbynge myght time gyue none anſwer conſyderid holy purpos thys holy mayde ye whyche myght wyth ſaye ne wythſtonde behylde alſo ſtyll mayden kepte clene pure vnto yt tyme bodely ſhe declared conſciens wordes grete prudence alſo ouer ſawe openli ſhe rather dipoſed forſake faders hous breke holy purpoos ſoo hadde nomore truſte weddyng wherfore lyked theym better wepe gyue anſwer wythin lytyll whyle whan hadde ceſyd wepynge fader yt loued ſoo tenderly dredde god dred god ſoo hyghely hadde mynde coluer ſawe many good dedes whiche ſhe vſed whiche dedes gretely merueylyng gaue ſuche anſwere ſayde dere doughter god forbede ſholde ony thynge wylle deſyre agaynſte wyll god whiche wyll fro whiche wyll knowe well thys holy purpoos cometh fro therefore ſoo ben taught longe experyence openly ſee thou art ſteryd herto lyghteneſſe chyldhode feruent charyte god make thy vowe therfore frely doo lyketh holy ghooſt techeth ¶ fro tyme forward ſhall neuer lette thyn holy purpoosne thyne ghoſtely excerciſe praye v beſely maye bee made worthy promys byheſte thyn ghooſtely ſpouſe thou haſte choſe ſpecyall grace thyn tender age ¶ thenne tourned hym hys wyf chyldren ſayde none tyme forward ne dere donghter greuous none ſoo hardy tyme forward let ony wyſe ſuffer ſerue ſpouſe freely ſhe praye v ſely myght neuer haue founde better huſbond thenne whiche vocheſauf ſo nere kynde wedde doughter haue wyf therfore haue none cauſe pfayne v ſythe ſoo haue receyued dedely man▪ vndedely god man ſpouſe ¶ whan fader hadde ſayde thyſe wordes wyth wepynge wyth weylyng bothe theym ſelfe alſo herde theym hym ſpeke namely ye moder louyd mayde maner fleſſhely then̄e holy maide katheryn ioyefully thanked oure lorde brought vyctorye alſo fader moder wyth alle maner lowenes dyſpoſyng ſelf vſe profytably lycence graū ted ende chapytre ¶ wylle ye knowen redyn heren booke mayſter reymound confeſſour holy mayde knewe neuer reuelacion fader ſawe coluer whiche reſtyd bleſſyd maydens hede fader deed thā mayſter reymoūd knewe bleſſyd mayde knewe reuelaciō coſyns dwellyd faders hous whiche coſins recorded bare wytnes fader ſawe ſuche culuer wyth ofte tymes therfore hadde greate reuerence wold noo wyſe ſhe hadde lettyd troublyd ¶ vyſyon ſhe ſawe ſaynt domynyk bothe mayſter reymound confeſſour afore hym knewe tellyng holy mayde whan mayſter reymound examyned ye wordes ſhe ſayde laſte fader moder brederen ſhe byhad peſecucions ſhe tolde hym alle ordre mekely ¶ hardeneſſe bodely penaū ce afflyction perſecucion ſhe fuffred therfore moder capitulū vj whan deuoute mayde hadde receyued ſo large lycence graunted longe tyme deſyred afore beganne ryght quyckely dyſpoſe merueylouſly alle lyf ſeruyſe god ¶ att begynnyng ſhe aſked haue lytyll chambre ſelf ſo de wherin ſhe purpoſed tourmente body wyth penaunce wylderneſſe ſhe myght haue fredome ſowle ſerue lord moche harde penaunce ſhe vſed tourmentyng body grete loue ſhe hadde ſeyng hyr ſpouſe lytyll chambre maye noo tongue ſuffre telle neuertheles haue reherſed ſom generall grete penaunce purpoſe telle maydens ſpeciall vnder fewe wordes hardneſſe penaunce ſoo ye grete vertuous herbes holy lyuyng maye taſte ſomwhat fruyte growen aboute herber bothe fyrſt laſte condycions kyndis fruyt ſhall declared helpe god afterward cauſe place reherſyd ſom̄e fruyte full vertuous lyuing nothynge ellys maydens ſholde able redyer ghoſtely excercyſe lytyll chā bre graunted ofte tymes ſhe conſydered ſwetely ghoſtely werkis old faders egypte ghoſtely werkys ſoo moche merueylous ſhe hadde trewe knowleche therof faders hous wythout enſample doctryne fyrſt ſhall telle abſtinence mete drynke fro chyldehood tyme ſhe came age ete full ſeldom fleſſhe reherſed afore whan ſhe come age ſpeciall fredom ſhe forſoke vtterly etyng fleſſhe ſoo fer forthe belonge cuſtome vſe ſhe hadde forſakyng ſo lyght ſome payne ſmelle ſhe told confeſſour preuely confeſſyon cauſe ye ſhold haue none gretter merueylle herof ſhall telle another grete abſtynence whan confeſſonr perceyued tyme ſhe gretly waſted feblyd body ſhe receyued none ſuche mete drynke febyll folke ſholde comforted wyth gaue counſeyll ſhe ſholde putte colde water ſhe dranke ſuger lytyl ſuger roſet wherby ſpyrytys myght quyckenyd wyth ſhe touenyd confeſſour ſayde lytyll lyf left wytt whiche ſemeth ye wolde vtterly quenchyd whan confeſſour hadde aſkyd knewe excuſacion vnderſtode wordes ſhe hadde ſoo vſed bytter mete vnſauory drinkys maner ſwete thyng noyous body cauſe dyſpoſycion tourned cuſtome ſoo etyng f • eſſhe reherſed afore whan ſhe ſholde drynke wyne contree foryeuyd tyme ſhe hadde lycence kepe chambre ſhe medlyd wyne ſoo wyth water loſte taſte ſauour alſo grete parte colour afterward whan ſhe xv yere age ſhe lefte alle maner drynkyng wyne vſed drynke colde water maner ſoden mete taken brede alone wythdrewe fro lytyll lytyll euery daye ſomwhat wythin lytyl tyme ſhe helde brede rawe herbes ¶ att laſie whan ſhe twenty yere age aboute ſhe lefte etyng brede helde rawe herbes thenne afterward ſhe came ſuche hyghe ſtate lyuyng nonght vſe kynde ſhall declared openly ynogh wythinforth helpe god oonly myracle alle body oppreſſyd gretely wyth many dyuerſe ſekeneſſe grete traueylles kyndly dygeſtyon body hadde noo place ſtomake alſo vſed myght vſe offyce defyeng yet ſtrengthes body notwythſtondyng ſtrengthe lyuyng mete drynke neuer febly er ſoo confeſſour recordeth alle lyf myracle myght neuer doo ſhe dede ſtrengthe kynde phyſyens ſayd tolde afterward confeſſour oonly myracle thyſe thynges ſhall clerely play nely helpe god openly declared wythin boke afterward concluſyon abſtynence fro tyme confeſſour mayſter reymound knewe recordeth ſhe lyued wyth mete ne drynke nouryſſhynge ne ſhe hadde none comforte none kyndely ſtrengthe yet neuertheles ſhe ſuffred gladly maner dyſeſes laboures came ſhe ſtate lyuynge trowe ye trewely bodely excercyſe vſe rather fulnes ye ſpirite ſhall tel wiſe ye fulnes ye ſpirite ſom̄e tyme rebonudeth body made ſubiecte acordyng werkys ſpyryte ſpiryte goſtely creature fedde wyth gyftes goſtely grace body ſuffreth pacientli aboue naturall ſtrengthe nedes wold dobute herof trowe none reſonable creature whether martyr holy martyrdome ſuffred gladly aboue naturall ſtrengthe tormente myſerye theyr bodyes paſſyons trowe yeis fro whens cometh trowe ye fulneſſe ſpyryte ofte tymes knowen experyens oure dayes yf man womman occupyed goddes ſeruyce deuoutly reketh neuer longe faſteth neuer ſpeke wyth creature whan ceſeth ſpeciall deuocion occupyed outward bodely beſynes harde hym faſte doo dyde whens cometh grace oonly fulnes ſpyryte conforteth body whiche accordeth werkis alle gyfte aboue nature yet naturally ſpyryte otherwhyle communeth wyth body body wyth ſpyryte bothe good euyl thyſe wordes denye ther ben ſomme whiche maye faſte eſely ſomme ſymply faſte abſteyne longe tyme togyder lyf ſemeth inpoſſyble bi nature thus moche reherſed grete abſtynence tyme takyth hede alſo another thynge holy mayde tourmentyd body wyth beſyde abſtinence made bedde al bordes wythout ony ſtuff otherwhyles ſhe wolde ſytte ſtonde holy medytacions whyle knele praye alwaye whan ſhe wolde ſlepe ſhe laye coun wythout ony doyng awaye weryng clothes ſhe weryd alwaye wollen bothe nexte body wythout ſome tyme ſhe vſed hayre cilyce yt ſhe lefte afterward cauſe confeſſour ſuppoſed ſhe clene wythin eſchewed vnclen̄es wythout engendred cilyce hayre hayre ſhe vſed yron chayne next body euyr ſyttyng faſte ſydes wythoute ony remeuynct eaſe vnto tyme endented ſkynne made marke ther vpon hadde forbrennyd ghoſtely doughters felawes tolde ward mayſter reymond confeſſour whiche ghoſtely doughters felawes ofte tymes dyuerſe ſekeneſſes ſhe ſuffred conſtreyned chaunge clothes waſſhe awaye ſwete therfore confeſſour afterward cauſe grete ſekeneſſe ſhe ſuffred lytyl ſhe ſholde deed conſtreyned obedyens ſhe ſholde leue cheyne ſhe wolde doo hyr good wyll euermore ſhe contynued wakyng tyl daye dawed morowe ſhall declared opynly afterward lytyll lytyll lorde gaue grace ouercome ſlepe vnnethe ſhe wold ſlepe half houre two dayes vnnethys ſhe wolde receyue half houre ſekenes couſtreyned therto ſhe wolde ſaye otherwhyle confeſſour mooſt traueylle euer ſhe hadde ouercome ſlepe ſoo harde bataylle ſhe myght haue vyctorye yet ouer confeſſour recorded yf ſhe myght haue founde ony body cowde hadde vnderſtonde commyned wyth hyr vertue goodnes god ſhold greue though ſhe hadde wythout mete drynke ſlepte hondred dayes hondred nyghtes ſhe ſholde neuer haue wery rather freſſher ſhe gladder tolde ofte tymes confeſſour ſhe neuer ſoo well refryſſhed ſpyryt thys lyf whan ſhe myght fynde wyth whome ſhe myght commyne goodnes god knewe well tho whiche conuerſaunt wyth ¶ openly perceyued whan ſhe myght haue leyſer ſpeke god tho thynges vertu whiche hyd herte appieryd ſtrongely ghoſtely gladneſſe body outwarde ¶ whan ſhe hadde noo leyſer talke oure lorde thenne ſhe feble herof bereth wytneſſe confeſſour mayſter reymound worſhyp god owne ſhame oftymes whan holy mayde wolde ſpeke goodnes lorde greate myſeryes ſhewed cauſe longe tyme contynuaunce ſpekyng alſo cauſe ferre louyng ſayde hym ſelfe fyll ſlombryng alwaye ſhe contynued forthe ſpekynge ſhe reyſyd vp loue breſte oure lorde nothyng perceyuynge ſlepe tyll longe tyme afterward whan ſhe perceyued ſlepe wyth grete voys ſhe awoke hym ſayde leſe ye prouffyte ſowle lytyll ſlepe ſpeke walle yow ¶ ferthermore ſhe deſyred aboue alle folowe ſtappes holy fader saynt domynyke wyſe ſhe receyued euery day theyes dyſcyplyne wyth yron chayne fyrſt dyſcyplyne ſelf ſeconde alle tho lyue thirde deed ¶ thus rede legende ſaynt domynyk vſed contynually therfore ſhe vſed ſame longe tyme afterward ¶ tyme ſhe feblyd ſekenes ſhe myght longer vſe hyt ¶ whanne hyr confeſſour axyd hyr pryuely wyſe ſhe vſed manere penaunce wyth grete ſhamefaſteneſſe ſhe knowleched hym ¶ euery dyſciplyne ſhe occnpyed houre halfe ſo mooſt partye blode folowed foo ſholdres doune fete ¶ loo maydens perfeccyon thys holy maydens ſowle thryes daye lete hyr ſelf blood goddys loue ſhedyng hyr blood hys blood see • ye vertue ſhe wyth ony exaumple informacyon ony man erthe vſed ſuche grete penaunce wyth hyr faders hows redeth sayntes lyues wrytyng holy faders egypte leueth none vnſought ſercheth ouer eſpye whether ye fynde ony lyke hyr ye ſhall fynde saynt powſe fyrſt heremyte lyued longe deſerte crowe brought hym euery daye half lof hys mete ye may alſo fynde ſaynt anthonye full holy lyuer dyd grete meruayllous penaunce yet wente dyuers ankrys aboute eche gadred ſomme floures vertue ye may alſo fynde saynt hyllaryon holy lyuer yet saynt jerome ſeyth fyrſt enformed vertuous lyuyng saynt anthonye ro wente deſerte myghtly ouercam hys enemyes ye may fynde alſo macharye arſenye many whyche longe telle techers vertuous lyuyng one moo bothe worde alſo exſaumple deſerte relygion holy mayde nethyr hyr doctryne vertues relygyon nother deſerte hyr faders hows wythout ony informacyon exaumple ony man erthe came grete perfeccyon abſtynence notwythſtondyn ge manyfolde lettyng whyche ſhe ſuffred hyr faders hows shall yet ſaye thys maydens commendacyon praye lyſtene lytel whyle ſhall telle holy wrytte maketh mencyon yt moyſes faſted twyes fourty dayes wyth mete drynke ely one lord iheſu cryſt alſo goſpell ſayth thei faſted many yeres contynued holy wrytte telleth saynt johan baptyſt though deſerte lyued hony ſoukeles herbes ſymply faſted fynde nowhere wryton marye magdelyne allone hyr ſtorye maketh mencyon hyr lyf ſhe faſtyd euery yere fourty dayes gyder wyth mete drynke thre thyrty yeres folowyng leuyng roche ſee trowe lord hye blyſſed moder commytted hyr thys holy mayde hyr may ſtreſſe hyr moder ſomwhat touched afore ſhall clerely de declared afterward helpe god thys may ye knowe thys holy mayde ſpecyall yefte ſynguler grace god ſhe preferryd holy lyuynge aboue alle sayntes whyche ben reherſed afore full odyous comparyſon make ſuche lykenes bytwene sayntes among whiche ſayntes ſauyour iheſu cryſt nempned whome lyken ony ſaynt comparyſon holy lyuyng ſholde euen wyth hym blaſfemye al tho ſayntes whyche ben named reherſed make lykeneſſe merites lyuyng ye ſhal conſydere take hede fyrſt grete magnyfycence lord iheſu cryſt euery day hys gracyous plentuous largenes mult • plyed hys newe yeftes grace wyth arayeth ghoſtly maketh perfyte hys choſen ſowles another alſo ye ſhall conſydere take grete ſynguler worthyneſſe hyr noo iniurye ne wronge ſayntes holy chyrche ſyngeth ſeyth ſpecyally ſyngulerly euery ſaynt hym ſelf thes wordes salamon non eſt inuē tus ſimilis illi none founde lyke thys theſe wordes muſte vnderſtonde grete myght large fredom lord makyng holy perfyte hys choſen ſowles whyche may wylle endowe arraye euery ſaynt ſyngulerly wyth ſpecyall yefte grace wyth ony wronge alle thys mater ſhall ceſſe procede forth fyrſt purpoſe thyſe condycyons abſtynence thys holy mayde may vnderſtōde clerely ſhe lene body wyth ſo many herdenes penaunce ſharpe afflyccyon • ſo often tymes tamed make hyr body buxom ſubgett • ſeruyce ſholdres borthen hors bere bere vp hyghe garet aboue two longe ſteyers ſhe tyme ſhe ſayde twyes ſoo grete body thanne ſhe afterward age xxxviij whan ſhe contynued ſoo grete penaunces hyt meruayll ſo weyker wexxd body though wer • ouercome ſowle wythſtondyng alle thys ſhe wolde euer laboure gladdely namely helthe ſowles ſhe ſuffred grete ſekeneſſe hyr body ſpyryte whyche ſo ſtrong wythin ſuſteyned ſtyghe vp ghooſtly hyr heuenly ſpouſe ſerpent ol de enemye fende though ſhe ouercome hym dyuers tymes afore yet ceſſed aſſaylle hyr eſteſonys ſteryd eue hys doughter lapa thys maydens moder carnall loue ſhe hadde body hyr doughter hyr ſelf lette hyr hyr penaunce tyme whan moder came hyr doughter aſpyed howe ſhe bete hyr ſelf wyth yren chayne ſhe cryed waylyng wyth lowde voys ſeyde doughter doſte thou thou arte dede thou ſleeſt thy ſelf allas hath coūſeylled doughter herto hath ſteryd hyr thys ſoo wyth cryeng waylyng thys olde womman tormēted hyr ſelf ſhe wood body wyth • ryng hyr clothes hyr ſhe thought hyr doughter dede noyſe thys cryeng neghbours ſtyred aboute come inne ſee thys olde woman eyled whan cam ſawe thys holy mayde made hyr bedde bare boordys ſhe reſted ſhe wolde ſlepe wyth vyolence hyr moder took hyr chambre broughte hyr owne chābre ſhe laye ſhe thought ſhe wolde make ſlepe owne bedde wyth hyr whan thys holy mayden ſawe thys wyſdome ſpyryte ſhe ſhewed grete gladnes chere kneled doun fore hyr moder prayng mekely wyth eſy wordes ſhe wolde woucheſauf put awaye alle hyr ſteryng vnpacyence eſy ſhe redy obeye hyr ſhe wolde haue hyr redy lye wyth hyr ſhe wolde bydde hyr whan ſhe thus wyſely p • ſyd moder kepe hyr quyete ſhe layde hyr doune one ſyde bedde ſwete medytacyons ſhe wont • haue tyme hir moder ſlepe ſhe roſe vp pryuely wente agayne hyr holy ghoſtly wyth hyr ſhe took pryuely poſt leyde hyr bedde vnder ſhete clothes abouen moder whan ſhe wold comen vyſyte hyr ſholde ſuppoſe ſhe whyche laye vnder clothes yet neuer theleſſe ſhe kepte hir comyn •• ſtome harde lyeng ſhe dyd fore hyt longe tyme moder aſpyed thys well ſhe aſpyed ſhe ſayd hyr doughter thys wyſe doughter ſee well alle laboure vayne may chaunge thy purpoſe eſe lete ouer paſſe lyghtly therefor go ſlepe thou arte wont • ſoo ſhe ouercomen wyth ſtedfaſtnes thys holy mayde ſuffred hyr euer afterwarde lyue holy ghooſt ſtyred hyr thus endeth thys chapytre somme thynges ther ben reherſed inne hyr confeſſour mayſter reymond knewe hadde reuelacyon holy mayde katheryne▪ hyr grete abſtynence ſharpeneſſe penaūce hyr maner worchyng ſomme thynkes knewe reuelacyon hyr moder lapa ſom dyuers matron conuerſaūt ſom thynges knewe hym ſelf namely hyr ſynguler gracyous yefte abſtynence ¶ laſte vyctorye ſhe bathe ſhe took abyte saynt domynyk whyche ſhe long tyme deſyred fore ca vij whan thys holy mayde reſtoryd ageyn hyr deuoute excercyſe ſhe perceyued enemye mankynde beſy lette hyr feruent ſhe hyr ghoſtly excercyſe euery day ſhe wayled euery day ſhe wepte axynge prayng lorde deuoutly wold woucheſauf gyue hir grace reſceyue abyte ſaynt domynyk ſhe long deſyred whiche thorugh hys grete • yt •• hote hyr • holy fader saynt domynyk vyſyon ſhe neuer ſeker hir ſelf kepe purpoſe maydenhode vnto tyme ſhe reſceyued holy abyte ſhe wyſt well tyme ſhe arayed wyth abyte alle maner ſpeche hyr weddyng ſhold ceſſe ſhe ſholde ſuffred ſerue hyr ghooſtely frely wherfore ſhe prayed hyr fader moder wold gyue hyr leue one ſuſters penaūce ſayn • domynyk ben called comyn ſpeche cyte senee ſuſters mant • ouermore ſhe prayed ſame ſuſtres receyue hyr ſame abyte amonge theyr • holy nombre thys axyng mod well apayed alle ſhe ſayde one nay euer ſhe aboute moche ſhe myght withdrawe hyr hyr grete penaunce ſhe vſed thys cauſe ſhe purpoſed tyme go hoot bath bathed hyr doughter wyth hyr aſſone thys holy mayde felte ony maner comforte ſolace body bathyng lytell lytell ſhe ſhold haue left hyr grete penaunce▪ thys done wythout wyll fende whyche beſyed hym myght wyth drawe ſuche feruent ſowle ghoſtly callynge hyr heuenly ſpouſe taught thys ſynfull wōman lapa maydens moder full pryuely malycyous wylles neuertheleſſe bi cauſe ther may counſeyll preuayll ne haue mayſtrye ageynſt coūſeyll god thys holy mayde armed wyth armere vyctorye bothe hyr ryght ſyde eke hyr lefte ſyde torned alle fende trecherous wylles grete profyt • hyr ſowle whan ſhe came bathe ſhe founde newe maner bathyng hyr ſowle ſhe ſhold tormente hyr body amonge delycyous bathe went condyt • hote water cam inne bathe ſhe ſatte naked ſuffred pacyently hote water brenne hyr tender naked fleſſhe whyche payne hyr thenne whan ſhe bete hyr wyth cheyne ſhall telle hyr confeſſour knewe tyme hyr moder lapa • lde mayſter reymond afore hyr doughter went bathed thenne thys mayde pryuely tolde hym ſhe bathed wyſely peryll deth thys mayde anſwerd hym ſayd full ſymply whan ſhe ſatte bathe ſhe thought beſyly vpon paynes purgatorye hell prayng lord whome ſhe ſo hyely offendyd wolde woucheſauf torne mercyably tho peynes ſhe deſerued temperall payne ſhe ſuffred gladly hys mercy ſhe ſo grete gladdeneſſe hyr herte peyne ryght ſwete hir therfore hyr body thynge hurte though ſhe felt peyne whan ſhe tolde thys tale hyr confeſſour wente home ſhe ageyne hir penaūce ſhe wont vſe whan hir mod yt ꝑceyued ſhe hope tho hir chaungyng yet ſhe ceſſyd neuer wyth grutchyng penaunce ſhe vſed whyche grutchyng thys mayde hyr eche ſuche ſadde age yt myght coude gouerne ſelf ſaddely cauſe theſe ſuſters penaunce anſwerd thus ſhall declared helpe god openly nough next chapytre ſueth whan moder anſwere ſhe went home tolde hyr doughter whiche anſwere doughter full gladſome moder full heuyſom neuertheleſſe yet thys holy mayde myſtruſted ſhe wyſ • welle hyr purpoſe ſholde fulfylled behot hir ſo gloryous fader saynt domynyk
