ſone happed thys mayde fyll ſeek body whyche ſekeneſſe comynly yong folk ben vexyd wyth thā ne come ſadde age yet p • raduenture paſſynge •• ſh • ſuff • ed hote bathe myght cauſe al wyl god yt ſhold ſo ſkynne hyr body full bladder byles vnnethe ſhe myght knowe alſo ſhe ſtrong feuer moder ſeyng hyr doughter ſoo ſeek though ſhe loued hir ſones doughter tenderly yet thys doughter ſhe nouryſſhed wyth hyr owne mylke ſhe loued tenderly therefor ſhe ſory hyr dyſeaſe ſhe knewe cauſe thys ſekeneſſe cam ſuche ſekeneſſe myght come abſtynence rather ſupfluyte alſo ſame tyme comyn ſekeneſſe yong chyldren yong maydens therefor ſhe coude deme ſekeneſſe came eſe remedye ſhe myght ſhe dyd bothe wordes comfort alſo dede ſyttyng alle waye beddes ſyde hyr ſeker ye doughter body ye ſtrenger ſhe hyr holy deſyre wayteng leyſyr conſtreng hyr mod manere purſewe fulfyll hyr deſyre wyſely ſwetly ſhe ſayde hyr moder good dere moder yf ye wold hole ferd • well praye beth aboute yt deſyre may fulfylled receyue abyte penaūce ellys wote well lord ſaynt domynyk whyche haue called ſeruyce woll ſo ordeyne ye ſholde longer haue thys lyf whan moder herde thys oft • many tymes reherſed hyr ſhe beynge ferde leſt ſhe ſholde haue deyde went ſame ſuſters ageyn prayed ſo entyerly abyte ouercome wyth hyr prayer ſo graūted hyr thys wyſe yf youre doughter noght ouer ſemely body ouer f • •• beaute ſhall graun •• axyng receyue hyr yf ſhe fayre drede v peryll ſlandre malycyou • lyuyng men thyſe dayes thys cauſe dare conſente receyue hyr noo wyſe moder anſwerd ſayde cometh ſee hyr eue ye dome whee ſhe fayre ſente two dyſcrete matron choſen amonge wyth lapa ſee thys mayde bothe dyſpoſycyon hyr body alſo ſerche hyr deſyre ſoule come founde thys mayde lyeng ſeek bedde therefor myght clerely knowe dyſpoſycyon hyr body ſekeneſſe neuertheleſſe hyr wordes knewe hyr feruent deſyre ſowle ſeruyce god gretly aſtoyned alſo gladde ſeeng ſo yong mayden paſſe vertuous • yuyng many olde matron wherefor took leue ioyefully gretely edyfyed hyr wordes tolde theyr felawys grete ioye harde ſawe whan thiſe ſuſters herde thys counſeyll frerys receyued hyr oo wyl one aſſent • amōges ſendyng worde moder alſo ſone ye mayden hole ſhe ſhold brynge hir ye frere prechours ſhe myght r • ceyue abyte saynt domynyk whyche ſhe ſo long deſyred preſence brethern ſuſt • en ſame abyte cuſtome whan moder tolde theſe wordys hyr dought ſhe gladde ſhe wepte ioye thanked lord ſaynt domynyk hadde fulfylled hys promys byh • ſt thanne ſhe began preye god ſhe myght hole hyr bodely infyrmy •• fulfylle hir holy purpoſe receyuyng abyte leſt ſhe ſhold lette delayed hyr deſyre bodely ſeke •• ſſe ſhe fyrſt gladde hir bodely ſekeneſſe meke ſuffraū ce afterward ſhe heuy therof beſekyng lord beſy prayer wold wouchelauf delyuer hyr wyth ony taryeng ſekeneſſe whiche letted purpoſe hyr deſyre ſhe prayed lord graūted hir wyth fewe dayes afterward ſhe hole lord wold alway goodneſſe denye axyng ſuche conferme euer wyth theyr beſyneſſe fulfylle hys wyll euer ſhe axyd deſyred ſhe referred ſhe loued wyth myghtes hir ſowle • ſeruyce ſhe offred hyr ſelf hole body ſowle whome ſhe reſtoryd bodely hele alle mod aboute tarye hyr hyr purpoſe lenger tyme made ſuche inſtaū ce hyr moder day houre aſſygned whan ſhe ſholde receyue hyr abyte whyche abyte ſhe receyued wyth grete ghoſtly gladneſſe whanne moder doughter come gyder chyrche frere charge ſuſters arayed holy mayde wyth maner abyte preſence colour whyte blak token innocence keneſſe whyche abyte holy faders saynt domynykes ordre ordeyned hadde soo whytnes vnderſtonde innocencye blakneſſe mekenes mayſter reymond hyr confeſſour recordeth wryteth▪ ther none abyte ſoo well accordyng hyr conuerſacyon lyuyng bothe inward outward thenne thys mayden wyth alle hyr myght •• tyme forthward mortyfyed hyr body ſleyng olde luſt ſynne wyth alle hys braunches pryde wynnyng veray mekeneſſe whyche mekeneſſe betokeneth mantell blacke ſhe hadde receyued alſoo ſhe beſyed hyr wyth alle hyr myghtes kepe innocencye virgynytee maydenhode onely body alſo ſowle endeles ſpouſe iheſu cryſt whyche veray lyght receyue hym fayreneſſe vertuous lyuyng whyche fayreneſſe betokenyd whyte cote vnder mantell yf hyr abyte black alle whyte tho two thynges mekeneſſe innocencye myght properly vnderſtonde therby yf hyr abyte hadde ben graye ruſſeth myght repreſente mortyfycacyon properly puryte clenneſſe ſowle thys cauſe ſuſters begynnyng denyed hyr thys abyte leſt ſhe hadde able bere mekeneſſe clenneſſe herte dredyng hyr yonge age whanne holy mayde hadde receyued abyte hyt become hyr better dyd matron therfor well hadde denyed hyr whyche abyte ordeyned fore holy faders token innocencye syth ſoo ſhe paſſyd clennes alle chaſtyte wedowhode one thynge hyr confeſſour mayſter reymond recordeth wryteth abyte hadde neuer hys full perfeccyon cytee senee vnto tyme holy mayde hadde take vpon hyr hyt fyrſt mayde cytee took vp hyr whyche many maydens afterward receyued alſo soo myght ſonge hyr verſe dauyd prophete ſpeketh adducentur regi virgines poſteam lorde god endeles kyng many maydens ſhall brought inne thys holy mayde katheryne ¶ thys mayden encreced ſhall declared afterward helpe god ſhall make ende thys chapytre procede forthe thys holy abyte beganne thys holy relygyous eſtate leſt defaute knowyng opynyon fame thys holy maydens vertuous lyuynge myght leſſenyd therby ſomme mennys hertys matere whyche reherced thys chapytre mayſter reymond recordeth ſeyth hadde relacyon hyr moder hyr ſelf abyte nedeth profe knowen openly ynough ¶ begynnyng foundamente relygyous ſtate ſuſters penaunce saynt domynyk came manere lyuyng tho ſuſtren capitulum viij alle tho wyll rede thys preſente chapytre folowynge ſhall fynde wryten recorded many feythfull creature dyuerſe partyes ytalye many worthy actys dedys holy fader saynte domynyk gloryous worthy confeſſour cryſte tutor defendour feyth holy chyrche saynte domynyk alſo techer enfourmer good ſtate perfyte lyuers ouercame myghtely bothe tholoſe alſo lombardye hym ſelfe hys brethern many heretykes tyme canonizacion rome prouyd openly • holy fader pope hondred thouſand heretykes tourned hys prechyng ſhewyng myracles lumbardye alone ¶ neuertheles venemous doctryne heretykes hadde ſoo enfected peple ſowles almooſt poſſeſſyons holy chyrche laymennes hondes kepyng owne herytage cauſed byſſhoppe • goo aboute begge hadde none power neuer wythſtonde • ye defaulte temperall ſubſtaunce ne releue clerkys poure folke dewe offyce conſydered holy fader saynt domynyke myght none wyſe ſuffre myſcheff holy chyrche grete entyrly loue hadde therto chaas worthy lyf pouerte hym ſelfe alſo theim ſhold folowers thenne beganne purſue forthe ryght holy chyrche aſſoſyeng • hym cert • yn laye people • ed god knew well ſo cōmyned wyth theym ordeynaunce holy lyuyng ſholde recouere againe rycheſſes holy chirche defended myghtely euer afterward faithfully agaynſt heretikes comyn aſſent ſuche lyf ſoo graunted ordeyned ¶ holy fader saynt domynyke founde ony well wyllynge folke ſuche lyuyng fyrſt enduced theym ſwere ſholde kepe obſerue thynges ſhold reherced theym vtereſt putte goodes lyf therfore jeoperdye le • te holy lyuynge ſholde bee lette ſuche •• wedded made alſo wyues ſwere ſholde alſo lette huſbondes maynten ſuche poure lyuyng ryght holy chyrche rather ſholde helpe theym power might eyther partye holy fader ſaynt domynyke byhote theym ſykerly yf kepte purpoos endeles lyf mede ¶ tho men toke holy lyf vppon called fryer cryſico knyghthode neuertheles cauſe • ey ſholde beknowen fro ſomme token ſholde haue ſomme maner beſynes aboue vſage laye peple gaue colour owne habyte bothe men wymmen ſame knyghthode iheſu cryſt ſhold whyte blake soo eyther colour ſholde apere outward token innocencye mekenes euermore aſſigned theym ſaye certeyn nombre pater noſters aue maria ſholde occupyed euery houre diuyne ſeruyce day • day▪ whan tyme ſaynt domynyk paſſed worlde blyſſe heuen encreſyng myracles canonyzed court rome f •• re ſuſter • yt fyrſt called ye knyghthode ihu cyr •• amo •• ſynguler▪ worſhyp foūder ſaynt domynyk chaūged name cō mī aſſ • called f •• er ſuſters penaūce ſaynt domynyk ye cauſe thought yt fyrſt name ſholde chaūged ſaw bi merytes myracles ſaynt domynyk prechyng ye fryer curſed hereſye cauſe wherfore theym thought yt moche nedefull occupyed ſuche outward batayle prechyng rather wythinward batayle agaynſt goſtely enmyes choſe therfore called fryer ſuſters penaūce ye laſt ye nōbre fryer prechours encreſyd ſo hugely amonge one clere ſhynnyng ſterre saynt peter bothe martyr mayde whiche martred heretykes ryght holy chyrche deſtroyed heretykes deth ſoo thys company wulues aboute deſtroye goddes vnite holy chyrche vtterly avoyded pea yelden holy chyrche wherfore cauſe name knyghthede ſeſyd channged name penaunce neuertheleſſe maner ſtate louyng deſcendeth remayneth men whyle ther wyues ben left ſoole lyuyng theym ſelf relygyous lyf neuer afterward deſyryng bee wedded cauſe relygyous kepte wyth huſbondes fore ſtate whiche began kepte lyues ende ¶ conſyderyd behelde wydowes purpoſed kepe theym wedowhode deſiring folowe ſuſters penaunce saynt domynyke remedye ſynnes prayed fryer prechours italye enforme maner lyuyng whiche ordeyned saynt domynyke cauſe maner lyuyng hard bleſſyd fader ſame ordre whiche called munyo wrote maner lyuyng toke thyſe wydowes whiche manere lyuyng daye callyd amonges theym rule thay may properly callyd ſoo moche encludeth wythin thre pryncypall vowes relygyous folke haue tyme nombre ſuſters thus encreſed dyuerſe partyes italye holy fader pope tho dayes whiche called honoryus perceyued good lyuynge thyſe ſuſters graunted theym bulle tyme interdyction myght dyuyne ſeruyce amonges fryer prechours ſoo holy fader pope johan whiche came hym hadde made conſtytucions clementynis agaynſte vyrgyns gardys declared bulle ſame decretall conſtytucion ſholde vnderſtonde ſame ſuſters penaunce saynt domynyke decretall aſtate repreued ony wyſe ¶ loo maydens ye may vnder ſtonde ſtate liuing foū de wymmen ſuſters anſwerd ſoo att begynnynge moder holy mayde wounte receyue maydens ſtate lyuyng oonly wydowes approuyd ſadnes thyſe thynges ben wrytten chapytre parte mayſter reymound founde wryten im dyuerſe place italye ſome mater herde vnderſtode theym wyth inquyſycion many holy faythfull olde fryer ſuſters saynt domynyke thus endeth chapytre ¶ wonderfull encrece ſhe prouffyted vertu holy lyuyng ſhe ſholde bee byloued thynges whiche ſhe reherſed confeſſour grace done lorde capl ix holy mayde receyuinge habyte made none byheſt thre pryncipalle avowes relygyon cauſe eſtat aſked nought reherſed afore yet neuertheleſſe ſhe purpoſed kepefull ſtedfaſtly tho thre pryncypal avowes ī ſelf vowe chaſtyte none doughte ſhe hadde made avowe maydenhode afore tender age touchyng obedyence purpoſed oonly bee obedyent fryer mayſter ſuſters pryoreſſe ſame ſuſters alſo confeſſour whiche obedyence ſhe kepte lyues ende ¶ ſhe ſayde lyue whan ſhe ſholde paſſe worlde hadde neuer mynde ſhe brake oni obedyence neuerthels cauſe ſomme whiche hadde enuye holyneſſe bacbyters lyers ſayde contrarye ¶ doo vnderſtonde maydens thowe holy mayde hadde none tourment whyle ſhe lyuynge erthe oonly vndyſcrete byddyng myſſeyng ſouereyns ſhe myght haue ben maner martyr grete pacience whiche ſhe ſuffred confeſſours vnderſtood nonght ne gaue none credence many tymes excellent gyfte grace ſhe receyued god ne gaue none reuerence werkys lorde wrought merueylouſly therforre wold haue made lyuyng commyn lyuyng ſuſters conſyderyng ye opyn token grace ſhewed dyuerſe tymes rather myghi lykened ye pharyſens ſeyth opyn myracles whyche lord wrought yet grutched cauſe helyd man vpon ſabat daye ſeyng thus ¶ non eſt hic homo deo qui ſabbatum non cuſtodit man god halſ kepeth ſabat daye holy mayde whan ſhe hadde receyued habyte penaunce▪ ſhe beſyed ſhe cowde obeye ſouereyns therto ſhe durſt forſake ye waye vertuous lyuynge whiche lord taught hym ſelf ſoo bytwene thyſe two ſhe ſore angwiſſhed tourment ther maye none tongue telle ne penne wryte trought ye maydens martyrdome trowe yeis lorde god ofte ſayde repref yt vyſyons come nought god fende ¶ notwythſtondyng whiche ſawe many merueylous werkes therto myght ſee lyf myracle ſhall declared clerely ſtronge martyrdome ſemeth ¶ touchyng pouerte lynyng ſhe kepte ſoo perfyghtly vertu pouerte ſhe beyng faders hous houſholde greate plente temperall goodes ſelf ſhe toke thynge ſhe wolde gyue frely poure folke therto fader gaue ſpecyall leue ¶ loued ſoo moche pouerte ſhe ſayde preuyly confeſſoure ſhe hadde neuer ioye faders hous cauſe temperall goodes ſoo plenteuoſly vſed therin therfore ſhe prayed oure lord hertely wolde vocheſauf tak awaye rycheſſe brynge hyr frendes pouerte ſeyng wyſe lorde whether good aboundeth ſoo plentuouſly myn faders hous good ſholde aſke myn frendes nought oonly good euerlaſtyng knowe well lord amonges thyſe temperall goodes moche peryll medeled amonge therfore wolde nought myn frendes encombred wyth theym ¶ whan ſhe hadde thus prayed lorde goodnes herde prayer ſuffred hee frendes fader moder kynne falle ryght lowe pouerte many merueylous chaunces wythout ony treſpaas theym well knowe tho knewe theym whyles lyued may ye knowe mayden kepte full dewely thre pryncipall vowes relygyon obedyence chaſtyte pouerte ſhe made none avowe openly whan ſhe receyued habyte penaunce ſhall telle perfection tyme ſhe hadde receyued habyte whan ſhe hadde receyued habyte holy fader saynt domynyke promyſed ſhe began anone ſwete vertuous lyuynge ſought occacions cauſes conſtreyne ſelf ſtreyghtly ſhe dyde afore ſhe myght deuoutlye loue ſpouſe iheſu ſeyng ſelf wyſe lo thou haſt take vp maner relygyon thou mayſt nomore lyue thou haſt doo thy ſeculer lyuynge goo newe relygyon come whiche reule thou muſt nedes reuled • eſt thou colour thyn clothes nedeth fro time forward kepe perfyghtly pouerte clenneſſe body ſowle whiche tokeneth bi whyte cote nedeth alſo dede worlde whiche betokenneth blake mantel therfore ſee thy ſelf thou gouerneſte thou muſte goo ſtreyte waye fewe walken ynne ſekerneſſe therfore kepyng pouerte clē neſſe ¶ holy mayde purpoſed kepe ſylence full ſtreyte ſpeke whan ſhe ſhold ſhryue confeſſour ſayde wrote afore mayſter reymound▪ thre yere contynuelly ſhe kepte ſylence whan ſhe wolde beſhryue kepte alſo contynuelly chambre whan ſhe wolde goo chyrche mete ſhe hadde none nede goo lytyll ſoone doo ſhe vſed ete none maner mete made fyre taken breed alone reherſed afore ¶ alſo ſhe made ordynaunce owne herte neuer come mete wyth wepyng ſoo euer afore mete ſhe wolde offre lord teres fede ſoule fyrſt afterwarde wolde ſhe ſuſteyne body wyth mete ¶ faders hows wylderneſſe deſerte notwythſtondyng confluence peple therin ¶ beſyde wakyng prayer medytacions teres ſhe vſed trowe none tongue cowde telle ¶ made alſo ordynaunce ſelf whan bretheren freer prechours ſtepte ſhe wolde wake whan frier hadde tonge ij peel matyns anone erſt wolde ſhe ſeye ſpouſe iheſu cryſte wyſe loo lorde myn bretheren thyn ſeruauntes haue reſted thē tyme haue prayed theym thou ſholdeſt kepe fro deuelys fro ouercomyng fendes ¶ lorde aryſe praye therfore lorde praye kepe theym gyue leue reſte whyle ſoo ſhe laye doune vpon hard bordes ſtoke vnder hede ſtede bolſter ¶ lord iheſu gracious ſpouſe ſeyng mayde whiche gaue thyſe grace wolde ſuffer ſoo able ſoo dylygent dyſcyple vntaught wythout perfyght mayter nother man ne angell hym ſelf wolde informer vertu anone ſhe ſhett vp chambre oure lorde iheſu cryſte well beloued ſpouſe ſauyour alle mankynde appieryd taught enformed fully tho thynges longeth helthe ſowle ſhe ſelf tolde priuely ward confeſſour ſayde hym thyſe wordes fader vnderſtondeth trouthe neuer taught ne enformed ony thynge longeth helth ſowle man ne woman oonly myn lorde iheſu ſpouſe ſowle inſpyracion ellys hys open apperyng ſpekyng nowe ſpeke ¶ knowleched alſo confeſſour begynnyng vyſyon whan apperyd openly bodely wyttes ſoo ſhe perceyued wyth bodeli erys voys ſhe began waxe ferd leſt hadde deceyte fende ofte tymes tranſfygureth hym angell lyght whiche feer noo wyſe dyſpleſyd lorde rather commended feer ſayde longe man woman lyueth lyf ſholde euer aferd ſoo thou mayſt fynde wryten ¶ beatus vir qui ſemper eſt pauidus ſaye bleſſyd man euer feerfull ¶ ferthermore oure lorde iheſu cryſte ſayde doughter wylt thou ſhall teche thou mayſte knowe myn vyſyon vyſyon fende holy mayde anſwerde full mekely prayed hym wolde voucheſauf teche thenne ſayde oure lorde thyn ſoule may eſely taught inſpyracyon worde dyſcerne bytwene one cauſe wolde myght prouffyghte well therfore ſhall teche worde ¶ doctours holy chyrche whome haue taught trouthe ſeyn ſoothe myn vyſyon begynneth wyth drede euer paſſyng ſetteth ſowle greate reſte ſekernes begyn̄eth wyth maner bytternes euermore wexith ſwete contrarye herte dothe vyſyon fende gyueth begynnyng ſemeth maner gladdenes ſykenes ellys ſweteneſſe whan paſſeth awaye euer encreſeth ſowle dred bytterneſſe treweſt knowleche knowe myn wayes fendes wayes ¶ waye penaūce kepynge myn preceptys commaundementes begynnyng ſemeth harde ſharpe ſowle prouffyteth kepyng theym eſely waxith ¶ waye ſynne begynnyng ſemeth full delectable euer encres therof ſowle made dampnable ¶ yet ſhall gyue another token knowe myn vyſyon vyſyon fende vnderſtonde ſothe ſythe ſoo trouthe euer myn vyſyons ſowle man receyueth greate knowleche trouthe cauſe knowleche trouthe full neceſſarye ſoule well ſelf ſhe may knowe ſelf whiche knowleche ſhe paſſeth fro ſelf ſettinge lytyll ſelfe honoureth worſhyppeth whiche condycion properly called condycions mekenes therfore full nedefull ſowle ſholde thus knowe ſelf ſoo made meke vyſyon contrarye vyſyon fē de ſythe ſo fende fader leſynge kynge chyldren pryde may gyue hathe leſyng pryde therfore viſyō ſoule ſemeth moche ſelf made glad 〈…〉 joye whiche properly condycion pryde ſo ſhe lefte ſwellyng bolnyng pryde then̄e therfore yf thou examyne dyſcuſſe dylygently thy ſelf mayſte knowe whether vyſyon come trouthe ellys falſeneſſe yf come trouthe maketh thyn ſowle meke yf come falſenes deſceyte maketh thyn ſowle proude ¶ thenne hooly mayde whan ſhe hadde herde thys ſhe kepte holſome doctryne full dylygently ſowle tolde afterward confeſſour alſo edyfycacion ſhall reherſyd wythinforthe helpe god thenne began lorde ſhewed holy mayde viſyons reuelacyons plentuouſly ſoo ferforth yt vnnethe myght founde two men ſo homely conuerſacion gyders oure lorde jheſu ſhe gyders whether ſhe prayed redde medytacions walked ſlepte wyſe ſhe comforted many time whan ſhe ſpake wyth ſhe hadde reuelacions vyſyons ſpake ſowle lord whyles tongue ſpake outward myghte longe contynue ſowle ſo wonderly drawe vp ſpouſe jheſu wythin lytyll whyle afterward rauyſſhed bodely felyng rauyſſhyng came many merueylous thynges foloweth afterward▪ well grete abſtynence merueylous doctryne alſo vpon myracles whiche oure lorde ſhewed lyffe leſt ſomme wolde doubte whether holy mayde hadde ſuche reuelacions ſhalle telle confeſſour mayſter reymound preued whether reoelacions vyſyons trewe begynnyng whan mayſter reymound herde hye cōuerſaciō liuyng begā waxe homely wyth comunycacion wyth coude fele verely yt ſuche reuelacyons myght trewe whiche myſtruſte better therfore enquyred diuers menes wayes knowe whether came god fende whether fals trewe thenne came mynde ypocritis whiche regnyd dayes founde many dyſcetys namely amōges wymmen ye deuyll dyſceyued wyth ye vyce aboue creaturs hyt came alſo mynde ye fyrſt womman eue deceyued many ſuche therefor doubted holy mayde whyle ſtode long thus ſuche doubte came mynde yf myght hir prayer gete lord one grete contrycyon hys ſynnes aboue cuſtomable contrycyon yt wonte haue myght knowe hyr vyſyons reuelacyons dedys come holy ghoſt ther may none gete ſuche contrycyon yefte holy ghoſt ther none lyuyng ſaye whether worthy god hate loue yet hertely contrycyon ſynnes grete token grace mayſter reymond ſo ſone thought thys went thys holy mayde prayed hir hertely ſhe wold praye hym oure lord yt woucheſauf gyue hym ſynnes whyche done thys holy mayde anſwerd ſayd ſhe wold full gladly ſayde mayſter reymond myght eaſyd deſyre hyr prayer onely yf bull hys ſynnes gyuen thys holy mayde axed wyth ſmylynge chere bull deſyred haue anſwerd token bull axed one grete contrycyon hys ſynnes whiche contrycyon thys holy mayde ſayde ſhold haue redy thenne tyme hyt ſemed mayſter reymond ſhe vnderſtode clerely hys thoughtes ſo went hyr morne happed mayſter reymond ſeek laye bedde kepte one hys brethern deuoute man whyche called nycholas pyſe place ther lay ſeek hows ſuſtres moche caught hys ſekenes ſodeynle jorneyng waye whan holy mayde perceyued ſeke • o vp hyr bedde wythſtondyng ſhe ſeek hir ſelf feuers dyuers paſſyons ſayd hyr felawe goo ſee ſrere reymond dothe fare hyr felawe anſwerd ſayd nede though nede yet ſhe ſeker neuertheleſſe yet ſhe come hym axyd ferd anone whan ſawe hyr meruaylled gretety ſayd hyr fe • illy myght ſpeke aa lady come ye hyther ye agrete dele ſeker thanne ſhe began ſpeke goodneſſe lord ſhe wonte oure vnkyndneſſe ayenſt hym wyth mayſter reymond hir confeſſour aroſe vp hys bedde gretely comforted hyr wordes ſate bedde beſyde hauyng mynde yet wordes holy mayde ſpake hym euen afore whyle ſhe contynued ſpekyng kyndenes lord oure grete vnkyndenes sodeynly tyme hyr deuoute comunycacyon came hys mynde clere conſyderacyon hys ſynnes hym thought ſtode afore ryghtwys jugement condempned peyne wycked lyuyng ryght theef ſtood temporall juge hym thought alſo ſawe hys ſoule grete benygnyte mekenes lorde gracyouſly delyuered hym fro peyne worthy haue onely alſo clothed hym wyth hys owne clothes ther naked hym hys holy hows fedde hym nouryſſhed hym accepted hym hys ſeruyce ther ſynguler grace hys ende loo goodneſſe hys deth vnto lyf hys drede vnto hope hys ſorow vnto ioye hys ſhame vnto worſhyp thyſe conſyderaciōs clerely knowynges ſyghte hys ſoule wyckettes wyndowes harde herte broken vp opened wellys ryuers wepyng terys aperyd plenteuouly cauſe foundament grounde hys treſpaſſys ſhewed ſo clerely hym ſo moche wayled aferde laſte ſuche grete plente ſorow hys herte breſt wold haue barſt whan thys holy mayde ſaw ſhe ſtyll ſuffred hym whyle fedde wyth hys owne terys therefore ſhe came wythin whyle ceſſyd lytell lytell bethought meruayllouſly newe grace thynkyng alſo hys petycyon whiche axed holy mayde day wyth torned hyr ſayd thys thy bull ſpak yeſterdaye anſwerd ſayd ye laynge hir hondes vpon hys ſholdres ſeyeng thus haue mynde fader gracyous yeftes lord ſoo wente home hyr chambre abode ſtylle wyth hys felawe gretely edyfyed comforted another tyme ſame mayſter reymond another excellent token thys holy mayde wyth ony axyng afore hit happed tyme thys holy mayde vyſyted dyuers ſekenes laye ſeek hyr bedde ſent hyr confeſſour deſyryng comen wyth pryuely newe reuelacyons whyche lord ſhewed grete ſekeneſſe beganne ſpeke goodnes lord reuelacion ſhewed hyr day heryng ſo grete reuelacyon • wonderfull ſhewed hyr none euer herde hauyng mynde grace lord hadde gyue hym afore prayer holy mayde bethought hym ſomthynges ſhe reherſed ſayd himſelf thus whether trewe ſhe ſeyth whanne thought thus loked ſodeynly hyr face ſaw hyr vyſage tranſformed mannes vyſage berded whyche vyſage behelde hym ſtedfaſtly made hym ſore aferde hit ſyght ſemely longe vyſage myddel age hauynge long berde reſonable aſſiſe coloured whete ſhewyng ſyghte mageſte mageſte oure lord jheſu myght wyſe tyme ſee none face onely face thys ſyght ſo grete fere lyfte vp armes began crye ſayd oo loketh vpon whome holy mayde anſwerd ſayd ſeeth beholdeth wyth worde dredefull face vanyſſhed awaye maydens vyſage appyred clerely thys feynyng thyng trewe recordeth bereth wytnes hys wrytynges recordeth alſo confyrmacyon myracle ſenſybly vyſyon hadde ſoo clere knowyng wythin hymſelf im ſowle ghoſtly illumynyng mater holy mayde ſpak hym whiche wyll pupplyche openly hym thought felt experyence thyng whyche lorde ſayd hys dyſcyples whan behote holy ghooſt ſeyeng theim thus et que ventura ſunt annunciabit vobis whan ye haue receyued holy ghoſt ſhall ſhewe thynges ben come loo myſtruſt hadde wordes oure lorde gracyous goodneſſe woucheſauf teche hym clerely ſelf afterward bere wyttenes hir reuelacions ben trewe pryntyng ſtedfaſtly mynde grete grace ſhewed saynt thomas inde wolde taught enfourmed open tokenes gracyous gyfte whyche receyued holy mayde taught enformed example ſuche diſciple myſtrowyng tyme receyued gracyous token conpunccyon lord fore merytes holy prayer holy mayde yet contynued myſtruſt hyr reuelacyons trewe wherefor lord himſelf ſhewed hym ſelf openly outeward wyttys myght therby knowe open experyence ſpak hir ſo may ſayd ſhewed thenne mayſter reymond whiche myſtrowed dyd ſom tyme ſaynt thomas inde bodely felyng ryght cryed afterward ſayd worde deus meus et dominus meus god lord may thys myſtrowynge renuwed ſaye thiſe two vyſyōs holy mayde ſhe veray ſpouſe veray diſcyple lord god theſe ben reherſed maydens ye ſholde doubte ne deſpyſe reuelacions vyſyons whiche ye ſhall helpe god afterward alle wytnes may founde recorde ſaue ſhe allone ye ſholde hem rede hem vnderſtonde hem reuerence alſo ye may lerne ther holy example doctrynes whiche lord hath ſhewed ſuche veſſell kynde ſeke bryttell grace meruaylouſly made ſtrong precyous thus make ende chapytre thoo thynges whiche mayſter reymond taught enfourmed holy mayde hath declared openly chapytre outake one thyng charged hyr kepe pryuely certeyn reuelacion reherſed fore ¶ noble doctryne whyche lord gaf hyr begynnyng doctrynes whyche founded hyr maner lyuyng capitulum x syth ſo grounde foundament truſt byleue touche reuelacyons holy mayde helpe god declared chapytre goth afore therfore ſhall procede forth ſhewe ſpyrytuall edyfycacyon ſame mayde cauſe trewe ſowles feythfull ben fedde edyfyed wordes lord therefor ſhall telle ſhewe notable doctryne ye whiche holy mayde taught lord ſelf thys holy mayde tolde hyr confeſſours amonges mayſter reymond one begynnyng hyr vyſyons lord appyred hyr whan ſhe prayed ſayde hyr wyſe knoweſt thou doughter thou arte yf thou knowe well theſe two wordes thou art ſhalt bleſſyd thou art ſhe art yf thou haue veray knoweleche theſe two thynges thy ſoule thy ghoſtly enemye ſhall neuer dyſceyue thou ſhalt eſcape gracyouſly ſnares ne thou ſhalte neuer conſente ony thyng ayenſt commaundementes preceptes alle grace alle treuthe alle charyte thou wylte wynne wythout ony hardeneſſe bryef worde grete maner infynyte endeles oo grete wyſdome expreſſyd vnder fewe ſyllables whether leng brede heythe depthe whiche ſaynt poule deſyred haue wyth ſayntes trowe yes oo dere maydens conſydereth beholdeth meruayllouſly incomparable treſoure whiche founde holy maydes breſte lord jheſu vndeceyuable trouth ſeyth holy mayde thus yf thou knowe thyſe two thynges thy ſowle fende ſhall neuer deceyue ſemeth full good make thre tabernacleſ dwellyng place vnto worſhyp god excellent doctou • whiche • ched vnderſtondyng thyſe fruytfull wordes another loue deuocyon holy mayde katheryne whiche receyued holſom doctryne fewe fruytfull wordes thyrde ghoſtly treſoure valour tho whiche fynden lyf fewe fruytfull wordes vnderſtondyng thoo fruytfull wordes founden ghoſtly rycheſſe ſo plenteuouſly ſhall nede alle tho haue ſoo founde ghoſtly rycheſſe begge whether bryef fruytfull ſentence trewe ſayde art thou ſhe troweyes euery creature made maker jheſu cryſt nought ferforth yf lord jheſu cryſt oure maker wolde ceſſe tyme neuer ſo lytell fro conſeruacyon hys creature hath made anone creature ſhold torne nought whan ſoo euer creature doth ſynne whyche ſynne hym ſelf nought ne hym ſelf may noo thynge thynke ought saynt poule ſeyth meruaylle may ne haue beyng ſelf ne yet conſerued ſelf beyng therfore apoſ • le ſayd qui ſe exiſtimat ali • uid eſſe cū nichil fit ipſe ſe ſeduci • wenyth ought nought decey ueth hym ſelfe se • ſt thou mayde noughty creature creature made nought euer ſelf • owyng nought ſynne maketh ſelf noughte saynt auſtyn ſayd may noo thyng ought hym ſelf rather nought oure lorde ſayd sine nichil po •• ſtis ſacere wythout ye may ryght nought whyche nought ſynne therfore ye may wel clerely know creature hym ſelf nought knewe well saynt • afore thys tyme whiche knoweleche veray wyſdom excluded vera • ly theyr ſowles alle manere ſynne manere inflacyon ſynne may entree ſuche ſowle whiche knoweth hir ſelf nought may ſhe ioyfull vayne glorye ony good werke euer ſhe dyd whiche knoweth wel nough ſuche good dedys come neuer hir fro god may ſuche ſowle enhaunce hir ſelfe pryde aboue holdeth hyr ſelf nought may ſowle thus ſett • th hir ſelf nought inwardely deſpyſe haue enuye may ony creature haue vaynioye outwarde rycheſſe hath dyſpyſed owne ioye hym ſelf trowe ſuche creature taught wordes lord endeles wyſdom ſayd siego quero gloriam meam gloria mea nichil eſt yf ſeek myn owne ioye ioye nought alſo may ſuche creature knowed hym ſelf wyſe owne onely made hym ſee alle outwarde thynges myne ſyth hym ſelf myght make ſuche creature haue delectacyon fleſſhely ſynnes euery day reſtreyneth hym ſelf ſuche manere conſyderacion nought loo maydens bryef fruytfull wordes thou art nought ye may conſydere maner ſynne may excludeth bryef fruytful worde oure lorde ſayde holy mayde whether bryef fruytful worde newe worde ye forſothe bothe newe olde olde worde lorde ſayde moyſes ſuſſh whiche ſemyd brennyng whan ſayde qui eſt miſit ſay chyldren iſrael ſente hit alſo newe worde cauſe newe reherfed holy mayden lyke wordes ſhe whiche fyrſt bryef fruytfull ſentence taught knowe hir ſelf nough ſholde lerne nexte fruytfull ſenten • e aſke lorde ought whiche endeles welle eſſencyall beyng thyſe bryef fruytfull ſentencys may ye knowe creature nought hym ſelf hath vertue beynge cometh god maker creature almyghty god maker al creature hath onely hym ſelf none endeles perfeccyon eſſencyall beynge myght neuer forme make thyng nought yf infynyte vertue eſſencyall beyng hym ſelf wherfore alle euer oure lorde jheſu ſouerayne mayſter taught ſpouſe tho two bryef ſentences reherſed afore thyng ellys ſhe ſholde knowe hir ſelf ſhe lord verayly hir maker depnes hir herte thenne ſhe thus doughter yf thou wilt gete vertu ghoſtely ſtrengthe thou muſte folowe myght myn goodly vertu ouercome power fendes many maner wayes ouercomyng ¶ yet gyue enſample manhede wolde ouercome hym takyng dethe vppon croſſe ye myght taught therby yf ye wolde ouercome ghoſtely enemyes take croſſe dide whiche croſſe ſhall grete refreſſhyng temptacyons yf ye haue mynde paynes ſuffred vpon temptacyons certeyne paynes croſſe may well called refreſſhyng temptacion payne ye ſuffre myn loue lyke ye bee paſſyon nedes ye muſte lyke joye ¶ therfore myn loue doughter ſuffre pacyētly bytter thynges none ſwete thynges doughter none wiſe thou ſhalt ſtronge enough • ſuffre alle thynges pacyently▪ ¶ whan holy mayde hadde herde holy leſſon ſhe foryate nought bare euer quykly mynd euer afterward hadde joye delyte trybulacions ſoo ferforthe noo thynge erthe ſoo grete refreſſhyng paſſiōs trybulacyons ſwete ſufferaunces trybulacions ſhe wyſte well crowne encreſyd bleſſe heuen ¶ tyme kynge salamon oure lorde jheſu cryſte kynge heuen ande erthe hadde armed hys bleſſyd toure maydes ſowle ſwete myghty holſom doctrynes ſuffred enemyes come preue toure yf myght ony waye wyſe deſtroye ¶ kynge babylone oure ghoſtely enmye fende wyth alle hys curſyd companye come byſeged thys bleſſyd toure thorugh ſufferaunce god rounde aboute wyth many wretchid temptacions ¶ fyrſt began aſſayle mayde fleſſhely temptacions oonly tempted thoughtes withinforthe ne ylluſyons fantaſyes ſlepe opyn vyſyons wakynge bothe ſeyeng herynge ſeyng ¶ tempted many maner wyſe takyng vppon hym body eyre▪ ſhame foule fleſſhely ſynne tempted therfore ſhall reherſe theym clene ſowles delectable ¶ holy mayde ouercame ſuche foule deluſyons therfore ſhall reherce whan holy may de perceyned beſy fende brynge ſynne aroſe agaynſte ſelf▪ myghtely punyſſhed body weryng cheyne ſoo moche blode folowed therto ſhe walked thenne ſhe • wonte doo chirche almooſt vſe whiche ſlepe taken awaye yet wolde fende ſece fro bata ••• e hadde begonne toke vppon hym body eyre haue reherſed fore wyth greate nombre horryble companye wyth hym came ſtode byfore holy mayde thought hadde compaſſyon coū ſeylled ſayd wretche tourmenteſt thou thy body ſoo ydell ſhalt thou wynne ſuche tourment peyne weneſt thou thou mayſt contynue therin thyn laſte ende thenne mayſt thou neuer contynue therin warne well yf thou wylt ſlee thy ſelf ſoo better ſeſe grete folye thenne ſoo ſlee thyn owne body yet haſt thou tyme haue ioye worlde thou arte yonge therfore thou mayſt ſonner recouere thyne ſtrengthe thy body agayn ¶ notwythſtondyng thyn grete penaū ce thou haſt doo lyue wymmen doo take huſbond brynge forthe chyldren encrece mankynde yf thy deſyre pleſe god troweſt yu holy wymmen haue weddyd thynke sara rebecca lya rachell weddyd brought forth chyldren yet hooly wymmen wherto haſt thou tabe vppon ſynguler lyf thou mayſt noo wyſe contynue whyles ſuche wordes many lyke fende wyth curſyd companye multeplyed agaynſt prayed euer deuoutlye com̄aunded lyuyng ſpouſe jheſu kepte herte keyes whyles fendes ſtood afore ſhe anſwerde none worde theym thus truſte myn lorde jheſu cryſte myn ſelf worde myght neuer haue alwaye ſhe contynued ſtedfaſtly deuoute prayer afterward ſhe tolde confeſſour mayſter reymound thaughte many conuerſaunt leſſon generall rule whan temptacions aryſen v ſholde neuer dyſpyſe ne make queſtions ſhe ſayd fende ſeketh v falle queſtyons wyth hym truſted ſoo hyely grete ſotelte malyce ſholde ouercome v wyth ſofyſtycall reſons whiche ſholde make queſtyons wyth hym ne anſwere queſtyons ſhall tel enſample ryght chaſt womā hir huſbonde ſholde anſwere ſotelte maundes wonteth make rather bowe awaye hym yf ſhe wolde eſcape ſynne ryght ſo ſowle whiche coniuncte oure lorde chaſte loue ſholde neuer make queſtyons ne anſwere queſtyons fende curſed auout •• er enemye rather tourne deuoute prayer commaunde lorde ſhe conſente ſotell demaū de vertu deuoute prayer ſtedfaſte faythe maye ouercome alle ſotell temptacions fend thus wyſe holy mayde cryſtis ſpouſe ouercome enemye ſoo ceſyd kynde temptacions agaynſt tourned hym another abhomynable kynde temptacions brought afore likeneſſe mē wymmen medlyng togyders fowleſt wyſes myght deuyſed spekyng gyders foule dyſhoneſt wordes ſoo moche curſyd company ranne abonte wyth ȝellyng cryeng ſtere ſuche abhomynable ſynnes ¶ lorde god traueyle hadde ſhe ſowle ſoo conſtreyned ſee thynge ſhe hadde mooſt abhomynacion al ſhe cloſed hir eyen ſtopped hir eren ther yet ſhe hadde another torment hir ſpouſe lorde jheſu wonte vyſyte hir comforte gracyouſly semed tyme ferre hyr nother vyſybly ne vnuyſybly ſhewed hyr helpe ſemed whyche ſhe hadde full grete ſorowe hyr ſowle ſhe ceſſyd hyr grete penaunce euer contynued ther inne deuoute prayer laſt ſhe bethought inſpyracyon holy ghooſt certeyne fleyte whyche ſhe tolde afterward hir confeſſour many eſhe ther ſotell temptacion fende happed ſhe ſayde whyle deuoute feruour ſowle leuyng oure lorde jheſu ſomme certeyne ſynne ellys newe ſotyll temptacyons fende wexyth dull ſlowe whyle brought veray coldeneſſe ſo moche ſomme vnwytty folke conſyderyng ben deſtytute ſo fro ghoſtly comfortes whiche wonte haue leue therfore theyr ghooſtly excercyſe wonte vſe prayer medytacyons redyng holy comynycacyons penaunce doyng wheby made redy ouercome fende deſyred thyng ellys cryſtys knyght ſholde putte waye hys armour whiche wonte ouercome hys enemye wyſe knyght lord jheſu cryſte ſhold thus ſeeth hym ſelf dull ſlouth colde deuocyon rather ſholde contynue hys ghooſtly exercyſe nought make leſſe rather encrece another thynge alſo thys mayde ferned lorde jheſu vſed ſaye hyr ſelf edyfycacyon thou vyle wretchyd creature art thou worthy ony maner comfort lyffe hoſt thou mynde thy ſynnes ſuppoſeſt thou thy ſelf wretchyd ſyn̄er nough troweſt thou thou art eſcaped mercy lord fro euer laſtyng dampnacyon therfore thou ſholdeſt well apayed yu wretche though thou ſuffreddeſt peynes derkenes ſoule dayes thy •• f art thou thanne heuy ſorowfull ſuffre ſuche peynes sythe goddes grace thou ſhalte eſcape endeles peynes wyth cryſt jheſu wythout ony doubte thon ſhalt comforted endeleſly yf thou ſuffre peynes pacyentely whether thou haſt choſen ſerue lorde onely comforte thou mayſt haue hym thys fyf nay conforte thou ſhalte haue hym blyſſe heuen therfore aryſe vp ceſſe thy ghoſtly excercyſe yu haſt vſed rather encrece ther wyth thyſe dartes mekenes holy mayde wounded provide kynge babylonye hyr enemy fende ſtrengthed hyr ſelf gretely wyth ſuche wyſe wordes ſhe knoweleched hir confeſſour mayſter reymond ther ſuche multytude fendes hyr chambre hyr ſemed • ſawe hyr eyen aboute ſtyre hyr foule thoughtes ſynne ſhe fledde hir chambre tyme kepte hyr ſelf chyrche thanne ſhe wonte alle ſhe purſued thyder theyr ſotyll temptacyons yet neuertheleſſe ſhe thought ſhe wolde folowe ſteppes saynt jerome fleenge hydyng hir ſelf dale hylles eſhewyng ſuche abhomynable temptacyons euer whan ſhe came home fro chyrche hyr chambre ſhe founde ſo many multytude fendes inne ſeyenge vnhoneſt wordes doyng abhomynable dedys lecherye hir ſemed rennyng aboute hyder thyder ben paſſyng ſwarme flyes thanne ſhe took hir prayer ſo longe ſhe prayed lorde vnto tyme heuyſom compayne ſwaged ſomwhat fro theyre abhomynable temptacyons whan thyſe wretched temptacyons contynued many dayes gydres tyme whan ſhe come fro chyrche hyr chambre fyll doune prayer ſone ther appyred gladſome beme holy ghooſt opened hyr ſowle ſhe ſholde haue mynde many dayes fore ſhe hadde aſked lord vertue gyfte ſtrengthe doctryne lord gyue hyr gete gyfte vertue ſtrengthe anone ſhe vnderſtode meuynge foule temptacyons fende conceyued ther grete gladneſſe lord gyue hir ſuche ſtrengthe ouercome purpoſed euer afterwarde ſuffre mekely gladdely ſuche heuyſom temptacion maner dyſeaſes loue hyr ſpouſe one fendes bolder thanne ony wycked ſpake holy mayde thys wyſe thynkeſt thou wretche thynkeſt thou euer kepe caytyf lyf knowe well ſhall neuer ceſſe payne heuy thy deth vnto tyme thou conſente v holy mayde anſwerd hauyng minde doctryne whiche oure lorde taught ſeyeng thus haue choſe payne refreſſhyng therfore harde ſuffre theym rather dylectable loue ſauyour longe pleſeth mageſte ſhall ſuffre theym aſſone ſhe hadde ſayde worde anone ſodenlye abhomynable companye fendes vanyſſhed awaye confuſed grete vnſpekable lyht heuen appieryd ſhynned alle chambre lyght apperyd lord jheſu cryſte hynge vpon croſſe whan ſhedde precious blode called holy mayde hym ſayde myn owne doughter katheryn ſeeſt thou ſuffred heuy therfore ſuffre came nerre hyr another maner lykneſſe comforte hyr thanke hyr gloryoꝰ victorye ſhe wonne thenne ſhe thyſe wordes ſaint anthonye ſeyde hym thus lord jheſu thou whan ſowle ſoo vexyd wyth ſuche fowle fylthy temptacions lord ſayde agayne thy ſowle thy herte thenne ſayde ſhe agayn lorde ſauyng alway thy trouthe reuerence thy mageſte maye thou ſholdeſt dwelle ſo foule herte replete wyth ſoo many fylthy thoughtis vnclennes oure lorde ſayde eftſones whether cauſed tho temptacions tho thoughtes thyn herte gladneſſe ſorowe delectacion weylynge anſwerde naye lorde grete ſoro weylynge lord ſayde thē ne cauſe ſorowe weylyng dwellyd thyn herte yf hadde thylke foule thoughte ſholde hadde partyd thyne herte ſo thou ſholdeſt hadde dylectacion theym preſence cauſe theymyſlyked whan thou woldeſt hadde putte theym fro wyth dypleſaunce myghteſt thou woldeſt thou weptyſt ſory thys made preſente wythinforth wyth thyn herte defended thyn enemyes ſuffre wythout forthe troubled moche nedeful ſpedefull thyn helthe whan tyme bataylle fulfylled ended ſente wyth forthe bemys lyght anone derkenes fendes fledde might abyde lyght whiche enfourmed laſt tho peyne full holſom wynne ghoſtely ſtrengthe thou ſholdeſt ſuffre theym paciently longe lykynge ſhyneth beme cauſe thou offredeſ • thy ſelfe hertely ſuffre tho peynes paciently ſowle therfore frely wyth drawe fro ſhewyng preſerce therfore doughter haſt ſoo trewely ouercome vertue thyne thou haſt deſerued grace thenne thou weneſt wherfore fro tyme fortherward ſhall ſhewe famulyerly homely haue doo tyme vyſyon ended ſhe belefte ſo moche plente ſweteneſſe noo penne may wryte ye full belefte herte ſyngulerly amerueylous ſweteneſſe worde lord callyd doughter whan called myn owne doughter katheryne▪ soo ſhe prayed confeſſour mayſter reymoūd whā euer wold calle wold vouche ſauf calle ſame wyſe euyr ſweteneſſe myght therby renewed ſowle fro tyme fortherward oure lorde jheſu ſpouſe wyth ryght homely apperyd ofte tymes whyle hym ſelf allone whyle brought oure ladye bleſſyd moder wyth hym ¶ whyle ſaynt domynyk ther whyle gyders ¶ alſo ſomtyme brought wyth hym marie magdalene saynt johan euaungelyſte saynt poule appoſtle moo ſuche lyked party came hym ſelf allone ſpake wyth homely frende wolde ſpeke wyth moſte homely frende ſoo moche bothe gyders wolde walke vp doune chamber two relygyous men two clerkys ſeyng pſalmes howres gydres ſhe knewe ofte tyme afterward mayſter reymound confeſſour full ferefully merueylous thynge merueylous ſhewyng homely neuer hath herde afore neuertheles maydens ye nede doubte therof yf ye mekely inwardely conſydere depthe goodnes lorde eueryche choſen ſoules gyueth ſomme ſynguier gyfte grace wherof maye haue excellent joye aboue other▪ heythe ſouereygne magnyfycence apperyd ſayntes onys eueryche hym ſelfe ſomme ſynguler grace ryght ſene daye yt one man lyke another hathe ſomme maner dyfference ryght ſoo eueri ſaynte heuen hath ſomme dyfferē ce ſom̄e ſynguler grace gyuen god fro therfore merueylle gretely though ſomme ſpeciall grace bee ſeyde one founde therof cauſe haue reherſyd ſeynge ther pſalmes ſhall tell maydens holy maide lerned rede techyng man woman lerned ſhe neuer tolde one hir cōfeſſoure mayſter reymond ſhe hadde deſired kunne hyr mattyns therefore tyme ſhe prayed one hyr ſuſters gete b c teche knowe lettres ſhe hadde traueylled ſore many wekes gydres dyde ſpende tyme aboutes knowe lettres myght come therto bethought complayne oure lorde heuēly mayſter myſpendyng tyme prayeng hym wolde voucheſauf teche yf lykynge hym ſpendefull ſoo kunne rede ellys lorde thy wylle done inow yf lykyng ye ſymple lyuyng ſpende tyme holy medytacions merueylous thynge hadde ſoo ſoone endeth prayer ſhe coude rede lyuelye pſalmes redely ſhe hadde ben ony kunnyng clerke whan confeſſour perceyued gretely aſtonyed moche ſhe coude ſpelle ne knowe vnnethe noo lettre whiche ordeyned god ſuppoſed merueyllous token mayde gate bokes goddes ſeruyſe ſaye ther matyns howrys theri • amonge verſes ſhe ſayde ſhe marked verſe euery houre begynneth wyth deus adiutorium meum intende • n̄e adadiuuandum feſtina kept verſe ſpecially mynde lyues ende ofte tymes ſhe wolde reherce yt soone ſhe encreſyd ſoule merueylouſly perfeccion contemplacion thenne ceſſyd lytyll vocall prayer bycauſe ſhe ſoo ofte tymes rauyſſhed heythe contemplacion ſoo ferforth cauſe ſuche ofte rauyſſhyng ſhe myght ofte tymes perfourme ne make ende pater noſter ſowle rauyſſhed fro outward wyttes ſhall declare afterward helpe god thus ſhall make ende chapytre conteyned therin confeſſur ſom̄e knowleche pryuely ſomme relacion ſhe tolde hadde tolde another ſelf edyfycaciō ¶ merueylous diſponſacyon wyth whiche ſhe weddyd faythe lorde wyth rynge capitulum duodecium holy mayde encrecyd profyted day daye grace vertu came holy deſyre ſowle praye lord gyue perfyte degre feyth whiche fayth ſhe myght able hym • oythouten ony chaungynge thenne ſhe fore anone forthe ſhe prayed lord wolde voucheſauf encrece fayth make ſo perfyte ſhold neuer hurte • ne throwe doune violence ony maner aduerſarye ouce lorde anſwerd wyſe ſhall dyſpouſe faythe yet ſhe prayed ſame often tymes aftyrward euer hadde ſame anſwere lorde agayn laſte happened lytyll fore begynnyng lente dayes ye peple made ende eting offleſſhe manere made veyne ydil feſtys ſeruyng wombe▪ thys holy mayde cloſid lord apperid ſayde cauſe thou haſt putt awaye flelde maner nf vanytes etyng ſleſſhe thyſe dayes loue▪ ſette dylectacion thyn herte fully tyme aboute namely ſame hous thou dwelleſt maken feſtys ioyen therin ſhall therfore make ſolempne feſte diſpouſacion betwene ſowle ſo behyte ſhal diſpouſe faith lord ſoo ſoone ſayde wordes lady gloryous moder hys bleſſyd euangelyſte ſaynt johan gloryous appoſtle ſaynt poule ſaynt domynyke fader relygion apperyd wyth theym dauyd prophete brengyng honde ſauter muſyke ¶ fyrſt bleſſyd lady goddes moder came holy mayde toke honde holi honde ſtret chyng fyngers ſone prayleng hym wolde voncheſuf wedde mayde hym feythe whiche deuoute axynge oure lorde graunted brought forth rynge arayed rounde aboute wyth foure precious margarete ſtones ouer parte rynge encloſyd ryght fayre dyamant ſtone rynge put holy honde vppon fyngre maydens ryght honde ſeyeng thus loo dyſpouſe thy maker thy ſauyour faith whiche diſpoſycion ſhall confermed kept vndefouled vnto tyme yu ſhalt halowe euerlaſtynge weddyng wyth bleſſe heuen therefore douhter fro tyme fortherwarde worke myghtely put awaye maner doubte thou arte armed ſtrengthe feith ouercome therby thyn aduerſaryes thus gracioꝰ viſiō ceſſyd euer afterward▪ rynge bylefte vp holi maydes fynger folkes ſyht owne ſyght ſhe knewe many tymes ofte confeſſour maiſter reymound wyth grete drede fere ſhe ſawe euer rynge vppon fyngre neuer tyme ſhe ſawe loo maydens ryht ſaynt katheryn martyr virgyn quene baptym dyſpouſed lorde ye legende maketh mē cion ryght ye maye conſydre holy mayde katheryn ſo many victoryes temptacions fleſſhe ſolemply dyſpouſed ſame lorde ye conſydre coudycyons rynge ye ſhall • welle ſee tokene acordeth betokeneth axed ſtedfaſte feythe ſtrenger dyamaunt ſtone wythſton dyth maner hardeneſſe perſyth hardeſt thynge ſtone ſelf broke onely blode goote ryght ſoo ſtronge feythfull herte wythſtondeth ouercometh wyth ſtrenthe alle maner aduerſyte mynde cryſtys precious blood whiche called holy wryte goote whiche precious blode ſhadde vpon croſſe mankynde ſtroge herte lentyd al broſte four precious margarete ſtonys rynge betokenyth noo thynge elli foure purytres clenes yt whiche holy mayde clennes hyr entente clennes hyr thouȝt clennes hyr ſpeche clennes hir workynge alle thyſe ſhall declared grace god largely aftyrwarde ſuppoſo thys dyſpouſacion̄ thynge ellys confirmacioū godis grace token thys gracyous confyrmacion̄ ye rynge whiche apperid none cauſe ſhe ſhold fere ne drede delyuer owte wretched worlde prayer helpe ſpecial grace god hadde endowed wyth one ye princypall cauſes holy doctours ye almyghty god voucheſauf ſynguler preuylege ſhewe ſom̄e ben pleſaunt hym eſtate grace wycked world worſhyppe entent ſende fyght wyth wycked world worſhyppe holy name helthe ſoules dyde appoſtlis wytſondaye whiche token ſpecyal tokenes grace ryght ſoo hooly mayde aboue condycion alle wymmen tyme ſhe thus confermed • grace ſhe ſente openli wourſhyppe god procure helthe ſowles ſhall bee declared helpe god afterward openly therfore trowe ſhe toke lorde token confyrmaciō grace ſhe ſholde boldely myghtely doo execucion lorde commaunded thus ſhall make ende chapytre fyrſt parte legende hooly mayde ſaynt katheryn scene worſhip holy trynyte helthe ſowles regnaute ſemper oīꝰ ſcis domino noſtro iheſu criſto quī cum patre almo que ſpūiſcō viuit et regnat deus per oīa ſecula ſeculorum amen ¶ begynneth ſecond partye whiche ſhewed conuerſacion holy mayde men gyftes whiche ſhe hadde receyued oure lorde pryuyly encloſed wythin herſelf openly ſhewed worlde fyrſt oure lorde bad ſhe ſholde conuerſaunt amonges men capitulum prymum • tyme holy mayde deſpouſed reherſed afore lorde began drawe litill lytyll conuerſacion men full mennerly meſurably wythdrawe vtterly fro dyuyne preſence rather moche longeth meſure perfection encreſe ſhall declared openly afterward therfore tyme whan appyred hadde taughte kyngdom heuen ſhewed many myſteryes alſo ſeye pſalmes houres dyuyne ſeruī ce reherſed afore forthwith bad ſhe ſholde go doune mete moders houſholde afterward ſhe ſholde come agayn whan holy mayde herde ſhe ſobbyd wepte fyll doune feete ſorowe fayde hym thyſe wordes ſwete iheſu lorde putteſt yu awaye fro yf haue offendyd diſpleſyd mayſter loo lord myn body thyn foot punyſſhe ſhal gladly helpe therto ſuffre good lord punyſſhed wyth ſo • ſharpe ſoo hard payne departed ony maner wiſe fro thin bliſſed preſence haue doo wyth mete haue mete knewe whether receyueth anone lyf bodely mete ghoſtely mete lorde thou knoweſt well haue fledde conuerſacion men myght ſonner fynde ſythe haue founde mercy graciouſly thou haſte ſhewed though vnworthy ſholde nowe forſake precious treſour put conuerſacion men eftſones ſoo ben founde reprobable faythe nay lord ſuffer ſoo thyne infynyte goodnes whā ſhe thus longe wepte weyled wyth ſwete ſobbyng wordes oure lorde ſayde ſuffre dere doughter full ſemely thou ſhodeſte fulfylle maner vertu fruytfull thyn ſelf alſo myn ſpecyall grace myn entent dyſceuere departe ony maner wyſe rather ſhall haue ſtrenger medytacions neyghbours charyte kneweſt thou well thiſe two thynges ſcondeth perfection myn commaundementys loue god loue thyn neyghbour wil therfore thou wyll fulfylle verof thyſe two preceptis thou may go heuen wyth one wynge wyth tweyne haue doughter thin yonge age thou haſt hyther yele loue helthe ſowles hathe encreſyd ſo moche thyn yonge age thou purpoſed feyne aman cauſe thou myghteſt ſonner receyued amonge order fryer prechours ſtraunge contrees yu ſholdeſt knowen ſoo prouffyte helthe mennys ſoules yt ſynguler loue thou haddeſt myn ſeruaunt domynyk thou deſyreſt wyth grete honour habyte thou haſt receyued whiche domynyk pryncypally helthe ſoules ordeyned order merueyleſt thou wey leſt thou ſoo yf brynge thou haſt ſoo longe deſyred wyth thyſe wordes lord holi maide gretely comforted ſayde vnto hym lyke gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn marie ſayde gabriel ſuche wordes qn̄o fit iſtud good lord wyſe maner may done lord ſayde agayn myn goodnes ſhal dyſpoſe ordeyne then̄e ſhe good dyſcyple trewe folower mayſter cryſte iheſu ſayde lord thyn wyl done thynges derkenes thou art lyght ſhe nought thou art ought ſhe vnwis thou art endeles wyſdom ye fader yet praye lord maner wyſe may yu ſeyſte wretche ſoo freell ſhold ſoo profytable mannys ſoule thou knoweſt well lord men ſetten lytyll ſtore woman wordes ſpeke ye neuer ſo vertuouſly ſemely ne lyueſt thou wymmen ſholde conuerſaunt amonges men lorde anſwerd maner gabryell anſwerd oure gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn mary ſayd none word cometh fro goddes mouthe vnpoſſyble hym done whiche hathe made mankynde bothe man woman ſhappe euery eyther wyl enſpyre myn grace al one man woman necke agayn kynde cryeng one maydes ſuſters ſhe ſholde ceſe ſhe lefte tyme ſpyryte reſtoryd agayne bodely wyttys ſhe felte necke ſoo ſore thought ſmyten wyth many grete ſtrokys hooly mayde tolde afterward confeſſour maiſter reymoū de yf moder hadde put neuer ſo lytyll ſtrengthe ſhe dyde ryghting necke ſhe aboute▪ ſhe ſhold haue broken necke ſuche maner paſſyng body ſowle holy mayde ofte tymes rauyſſhyng▪ ſo whyle vyolens ſpyryte body lefte vp fro erthe marie magdalene tyme rauyſſhyng ſhall declared afterward openly ¶ ſhall tell myracle befyll begynnynge rauyſſhyng befyl tyme whan hooly mayde tournyd ſpete broche wyth fleſſhe fyre hote brenning cole ſowle enflam̄ed brente mene whyle wyth fyre holy ghoſte anone ſhe rauyſſhed fro bodely wyttes ſeaſyng ye tyme tournyng ſpytte whā brother wyf whiche callyd lyſa perceyued knowyng condycions holy mayde▪ ſhe toke ſpytte honde lete alone whan mete ynow▪ alſo folke ſuppyd yet ſhe bylefte ſarauyſſhyng thenne lyſa bethought abyde vpon vnto tyme ſhe hadde doo brought huſbond bedde chyldren came agayn aſpye ſhe dyde founde falle doun hote brennyng cole wyth lyſa weyled cryed ſayde ala ala katheryn alle brennyd ran anone pullyd fyre founde clothes nothyng hurt ne brente ne hauynge noo maner taſtyng fyre ne yet ouer bylefte nomaner aſſhes vpon clothes loo perceyue ye maydens vertu goſtely fyre wythin maydes ſowle who myght ſtrengthe outward naturall fyre vtterly wytdrawe see ye myracle chyldren whiche caſte ouen brent thenne renewed holy mayde myracle onys ſhewed ofte tymes ¶ onys befyll ſhe chyrche fryer whan ſhe ſoo rauyſſhed ſhe bowed hede doune pyler mene whyle whiche pyller certeyne ymages dyuerſe ſayntes reuerens whiche ſayntes man ſtyked vp waxe candell brennyng whiche candell fyll doune vppon thys holy maydes hede tyme rauyſſhyng ſoo brennyd vppon hede tyme candell waſted ſoo ſhe harme merueylous thynge wounderfull ye candell brennyd vpon hede till waſted hurte nothynge kerchies ¶ whan candell brente quenchyd vpon hede though hadde quenchyd vpon ſtone vppon erthe ¶ myracle bare wytneſſe many ſuſters ſawe tolde afterward confeſſour mayſter reymound one ſuſters whiche ſawe called lyſa another alyxa thyrde franciſca yet beſyde befyll lyke vnto ſame dyuerſe place worlde ſhe came namely whan ſhe aboute edefye men̄ys ſowles vertu fend malyce gretely ſtered agaynſt ſufferaūce god ſoo ferforth preſence many goddes ſeruauntes kaſt fyre whyles aboute drawe wyth wepyng weylyng ſhe ſmyled vpon theym come fyre ſelfe nothynge hurte neyther body ne clothes thenne ſhe ſayde theym ſtode aboute beeth thynge aferde myn ghoſtely enemye fende hath doo myracle recordeth dyuerſe ſawe mayſter reymound confeſſour ¶ another tyme alſo chambre bi beddes ſyde erthen panne wyth brennynge cole whiche brennyng cole enuyous fend caſte wyth ſuche ſtrengthe hede fyrſt fyll fyre ſo panne braſte vyolence ſtroke yet hed noo wyſe hurte aroſe vp ſayde wyth ſmilyng deuoute woman whiche callyd gabryell loo malycions enemye werketh lyke ride vitas patrum woman callyd infracia therfore none merueyle though lord ſuffer fende werke ſuche thynges derlynges choſen chyldren ſythen ſo ſuffred hym werke harde thinges perſone whā ſuffred hym ſette hym vpon pynacle temple vppon hye hylle ¶ tus ſuche merueylous thynges lord wrought merueylouſly hys mayden katheryn ſoo ſhe encreſyd grace euery daye perfection moche loue bothe rote cauſe werkys charytable werkisof neybours paſſed werkys charytable werkys double wyſe bothe body ſoule ¶ fyrſt ſhall telle dedis charyte mercy ſhe dyde neyghbours ſyke body afterward dedes charyte mercy ſhe dyde theym ſeke ſowle nexte chapytre ſhal declare openly dyuerſe merueylys lorde ſhewed helyng poure folke alſo merueylous charyte ſhe ſhewed nemptis hem ſeke body wytneſſe chapytre reherſed wythin ſame chapyter ¶ woundres whiche ſhe dyde helthe comforte neceſſyte theym poure nedy capytulum iij whan holy mayde katherin perceyued yt mylder ſhe neyghbours gracyous ſhe ſyghte ſpouſe iheſu ſhe applyed euer afterward ſocour helpe theym nede wyth herte largely ¶ cauſe ſhe wolde nothynge haue owne owne owne poſſeſſion▪ ryght relygyous woman hadde ordeyned owne herte kepe iij pryncipall vowes relygyon reherſed afore fyrſt party leſt ſhe ſholde founde gylty withdrawynge mennys good againſt ye hauer ſhe wente fader beſoughte hym mekely lowely wolde gyue leue gyue almeſſe conſcyence • ore folke goodis god gyue hym houſholde whiche fader graunted frely moche knowe well ſhe folowynge perfyghtly ſteppes graunted oonly thus pryuyte bytwene theym bothe alſo afterward houſholde gaue commaundemente noo body ſholde lette dere doughter gyue almeſſe ſuche goodes lord hadde gyue hym houſholde though ſhe wolde gyue poure folke euer hadde hys houſholde aſſone ſhe hadde lycence▪ ſhe began departe goodes fader poure folke neuertheleſſe moche ſhe lyued wyth gyfte dyſcrecion ſhe departed good alle wolde aſke theym ſhe knewe nede folke alle though aſked amonge nedy folke came two knowleched many poure nedy houſholders lytyll beſyde cyte gene grete nede ſore aſhamed aſke tyme ſhe knewe ſhe forgate ſhe aroſe vp erly ye morowe ſaynt nycholas dyde bare ſholders home houſes bothe wyne oyle thynges nedefull god wolde whan ſhe came ſhe founde dory opē ſhe put wythin dores ſhe brought drewe dore fledpreuyly waye ¶ befyll tyme ſhe ſeke body ſoo fro ſole fote toppe hede body ſwollen ſhe myght aryſe vp bedde ne ſtonde fete▪ ſhe herde ſaye poure wydowe lytyll beſyde whiche grete hunger greate nede wyth ſones doughters compaſſyon ſhe hadde poure woman chyldren nexte nyght ſhe prayed oure lorde wolde vocheſauf gyue ſoo moche ſtrengthe tyme yt ſhe myght goo ſo oour poure woman anone ſhe aroos vp erly vpon morowe fylled ſacke faders grete veſſell flacat wyne another veſſell wyth oyle ſhe myght euer fynde beſyde forth whiche myght bee neceſſarye mannys lyuelood thyſe ſhe kept chābre eueryche thyſe berdem ynow alone yet ſhe bare onys wedowes hous ſomme therof ſhe truſſed vpon ſholders ſomme vp ryght arme ſomme vp lift arme ſomme therof bonnden onder gyrdell myracle heuy ynouht bere eueryche hym ſelf ſhe bare alle onys eſely without ony peyne greuaū ec knowleche ward bothe confeſſour mayſter reymoūd fryer berdom wayde nomore thought ſhe hadde lifte vp lytyll waſe ſtrawe yet trouthe yf hadde trewely wayed ſholde haue wayed hondred pound weyte aboute er comyn bell cyte roungen erly morowe lefull neuer one walke cyte aft tyme ronge holy mayde waited well tyme toke journeye wyth burthen ſhe yonge forbolnyd byſekenes yet ſhe ranne poure wydowed hous ſo faſte though ſhe hadde felt nothynge paynes ne burthen whā ſhe came nyghe poure wydowes hous byrthen waxit heuy greuo • bere ſoo ſemed ſhe myght bere paas whan ſhe perceyued ſhe vnderſtoode anone yt oure lordes wyll prayed deuoutly wyth truſte wolde voucheſaufe eſe anone ſhe eſyd byrthen came poure wydowes hous founde dore half open preuyly ſhe coude ſhe drewe byrthen wythin dore yet made ſuche noyſe woke wydowe ſhe fledde ſhe myght ſekenes full ferre ſekenes encreſyd ordeynaunce god vnnethes ſhe myghte remeue waye wherfore ſhe ſpak lord wyth wei lyng chere maner ſmylyng chere ſayde good lord haſt thou ſo dyſceyued good ſhame thy wyll myn foly bee pupplyſſhed folke aboute haſt thou forgete thy mercy yu haſte ſhewed thyn vnwourthy▪ praye lord yelde myn ſtrengthe maye come home myn chambre tyme ſhe ſpake thus thyſe wordes lyke thyſe enforced ſtrengthed ſelf ſhe myght go forthe ſeyeng owne body thus thou mooſt nedes forthe though thou ſholdeſte deye waye therfore goo forth wyth goynge wyth crepyng forth ſhe wēt lytyll ſoo fer poure wedowe aroſe vp aſpyed habyte dyd benefet ¶ oure lord thenne conſydered ſhe gretely tourmentyd goyng reſtoryd agayne ſtrengthe ſhe hadde afore ſoo perfyghtely wyth grete hardynes ſhe came home er thenne lyght daye laye doune bedde ryght feble ſhe dyde thus oure lorde touched touched ſekeneſſe hym lyked loo maydens ye maye ſee myracles ſaint nycholas renewed holy mayde myracle many myracles ſhall procede forth ſhewe vertuous lyuyng ſaynt martyn lord ſhewed hym ¶ befyll tyme whan holy mayde chyrche freyers came poure man aſked ſomme helpe loue god holy mayde perceyued wel ſhe hadde nothynge ſhe myght gyue hī ſhe wonte neyther golde ne ſyluer ſhe prayed hym wolde abyde whyle tyll ſhe came home gladly ſhe wolde plenteuouſly gyue almes ſuche thynges yt ſhe hadde home houſhold thenne ye poure man ſade yf thou haue ony thyng gyue praye gyue may abyde ſo long ſuppoſe another yt apperyd poure man lykenes ſemed holy mayde ſhe ſholde goo fro ſomwhat ſhe bethought ſhe myght gyue hym fulfylle nede anone came mynde lytyll ſyluer croſe hynghe bodyes yt whiche tyme ſhe honde ſhe pulled away lytyll croſſe gaue gladly poure man whan poure man croſſe wente awaye fro gladly aſked nomore almes ye day none mā though come croſſe alone nexte nyght folowyng whan holy mayde prayed ſhe wounte almyghty god oure ſauyour apperyd hauyng ſame lytyll croſſe bleſſyd honde arayed wyth mani precious ſtones ſayde doughter knoweſt thou croſſe mayde anſwerde hym ſayde ſhe knewe well ſhe ſayde ſoo fayre araied whā ſhe lord ſayde yeſterday thou gaueſt gladly wyth grete charyte loue whiche loue charyte betokeneth thyſe precious ſtones therfore behote daye dome afore alle ye companye angel men ſhall ſhewe encrece thy ioye ſhall hede ne ſuffre hyd dedes mercy ben doo wyth lorde ceſyd aperycion ſhe thanked ourlord euer ſteryd doo ſuche almeſſe well proued afterward another daye alſo befyll whan deuyn ſeruice doo fryer tyme peple goo chyrche ſhe bylefte behynde alone wyth one ſuſters praye▪ ſhe came dounward fro chapell whiche ordeyned ſuſters penaunce oure lord apperyd lykeneſſe poure pylgrym age ſemed ij iij thyrty yere half naked aſked ſhe wolde gyue hym clothes loue god theen̄e ſhe tyme ſteryd doo dedes mercy euer ſhe ſhe prayed poure man wolde abyde whyle vnto tyme ſhe came doune agayn fro chapell thenne ſhe wolde helpe hym ſomme clothes wente vp agayn chapell dyde herk ertyll vnder whiche kertell ſhe wered nexte body cote wythout ſleues gaue wyth greate gladnes poure man tyme poure receyued aſked ſayde good lady praye ſythe ye haue gyue wollen clothe gyue lynen clothes nexte myn body thenne ſhe ſayde hym come thou ſhalt houe gladly ſhe went fore hir ſpouſe theſu vnknowyng pylgryme lykenes folowed whan ſhe came home ſhe went thyder lynen clothes fader brother layen brought bothe ſherte lynen clothes toke gladly poure pylgrym yet whan poure man hadde receyued aſked prayed ſhe wolde gyue hym ſleues kertyll couer armes ¶ wyth ſhe wente nothynge heuy crawyng gladly ſought aboute ſleues laſte ſhe founde newe cote mayden ſeruaūt hous hauyng hangyng vpon perche whiche neuer werid ther ſhe toke awaye ſleues toke gladly poure man yet aſked ſayde lady thou haſt clothed thanke who loue yu haſt doo yet haue felawe lyeng hoſpytall beſyde whiche nedeth gretely clothes ye wyll ſende hym ony clothes ſhall bere hym byhalue full gladly yet hooly mayde multyplyeng aſkynge neuer weryer rather feruent almes largely thought hyr ſhe mygth haue clothe clothe wyth nedy man yt lyeth hooſpytall thenne fyll hyr mynde meyne hou ſolde ryght lothe geuen almes take hyr fadre allone therfor ye ſhytte vp alle clothes vnder lok keye leſt ſhe ſholde fynde gyue almes ouermore ſhe conſydered dyſcretely ſhe take nogh awaye mayden ſeruaūt houſholde therfore ſhe wolde take awaye nomore hyres cauſe ſhe nedy hyr ſelfe thanne ſhe dyſputed wyth hyr ſelf whrther ſhe ſholde gyue hym hyr owne cote cauſe ſhe hadde noo moo one charyte ſayde yes hone ſte ſayd nay atte laſt charyte oueroo honeſte ſay charyte longeth ſowle ouercome honeſte whiche hadde compaſſyon vpon body thought yf pour man ſhold go awaye wythout ſomme clothe ſhold ſlaunderous yf ſhe gyuen hyr owne coote goo naked ſholde ſhe hadde ſlandred ſowles who ſoules ſhe ought loue body therfore hir ſemed ſowles ſhold ſlaundred wyſe temporall almes thanne ſhe anſwered poure man thus trewely dere frende yf honeſt lefull gyue cote thou ſholdeſt haue gladdely cauſe haue moo ſemely ſholde gyue awaye thys therfore praye holde excuſed gladdely wolde gyue yf hadde ony moo thenne poure man ſmyled vpon hyr ſayd well lady ſee well yf thou haddeſt moo thou woldeſt gladdely gyue therfore thanke fare well whanne borned fro hir holy mayde perceyued certeyn ſygnes ſholde whiche wonte appere hir often tymes conuerſaunt wyth hyr ſhe manere doubte hyr herte brenned loue neuertheleſſe moche ſhe helde hir ſelf comyne occupacyon houſholde ſhe wonte next nyght ſuyng lord jheſu cryſte appered hyr ſhe prayed lykenes poure man holdyng hys honde cote holy mayde gaf hym arayed wyth clere ſhynyng precyous ſtones ſayd hyr thus dere doughter knoweſt thou dote ſhe anſwered ſayd yes ſhe gaf ſo arrayed whome lord ſayd ageyne thou gaueſt yeſter daye cote ſo frely ſo charytable voyded awaye fro peyne colde therfore ſhall gyue cote whiche ſhall inuyſyble men ſhall ſenſyble myn holy body ſhall take hyue whiche bothe thy body thy ſowle may keuered kepte noyous colde vnto tyme yt ſhall arayed ioye wythout ende fore ſayntes angel anone forth wyth toke clothe ſangueyne colour wyth hys holy hondes wounde ſyde ſhynyng alle aboute quantyte meſure maydens bodye wyth arayed hyr wyth hys owne holy hondes ſayd thys clothe gyue whyle thou dwelleſt erthe token thy clothe ioye thou ſhalt arayed wythin heuen thus vyſyon ceſſyd holy mayde hadde ſoo grete grace receyuyng ghoſtly gyfte onely hir ſowle alſo hir body fro houre hyr endyng daye ſhe neded neuer moo clothes wynter thanne ſomer wedder neuer ſo colde ſhe vſed mo clothes cote kertell euer afterward ſhe ſemed ſhe felte ghoſtly cote vpon hyr whiche lord gaf hir cauſe ſhe felte colde see ye maydens worthynes holy mayde folowed saynt nycholas gyuyng atmeſpryuely folowed ſaynt martyn gyuyng hyr owne clothes whiche lord allowed hys holy apperyng thys bleſſyd mayde gaf hyr ſenſyble euerlaſtyng token fele erthe pleſaūt almes dedes ben hym ſemeth whan lorde ſayd thys holy mayde wolde ſhe hyr lytell croſſe daye dome whiche ſhe gaue almes alſo wolde araye hyr wyth clothe ioye heuen thyng ellys ſikernes endeles helthe therto excellent ioye blyſſe hir mede therfore maydens ſett lytell ſuche reuelacyons ſuche tokenes ſykerneſſe endeles helthe onely cauſeth ſo grete ioye ſo grete comforte ſowle impoſſyble tongue tell penne wryte foloweth ſuche ſykerneſſe ioye trowe ye ſowle trewely encrece vertue pacyence ſtrengthe temperaunce beſyneſſe delygence kepyng hyr ſelf holy werkes feyth hope charytr ſuche vertues harde ſuche ſoule fore ben made ſuche comfort ryght eſye loo grace ſuche predeſtynacyon notefyed clene ſowle wercheth another tyme alſo befyll thys holy mayde fulfylled wyth compaſſyon perceyued ther man whiche made pore wylfully goddes loue lacked mete wherfore ſhe toke preuely lynnen bagge fylled wyth egges bare wyth hyr preuely vnder hyr • oote refreſſhe wyth poure man whan ſhe mette wyth came place poure • dwellyd entred fyrſt chyrche beſyde praye whan ſhe entred ſhe bethought lord ſo inwardly anoue ſpiryte rauyſſhed ſoo ſhe fully tyme wythdrawe hyr outwarde wyttys reherſed afore whanne ſhe thus rauyſſhed happed ſodeynly body bowed pyler caſuelly ſyde egges ſo ſhe lened fully vpon bagge wyth eggeſ thanne ther ſame bagge goten fore thymbyll tayllours ſowen wyth whiche thymbyll broken thre partyes burthon hir body eyren charyte hyd hole noo partye broken thys meruayllous thyng eyren hole thymbyll coper broke ſo lorde ſhewed hys myracle charytable eyren lord ſhewed helpe holy mayde nedy folke alſo ſhewed hys myracle hyr werkes godhede declare openly ſhall tell meruaylles thyng whiche meruayll wytnes bothe men wōman aboute nombre xx maydens faders houſholde moder lapa tolde mayſter reymond hir doughters confeſſour tyme hir doughter thys holy mayde leue hyr fad gyue almes befylle meyne houſholde dronke amonges certeyn veſſell wyne ſo remenaūt whiche lefte freſſhe gyue poure men aſmoche ſhe cuſtome gyue beſte goddes loue went hyr next veſſell wyne beſyde hyr faders ſeller tamed poure folke gaf largely ther euery day neded many dayes gyder aſpyed meyne laſt whan fyrſt veſſell done boteler mynyſtred drynke meyne veſſell whyche holy mayde tamed yet holy mayde left therfore alwaye ſhe gaue ther poure folke ye meyne dronke largely ſhe gaue poure folke aſpyed ne wyne neuer vnfreſſher ne neuer laſſe veſſell allewaye kepte eſtate bothe fulneſſe freſſheneſſe alle meyne houſholde gretely meruaylled ther veſſell contynued ſo folke therfore ſhe gaue ther largely pour folke openly meyne myght ſee yet ſemed neuer leſſe veſſell moneth paſſyd began entre yet wyne contynued euer lyke freſſhe lyke full dyd fyrſte tyme grape rype make newe wyne whenne g • ape rype veſſellys ordeyned fylled wyth newe wyne mayſter wyne bad commaūded veſſell whiche cōtynued ſo long wyth olde wyne ſholde emptyed fyllyd newe wyne one ſeruaūtes made ordynaūce empte veſſell fyllyng botellys yet ſemed neuer leſſe atte laſte veſſell vndone gawgid knowe ther lefte veſſell founde drye though ther wyne ther inne many monthes afore thenne houſholde amexuaylled ye myracle thenne habundaunce wyne afore loo maydens myracle lord ſhewed gyuyng almes dede holy mayde katheryne whiche myracle openly afterward knowen cyte sene thus endeth chapytre wytteneſſe thys mater conteyned thys chapytre ben reherſed thys chapytre ¶ meruayllous dedys whiche ſhe dyd lowely beſy ſeruyſe ſyke capitulum iiij thys holy mayde meruayllous compaſſyon hyr ſoule poure folke nedy yet ſhe hadde excellent meruayllous pyte ſeke folk whiche pyte ſhe hadde ſhe wroughte many wonder thynges ſhall rerce grace god edyfycacyon theym whiche ſhall rede thys holy legende though ſeme ſomme incredyble yet ſhall leue therfore cyte sene ther full poure womman ſyke nede wantyng temporall gooddes ſhe conſtreyned lygge hoſpytak ſame cyte ſhe ſuppoſed haue fynde remedye hyr ſyknes ſhe myght haue hyr ſelf happed thanne ſhe receyued poure hoſpytall ſame cyte whiche hoſpytall vnnethe ſhe myght haue ſhe nedyd hyr ſykeneſſe encrecyd ſo hyghely ſhe lepre tho • ugh hyr body thenne euer wyth inne hoſpytall eſhewed hir te dyſpoſed ſhe ſholde ſente ſpytellhous wythout toune whyche ordeyned lazaros abyde amonges whanne thys holy mayde perceyued thys ſhe wente full owne perſone conſyderyng ſame leprous womman hir ſpouſt jheſu hyr ghooſtly eye therfore ſhe ſerued beſely dylygentely mekely thys holy mayde ſerued hyr prude vnkynde ſeek womman ageynſt hyr ſo ofte euery day thys holy mayde ſhe began chyde hir whanne ſhe ſerued hyr pleſaunce befyll whyle thys holy mayde longe chyrche contynued ſomtyme longer thenne ſomtyme cauſe ofte tyme ſhe taryed fro ſeek wōman whan ſhe came late ſeek wōman ſhe wolde chyde hyr ſhappely ſayde hyr ſoornfully many ſuche heuy wordes lady quene welcome haue ye ben ſo longe lady quene ye grete lady ſo long haue ben frerys comforted hyr lowely mekely ſhe wolde hyr owne moder ſeynge hyr ryght thus good moder goddes loue dyſpleaſed wyth though haue longe ſhall mende thyng anone ſhe hyd hyr faſt made fyre ordeyned beſyly hyr mete neceſſaryes ſhe wolde hyr owne moder ſoo ſeke womman hyr vnpacyence meruaylled hir pacyence thys rebukynge contynued longe tyme yet holy mayde neuer wery hyr ſeruyſe rather contynued many folk meruayll therof hyr owne mod lapa gretely troubled wyth al cryed vpon hyr ſhe ſholde leue minyſtracion leſt ſhe lepre ye ſeke womā oftymes ſhe ſayd hir doughter wote well thou ſhalt leper yf bothe fayrenes fylthes euery ſoule preſent afore thy bodely wittes afore tyme haue perceyued condycions bodyes ryght ſo tyme forward thyn ghoſtely wyttes ſholde perceyue conſydere condition ſpyrytes tho whilche ben preſented alſo who helpe thou ſhalt praye though neuer preſented thy bodely ſyght ¶ grace gyfte euer ward ſoo ſpedefull holy mayde fro tyme forward ſhe perceiued clerly qualytes dedes▪ kely treſpas ſeke ſuſter done agaynſt confeſſour afterward enquyred ſothe odyous cryme ſuſters ye whiche knewe thē well ynow ferthermore cōfyrmacion thyſe thynges benreherſed fore maiſter reymound cō feſſour recordeth yt ofte tymes ſpeker bytwene pope gregori xj ſhe ytaly coude vnd ſtonde none latyn pope gregorye coude vnderſtonde none ytaly therfore mayſter reymound confeſſour coude bothe felawes founde ſothe e ncombred wyth wretched ſynnes whiche ſynnes cō tynued wythouten repentaunce another tyme alſo ſhe ſpake wyth woman ye whiche woman ſemed honeſt womā ſoth ſhe concubyne man anſwerd ſayde fader ſyker ye hadde felt ſtynche ſynne felte ye wolde haue caſte oute alle body ſqweymuſnes loo maydens thyſe enſamples haue ſett ye ſholde knowe excellent gyftes grace lord gaue hooly mayde cauſe meke lyuyng ¶ ouermore ghooſtely enemye fend perceyuyng hooly mayde wan grete vertues ſeruyce ſhe dede ſeke folke thought ſomme maner wylle wythdrawe fro holy beſynes yet myght aboute lette ſhe encreſyd vertuouſly occupacion ¶ befyl tyme one ſuſters penaunce whyche called maner countree andred andred touched bi ſuffraū ce oure lorde wyth greuous infyrmyte thyſe hadde vppon breſt ſore whiche called cancer fretid fleſſhe rounde aboute ſoo corrupte myght none come nyghe ſtynche yf hylde noſe ſoo fewe none myghte ſuffre come nyghe ¶ whanne hooly mayde perceyued ſhe vnderſtoode oure lord receyued ſeke ſuſter kepyng thenne anone ſhe came wyth glad ſhe comforted ſhe ſerued gladly laſte ende ſekenes ſeke ſuſter toke ſeruyce freely moche ſhe conſydered forſoke holy mayde lefte thynge vndo yt longyng ſeke ſuſter encreſyd neuer abhomynable ſtynche neuer ſo moche ſtode opened wounde waſſhed wepte coueryd it▪ yet neuer ſhe hyldeth ſhe noſe noo ſtynche ne ſhewed none token lothſomnes ne neuer heuy ne wroth ſeruyce ne wery gladli dyd dilygēt ſeruyce ſoo ſeke ſuſter merueyle grete ſtedfaſtenes grete ſufferaunce grete fulnes loue charyte ſo yonge mayde grete loue charyte ſhe ſhewed ſeke ſuſter ye fende grete enuye aboute lette dede mercy charyte power ¶ fyrſt vpon daye holy mayde aboute vnoouere wounde waſſhe wype refreiſſh agayn▪ came ſuche odoure ſtynche vnnethe ſtomake myght ſuffer almoſt ſhe brought vomyte aſſone ſhe perceyued ſhe aroſe agaynſt ſelf wyth hyghe wrathe ſayde ſkeymons fleſſhe wyſe whether ye wretched fleſſhe haſte abhomynacion thyn ſuſter whiche oure lorde boughte wyth precious blode yu mayſte falle euery daye ye ſame ſykeneſſe ſhe verſe trewely thou ſhalt punyſſhed therfore anone ſhe bowed done ſore hyld noſe mouthe open agaynſt wounde ſoo longe vnto tyme ſhe felt ſelfe ſkeymouſnes goo ſoo ſhe ouer came fleſſhe contrary ſpyryte ſeke ſuſter behelde cryed merueylyng ſayde cecedere doughter corrupte thy ſelfe wyth foule ſtynkyng ſore ¶ holy mayde alle cryenge wolde aryſe vp vnto tyme ſhe felt enemye ouercome ſo ſhe aroſe vp auoyded awaye fro tyme conſyderyng myght haue mayſtry wrought wylyly agaynſt ſeke ſuſter put herte whome thys holy mayde anſwerd full pacyently ſoftely ſeynge thus▪ trewely ladyes ſuſtres grace lord jheſu cryſte mayde neuer wold ſhe ſay worde blamyng hyr ſo accuſed hyr onely thus trewely mayde areyſed ryght ſo power ceſſe therfore thou ſhalt contynue holy ſeruyſe thou haſt gonne gyue ſtede ſende wold let ſhall gyue full vntorye thyne enemye euer hath imagyned ageynſt ſhall torne hys owne wyth myghty ſpyryte thys wyſe doughter haue oft ſayd thou ſholdeſt nomore ſerue ſtynkyng woman loo reward ſhe hath gyue thy beſye ſeruyſe hath ſclaundred full foule thy ſuſtres yf thou euer ſerue hyr come hyr neuer ſhall calle ne name doughter afterward ne thou thy moder ſoty leſt wyll ther fende myght haue mayſtrye hir ſclaunde ryng hyr ſeek ſuſter beganne wyth maner pyte lette hyr hyr holy hir ſclaunder ſhe put vpon hir thenne lord ſhewed mercy hyr make good fame hys mayde ſhewed ſeek ſuſter tyme ſhe laye hyr bedde gracious vyſyon woucheſauf ſhewe thys holy mayde vpon daye whanne thys dyſeaſes thys myght mene clerely ſhe wyſt neuer ſhe loked aboute behelde maydes face tranſformed trāſfygured hyr ſemed ſhe thenne katheryn lapais doughter rather lyke heuenly creature gloryfyed lyghte beclypped hyr rounde aboute ſhe behelde hyr ſhe yelde hir ſelf gylty hyr ſowle lorde ſclaunder ſhe putt • vpon holy mayde whanne thys vyſyon hadde tary •• whyle whiche appyred bodely eyen ſeek ſuſter came ſo paſſyd awaye whiche paſſyng ſeek ſuſter long comforted alſo ſorowfull treſpas anone ſhe axed mercy holy mayde wyth ſobbyng terys ſhe ſo wyckedly treſpaſſyd ageynſt hyr ſclaundred hyr full falſely loo maydens outward lyght lorde gaf hyr inward lyght knowe falſely ſhe deceyued fende anone forthwyth whanne holy mayde herde mekely ſhe axed forgyuenes wente hyr mekely took hyr armes kyſſed hyr ſeyng hyr thus full comfortably dere moder dyſpleſed wyth wyſe wote well fendes malyce youres thanke yon wyth herte ye loue ye wolde kept clene therfore wyte thyng thys fende hath wrought ſo malyciouſly ageynſt wyth ſuche wordes lyke thyſe thys holy mayde comforted hyr ſeek ſuſter dyd hyr ſeruyſe ſhe wonte whan ſhe leſte ſhe ſhold haue ſpende hyr tyme vayne ſhe wente hyr chambre occupyed hyr prayer mene tyme ſeek ſu ſte knowleched hir gylty wepyng waylyng afore thoo came hyr ſayd openly afore theym alle dyſceyte fende ſhe ſclaundred ye holy mayde wrongfully ſhe axed forgyuenes hem alle ſhe ſayde ſhe knewe well ynough yt mayde onely pure clene fleſſhely ſynnes alſo ſhe holy fulfylled wyth holy ghooſt ſhe knewe well thenne ſomme ſaddeſt hyr ſuſters axyd hyr pryuely wyſely ſhe knewe mayde holy token ſhe hadde therof anſwerd ſtedfaſtly wyth feruent ſpyryt ſhe knewe neuer afore ſwetneſſe ſoule ghooſtly comfort vnto tyme ſhe ſawe thys holy mayde afore hyr tranſfygured tranſformed ouercouered vnſpekable lyght efteſones thenne hyr ſuſters axyd hyr whether ſhe ſaw ſyght wyth hyr bodely eyen ſhe coude telle wyth noo thyng fayrenes lyght ſwetneſſe ſhe felte hyr ſowle tyme thenne ye holy maydens name began encreace vertuouſly ouer fende aboute dyſceyue hynder hyr name holy ghooſt enhauncyd hyr name vertuouſly thys ryght ſhe neuer ſonner throwe doun euyll
