recey • ue none delycat • mete day ſhe tournyd agayn ſymple faſte yt ſhe hadde begunne fore ſoo lytyll lytill ſhe tournyd ſymple faſte coſtome contynuelly neuer herd tho dayes confeſſour mayſter reymound berith record ſayth ofte tymes knewe body comforted none bodely mete ne drynke colde water vnto tyme ſhe brought ſuche febylneſſe hym thought moo ſhe almoſt dede aſſone ſhe herd ſaye ony nede ſhold done man̄is ſoule ſhe caught ſtrengthe ſodenly wythouten ony bodely comforte ſhe able goo mightely euer ſhe wythout ony greuauuce boue commune ſtrengthe whiche folowed neuer wae wery wherof came grace trowe ye ſpryte comforteth quickeneth body merueylouſly aboue kynde namely ſuche body ſubiecte ſpyryte alle ghoſtely werkes may euery ghoſtely man vnderſtonde alle thys holy maydens lyf aboue kinde full myracle ¶ tyme whan ſhe hadde faſte ſoo longe lyued without mete drinke confeſſour mayſter reymound aſked wheder ſhe ony tyme ony maner appetyte mete drynke ſhe anſwerd thus haue ſo grete ſwetnes lord gaue receyuing bleſſyd ſacrament ye aulter owne precio • fleſh blod yt noo wyſe myght deſyre none maner bodely ſuſtynaunce mete drynke then̄e confeſſour aſked eftſones whether ſhe ony appetyte mete ye day ſhe hoſylyd ſaid nay whā happed ſhe hoſe lyd preſence ſyght bleſſyd ſacrament ſight ye bleſſyd ſacrmēt alſo preſens preſie whiche ſhe knewe welle hadde day ſayd maſſe touched bleſſyd ſacrament comforted ſuche wyſe ſhe hadde none mynde bodely mete ¶ holy mayde ſtode bothe full faſtyng wythoutforth faſtynge wythinforth full wythoutforth drye wythinforth moyſte flodes quyk water alle mane chaunces ſhe euer glad iocū de fende myght ſuffre ſhe ſhold thus endowed ſuche gracious gyftes venyms woodnes malycious enuye ſteryd bothe ſpyrytuall folke temperall folke relygious ſeculer againſte ſyuguler gyfte faſtynge merueyle though ſtyred ghoſtely folke relygyous agaynſt ſuche yf theyr owne loue theym ſelf fully quenched grace regnid perylous enuye namely whan ſee another doo whiche thynketh vnpoſſybyle theym serche wiſely aſpye whether ſoth amonges holy faders dwellyng thebayde ſeculer man came grete congregaciō phatomye abbot receyue habyte amonges theym whan receyued habyte ye holy congregacion couent ſawe merueylouſly lyued myght doo dyde came alle wyth one voyce gretelyſteryd agaynſte phatomye bad hym eyther put congregacion newe monke elli thei wolde abyde wyth hym loo yf ſuche enuye regned thenne tho dayes amonges ſuche yt holde ryht • fyght folk enuye tro ye myht regne amōges ghoſtely folke yt lyuē thyſe dayes none wonder therfore thou ghoſtely folke grutched holy maydes faſtyng ſomme ſaid none lyuyng gretter lord oure lorde yet ete dranke while lyued erthe bleſſyd gloryous moder oure gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn marye alle appoſtles alſo lorde bad ſhold ete drynke ſet afore theym ſoo dyde lyuyng erthe myght paſſe theym lyke theym trowe none somme ther alſo ſayde afermed ſaintes afore v taught worde dede ſhold none take vpon theym ſynguler lyuyng paſſyng ſhold lyue common perfyght lyuyng somme alſo preuy bachyters ſaide ende faſtynge ſholde vicious therfore gaue counſeyll take none enſample ſhe deceyued alſo carnal people open bacbyters ſayde faſtynge fayned thynge wynne therby veyn glory therfore ſemed ſhe faſted preuyly ſhe ete thynge enuye agaynſt who fals doer fals opynyons purpos reple helpe god fyrſte ſomme legged theym oure lord bleſſyd lady gracious virgyn mary appoſtles lyued common lyuyng wythout ony grete faſtynge thē ne ſholde ſywe ſaint johan baptyſte holy lord jheſu cryſte lord ſayde hym ſelf ſaynt johan come neuer ete ne dranke faſted ſone man come bothe ete dranke ſame alſo ſhold ſywe ſaynt anthony macharye illarion scrapion many holy faders whiche vſes many merueylous faſtynges ne woman brynge mete ner drynke whether ſhe gretter blyſſed gloryous vyrgyn lady gloryous virgyn mary neuer faſted ſo ne lyued ſuche roche wyll alſo ſaye many holy faders lyued many yeres wythout mete ſykeneſſes though ſhe hadde ſayd thus god doth myn ſelf alſo leſs ony maner ſpyce pryde ſholde appyre euer ſhe ſayde ſhe ſuffred infirmyte ſynnes yet ſhe ſayde agaynſt conſcience ſhe ſuppoſed ſtedfaſtely oure lorſt hadde ſuffred falle grutchynge men punyſſhe ſynnes maner euyll fyll wyted ſynnes good euer wrought ſhe put oure lord ¶ ſame ſentence good anſwere thrydde preuy bacbyters ſayden ſtoppe mouthes leſt ſholde ſclaūdred yt ſhe came mete euery day ye meyne ye houſhold therbi know whether ſhe myght dyde yet otherwhyle ſhe wolde aſſaye ete ſoo grete payne alle yt ſawe hadde drynkynking colde water ſhe receiued gladly refreſſhe chykes throte maner lyf ſhe lyued vnto aſte ende grutchers theym ſlaundred faſtinge confeſſour mayſter reymound perceyued grete peyne ſhe ſuffred gyftes lord ſayd ſoo coude vſe grace oure lorde ſholde euer haue vyctorye thynges fallen hym then̄e ſhe tourned confeſſour ſayde hym ſoo wolde ye dyde ofte ony newe thynge byfalleth proſperyte aboute kynde wete ye right wel yt fro tyme holy mayde dronke oure lordes ſyde drynke lyf reherſid fo •• many grete grace haboūdant ī yt ofte time ofte time maner contynuabyl occupyed actuell cō templacion ſpyryte lowyd lord parte ſhe lefte wythout felyng bodely wyttes soo reherſed fyrſt party armes founde ofte time ſoo ſtyf tyme ſuche actuell contemplacion rather ſholde breke thē ne bowe eyen cloſed eres herde none noyſe neuer ſo grete bodely wyttes tyme ſequeſtred fro owne werkynge ¶ ſholde none merueyle noman yf wolde take hede yt ſyweth oure lorde began bee ſoo homely brennyd ſowle wyth ſoo moche haboundante fyre loue oonly pryuy place alſo open place well ſtondyng goyng ſhe whiche hadde thyſe grete grace knewe playnely confeſſour ſhe coude fynde none wordes telle expreſſely grace ſhe felte ¶ tyme whan ſhe prayed oure lord feruentely wyth prophete dauyd ſeyeng deuoutly thyſe wordes ¶ cor meum crea deus et ſpiritū rectum innoua viſceribus mei prayng lorde ſpecially wolde take awaye herte owne wyll gyue newe herte wyll hadde ſuche comforte ſemed lord jheſu come opened lyft ſide toke herte went waye belyfte owne herte ¶ afterward befyll ſhe commynyd wyth confeſſour amonges thynges ſhe ſayde ſhe none herte body whiche wordes cō feſſour ſ •• rned maner blamed ſhe ſayde ſoo thenne ſhe reherſed eftſones confermed wordes trewely fader moche maye fele yet felyng myn body ſemeth lacke myn herte oure lorde apperyd opened myn leſte ſyde toke myn herte went way thenne confeſſour ſayde vnpoſſyble ſhe ſhold lyue herte ſhe ſayde naye nothynge vnpoſſyble god therfore ſhe bad hym gyue credens ſo ofte tymes ward ſhe reherſed ſhe lyued without herte fewe dayes afterward befyll ſhe wente chapell fryer ſuſters penaunce wonte knele whan goo home befil ſhe contynued prayer ſo ſhe fro ſelf rauyſſhyng laſte ſhe awoke rauyſſhyng went homward ſhe wente waye ſodenly lyght heuen bicliped lyght aperyd lord holdyng honde reed ſhining herte lykenes mannys herte commyng thys heuenly lyght ſhe aferde ſhe fyll doune vppon grounde thenne came lorde openyd lyfteſyde eftſones pute body herte whiche hylde hondes ſeyng thus ¶ loo dere doughter toke awaye thyn herte laſte daye ryght ſoo giue myn herte wherby thou mayſt lyue endeleſly whan hadde ſo doo cloſed wounde agayn made open fleſſhe neuertheleſſe left merueylous marke lykenes woūde heled ſame place euer afterward felawes tolde confeſſour mayſter reymound ofte tymes ſawe ſhe coude forſake hym whan aſkid whether ſoo meruayllous gracyous herte ſo gyuen hyr lord came many meruayllous werkys yet many moo meruayllous reuelacyons haboundeth wythin forth came neuer afterward hoſeled ther ſhewed hyr many ſynguler gyftes grace oft tymes ſhe ſawe lytell chylde preſtys handy whyle well growen chylde whyle hote brennyng ouen fyre whan preſte receyued blyſſed ſacrament ſemed hyr fyre entred hym whan ſhe ſhold houſeled ofte tymes ſhe taſtyd ſo grete odour blyſſed ſacrament almoſt hyr body defaylled confeſſour enquyred trouthe whether ſo founde trewe ſoo wrote perpetuell recorde ſowne noyſe lyke maner comyn ſownes men hadde noyſe aboue comyn cours kynde meruayll though ſhe made ioyfull noyſe aboue kynde syth ſo ſhe hadde receyued herte aboue kynde tyme ſhe hadde receyued newe herte reherſed afore ſhe ſemed ſhe ſame ſhe afore ofte tymes ſhe ſayd hyr confeſſour see ye fader ſame afore rather chaūged another perſone wolde god fader ye knewe fele trewe veryly yf creatour knewe fele ſowle ſholde reſolued made ryght eſye neuer ſo harde ſowle full melodye ioye meruayll may abyde body alſo grete hote brennyng dyuyne loue therin thys outward materyall fyre ſemeth cō paryſon fyre rather colde hote alſo ghooſtly hote kynde led ſowle ſemeth ſoo grete loue neghbours thynketh myght gladdely ſuffre bodely deth wyth grete ioye ouermore ghooſtly hote come ſoule renewyng purytee mekenes ſo moche ſemeth brought ſame purytee mekenes chylde foure fyue yere age inne ſhe tolde hir confeſſour preuely none tyme thys holy mayde thus fulfylled hyr ſowle ſuche plente newe gracys many notable vyſyons ſhewed hyr ſomme ſhall reherce grace god ¶ fyrſte lord jheſu hys bleſſyd moder marye magdalene appyred gydres hir comforted hyr hir holy purpoſe whome lord axed ſayd doughter deſyreſt thou wyth wepyng chere anſwerd ſayd lorde thou knoweſt nedeth better haue wyll thyne ne none herte thyn hert thenne came hyr mynde marye magdalene commytted hyr ſelf fully lorde whan ſhe ſatte wepte fete wyth ſhe felte ſame ſweteneſſe loue marye magdalene felte tyme whan ſhe wepte wherfore ſhe behelde marye magdalene lord ꝑceyued fulfyll hyr deſyre ſayd loo dere doughter thy ſolace cō forte gyue marye magdalene thy moder whome thou mayſt truſtely go comforted hir ſpecyally commytte thy gouernaunce grete gyfte holy mayde thanked lord wyth gpete mekenes reuerently deuoutly ſhe comended hyr ghooſtly gouernaunce marye magdalene prayng hyr ſhe wolde woucheſauf take hyr vnder gouernaunce syth lord ſpecyally commytted hyr fro houre euer afterward holy mayde called marye magdalene hyr moder whiche doo wythout grete myſterye ſemeth marye magdalene lyued xxxiij yere • oche wythout bodely mete tyme occupyed comtemplacyon ryght ſo holy mayde fro tyme ſhe endowed wyth theſe newe grace vnto age xxxiij yere afterward whiche yere ſhe paſſyd thys worlde ſo occupyed dyuyne contemplacyon ſhe many meruayllous thynges ſpake preuely tyme hyr rauyſſhyng many hygh wordes contemplacion whiche ſom ſhall tell afterward hyr confeſſour ſaw hyr one tyme rauyſſhed fro hyr bodely wyttes ſame wyſe reherſed afore herde hyr ſpeke preuely thenne came nere lyſten clerely ſhe ſayd herde ſhe ſayd formably thyſe wordes latyn vidi archana dei ſayd often tymes wordes ſayde ſhe none thoo whanne ſhe reſtoryd ageyne hyr bodely wyttes ſhe ceſſyd reherſe theſe ſame wordes cō tynuelly nomore ſay haue ſeen pryuetres god thenne hyr confeſſour deſyryng knowe ſhe reherſed tho wordes ſo ofte axyd hyr thys maner wyſe good moder reherſed ye ſoo ofte wordes wyll tell ye mene ye wonte anſwerde may ſay none wyſe hyr confeſſour axed hyr cauſe ye wont declare many thinges lord hadde ſhewed wyll ye ſo thēne ſhe ſayde ſholde haue grete conſcyence therof yf ſholde declare haue ſeen wyth langage ſoo vnperfyte ſholde haue yf blaſfemed lord inhonoured hym grete dyffrence bytwene vnderſtondyng intellecte ſowle illumyned god expreſſyng wordes ſeme contrary eche therfore tyme tell haue ſaye ben vnſpekable ſkylle thynke ſhe well commytted dyuyne prouydence lord marye magdalene faſter ſhold ſhe houſeled ſhe deſyred hyr ſowle receyue blyſſed ſacramet aulture ¶ oftymes ſhe wold breke ſay deuoutly thus ¶ wolde receyue lorde jheſu cryſtys body wyth lorde wolde appyre hyr wont doo fulfylle hyr deſyre toke maydens mouthe put hys bleſſyd wounde hys ſyde bad hyr receyue • fleſſhe hys bloode moche ſhe lyſt ¶ thenne ſhe receyued plentuouſly lorde breſte ſhe ſemed pure loue ſhe ſholde hadde dyed cauſe grete ſwetnes ſhe felte herte ¶ hyt befyll alſo vpon sanyt •• exis day holy mayde prayed lorde deuoutly wolde voucheſauf graū te hyr brēnyng deſyre receyue hys fleſſhe hys blood ¶ wyth ſhe • reuelacyon yt ſhe ſholde houſeled morowe doubteles forbeden hyr freres ſhe ſholde ſo ofte houſeled ¶ thenne whane ſhe hadde thys confortable reuelacyon prayed lord yt wold woucheſauf clenie hir herte agaynſt tyme ſhe ſhold receyue hym ſhe myght worthely receyue hym ¶ tyme ſhe prayed thus ſhe felte reyne comenge doun hyr ſoule maner grete haboundant flood water ſuche lyquore onely blood medelyd wyth fyre whiche hyr ſemed purgyd clenſed ſo myghtely •• rſowie ſtrengthe tyre • • ded body clenſed alſo hyr body ¶ thys morowe ſhe • oſeek waye ſemed hyr ſhe myght goo one foot ¶ neuertheleſſ ſhe doubted thyng ye ꝓmyſſe • lord truſtyng hym fully began go chyrche whan ſhe come thyder ſhe knelyd doun chapell beſyde aulter ¶ thenne came hyr mynde ſhe enfourmed yt ſhe myght houſeled preſt ſhe lyſt ſuche ben aſſygned hyr▪ ¶ wyth ſhe deſyred hyr confeſſour ſholde ſay maſſe ſame aulter anone oure lorde gaf hyr comforte ſholde ſing sodeynly lord thenne touched herte hyr confeſſonr wyth deuociō ſholdeſaye maſſe day wyll ſyng day ne wyſte holy mayde come chyrche ¶ thenne ſteryng lorde dyſpoſed maſſe wente ſame aulter holy mayde abode lordes beheſt whiche aulter alſo neuer wont ſynge ¶ whanne came founde holy mayde axyng houſeled charyte ¶ thenne rceyued wyll god ſholde ſyng day ¶ ſayd maſſe ende maſſe maner came houſele hyr holy mayde aulter ende ſhe redy receyue bleſſyd ſacrament ¶ hyr confeſſour behelde ſawe hyr vyſage ſhynyng rede al wepre wyth terys whiche grete meruayll wuth deuocion ſhe receyued bliſſed ſacrament ¶ tyme ſhe houſeled ſhe ſo plenteuouſly replete lorde day ſhe myght ſpeke worde noo creature ¶ morowe hyr confeſſour axed hyr hir eyled nowe grace ſhe receyued ye day fore cauſe ſhe ſo ſhynnyng rede whan ſhe receyued blyſſed ſacrament ſhe anſworde thus ¶ fader colour tyme wote nere thys knowe well whā vnworthy wretche receyued blyſſed ſacrament hondes drewe ſom alle thyng ſaue allone wexed lotheſom onely temporall thynges dylectacyons worlde alſo comfortes pleyſaunces neuer ſo ghoſtly wherfore deſyred prayed yt ſuche ghoſtly comfortes ſholde ſequeſtryd frome ſo myght pleeſe god ende leſly knytte hym alſo prayed hym wolde take away wyl gyue hys wyll ſo dede right mercyably ſayd thus ¶ loo dere doughter gyue wyll bi whiche thou ſhalte ſoo ſtrong euer happe fro thys tyme warde thou ſhalt neuer chaunged neſtyred ryght ſo ¶ euer afterwarde dyſpyſed ſette lytell alle folke neuer ſtyred ne troubled ageynſthem ¶ ouermore yet holy mayde ſayd confeſſour fader well wyll ye wete lorde ſerued trewely moder ſerued hyr lytell ſoukyng chylde whome ſhe loueth tenderly ¶ moder ſuffred hir childe ſtonde ferre hyr whyle ſhe ſheweth hym hirtete hir breſte ſuffred hym wepe longe tyme hit tyme lawhed ¶ laſt whan ſhe hath ſuffred wepe long tyme ſhe gothe ther wyth lawhyng beclypped armes kyſſed ſoo gyueth hyr breſte ſhe tete ¶ ryght ſo ferde lorde wyth day ſhewed hys bleſſyd wounde ſyde ſtondyng ferre ¶ deſyre hadde ther putte mouth bleſſyd wounde wepte haboundantly ¶ thenne lorde ſayd tyme yt hadde ſo ſuffred wepe came gladdely tooke ſowle hys armes putte mouthe wounde ¶ thenne ſowle grete deſyre entred hole hys bleſſyd wounde founde moche ſwetneſſe knowleche hys godhede ¶ yfye wyſtye wold meruayll myn herte gretneſſe ioye loue barſt ye wolde aſtonyed myght lyue lyf wyth ſuche grete paſſyng hete loue alſo another thynge befyll hyr next yere ſe wyng vpon ſame day ſhe boute receyue blyſſed ſacrament aulter whanne preſt helde bleſſyd ſacrament hys handes afore hyr taught hyr ſay thus lorde worthy thou ſholdeſt entre thenne whan ſhe de receyued hym hyr ſemed fyſſhe entred water water hym ryght ſo hyr ſowfe entred god god hir ſoo ſhe felte hyr ſelf drawe lord vnnethe ſhe myght come home hyr chambre whan ſhe come home ſhe layde hyr doune vpon hir harde bedde leyng long tyme ſtyll moeuyd laſt hyr body take vp ayre ſtode whyle gyder thre wytneſſys bereth recorde whiche name ſhall tell afterward thenne afterward ſhe came doun lay vpon hyr bedde alle weyke feble ſpake ſoftely many bleſſyd ſwete wordes hye contemplatyf wordes ſteryd hyr felawes wepe whiche herde amonges thoo ſwetr wordes ſhe prayed many folke ſom̄e ſpecyally name namely hyr confeſſour ſame tyme ſame momente chyrche thought tyme thynge ſholde ſtyre hym deuocyon ſodeynly hyr prayer felte meruayllous deuocyon neuer aſſayed afore conſyderyng meruayllyng newe grace camto hym ſoo ſodeynly houre whyle thought thus ſodeynly came hym one holy maydens felawes ſayd trewely fader katheryne hath moche prayed day ſuche houre thenne anone knowe ſuche newe denocyon came hym houre katherynes prayer axed hyr felawe ſhe prayed ſhe tolde ſhe prayed oure lorde wolde woucheſauf graunte euerlaſtyng lyf ſhe putt forth hyr honde prayed hym graunte thenne ſhe took doune hyr honde ageyne ſemyng hir al ſore wyth grete ſyghenge ſhe ſayde thus lord worſhypped mote thou euer comyn terme hyr mouthe ſaye whan ſhe ſeek ſore trauaylled whanne hyr confeſſour herde wente prayed hir tille hym hyr vyſyon meke obedyent mayde tolde hole byſyon ſayd afore whanne ſhe came mater ſhe prayed ſpecyall frendes ſhe ſayd hym fader whanne prayed lord wolde woucheſauf graun te euerlaſtyng lyf hadde comforte ſholde ſo forthwyth aſked token lord myght knowe ſholde ſo none incredulyte rather notable memorye thenne prayed ſholde ſtoetche myn honde dyde ſo putte honde nayle cloſed nayle ſoo faſte wyth inne myn honde thenne felte grete peyne myn honde though yren naylle hadde ſmyten thorugh myghtely wyth hamour ſoo ſemed mynowne ſyght thought jnuyſyble haue marke cryſtys woundes myn honde ¶ alſo contynuance mater ſhall tell another meruayllos thyng lyke thys befylle cytee pyſe mayſter reymond hyr laſt confeſſour bereth recorde tyme thys holy mayde came cyte pyſe many wyth hyr amonges whome mayſter reymond one whyche holy mayde receyued worthy mannes place ſame cyte beſyde chappell saynt cryſtyane whyche chappell mayſter reymond ſayde maſſe holy maydes prayer ther houſeled hyr hyr deſyre ſhe vſed contynuelly whanne ſhe hadde receyued blyſſed ſacramente ſhe anone rauyſſhed fro hyr bodely wyttes tyme mayſter reymond moo abode tyll ſhe hadde hyr ſomme ghooſtly comforte wonte ſuche rauyſſheng sodeynly behelde hyr body laye proſtratr vpon grounde reyſed vp ſhe kneled vpon hyr knee ſtretchyng vp hyr armes hyr hondes wyth clere ſhynyng vyſage whanne ſhe ſo long kneled wyth cloſyng ſtyf armes laſte ſhe fyll doun ſodeynly though ſhe hadde dedly wounded anone ſone ſhe reſtoryd ageyne hyr bodely wyttes thenne ſhe ſente mayſter reymond hyr confeſſour ſayde hym preuely thys wordes fader well wete mercy god body markys bleſſyd woundes oure lorde mayſter reymone thenne axed hyr myght ſtode hir tyme hir rauyſſheng ſhe anſwer de ſayde ſawe lord faſtned vpon croſſe comyng doune beelyppyng wyth grete lyght whyche gracyous vyſyon ſowle ſo gretely ſteryd wyth lorde yt body conſtreyned ſtrengthe ſpyryte aryſe thenne hole hys holy woundes ſawe fyue rede bemys come doune hym faſtned vpon body cauſe body forſtoeyned wyth cryed lord ſayde lorde god beſeche theſe woundes appyre ſyght men outward thenne ſodeynly whyle ſhe ſayde thyſe wordes er thenne thoo rede bemys fully come doune body changed hir colour rede meruayllous bryghtneſſe lykenes pure lyght reſtyd fyue placed body vpon hondes foot herte thenne mayſter reymond axed hir whether ony bemys come ryghte ſyde ſayde nay onely vpon lyfte ſyde vpon herte mayſter reymond axed hyr efteſones felyſt thou ony maner ſenſyble pryne thoo place anſwerd wyth grete ſygheng ſayde ſuffre ſoo grete ſenſyble ſorowe tho fyue place ſpecyaly herte god ſhewe newe myracle impoſſyble lyue longe tyme gydres body worde marked well mayſter reymond hyr confeſſour eſpyed coude ſee hir ony maner tokenes peyne whā ſhe told ſhe wold ſay depted ſonder chappell went gyders home theyr inne holy mayde went hir chambre ther ſhe lay doun femyng euer aboute hyr drawyng deth thenne mayſter reymond called hys feleſhyp ſee ye wound thyng whan come wepte ſore cauſe wend ſhe ſhold depted frō thē ſaw hir ne • ſo feble nygh ſo ye deth ¶ neuertheles within whyle ſhe reſorted agayn ſtrengthe receyued mete thenne ſhe ſpake eftſones maiſter reymound ſayde hym ſhe ſayd fore ſhe may longe lyue yf god ſhewe newe miracle thenne mayſter reymound called gyders chyldren men wymmen prayng theym wyth wepyng wold wyth one voyce praye lord wolde vocheſaf graunte v holy mayde katherin ghoſtely vertuous moder oure mayſtres whiche lythe paſſing abyde wyth v whyle thys lyf conferme v vertue alle graunted one voyce ſoo wold wente wyth mayſter reymound holy mayde • yeng tranſyte ſayeng ſuche wordes weylyng wepyng moder wete well thou deſyreſt bee wyth thyne ſpouſe wyth lorde jheſu cryſt thy mede thy rewarde reſerued fro auf haue rewthe v whome thou forſakeſt moder leue v ſo freell wythout better enformacion vertu wretchyd worlde knowe well alſo thy well byloued ſpouſe thou loueſt wyth ſoo grete deſyre wylle nothynge denye thou aſkeſt therfore beſeche praye hym vouheſauf graunte v tyme leſt thou paſſe fro v thyn ge lytyll edefyed thy good lyuyng though praye wel coude drede v leſt wyll v oure wretchyd lyuynge certayne ben ryght vnwurthy herd then̄e therfore haſt louyd oure helthe ſoo tenderly feruently praye ye v wynne lord mowe leue yt lyf tyll ben edefyed ghoſtely vertu many ſuche wordes ſayde amonges theim wyth grete wepynge holy maide anſwerd ye knowe well haue forſake myn owne wyll ne deſyre neuer goddes wyl haue deſyred helthe wyth myn herte yet knowe well yt whiche helthe myn better ordeine one creature praye wyll therfore bee done thynges neuertheles yet ſhall praye gladly voucheſaf hym ſemeth beſte whan ſhe hadde ſayd word wente ſyde tyme beyng grete ſorowe vnto tyme knowe anſwer next day afterward ſhe called mayſter reymounde ſayd ſemeth fader yt lord hath condeſcendyd prayer hope ye ſhold ſoone haue wylle entent▪ ſhe ſayd ſo ſone vpon morowe whiche vpon ſonday ſhe receyued cryſtis body ye ſacramēt ye aulter cōfeſſour hondes ryght ſondaye bifore ſhe brought greate febylnes rauyſſhyg tyme ſhe hadde receyued bleſſyd ſacrament ryght ſo ſonday ſhe gretly ſtrengthed rauyſſhyng bleſſyd ſacrament whiche grete merueyle aboute mayſter reymound ſaid hope yt oure lord hath accepted teres cōdeſcēdyd prayer though thei ben vnwourthy then̄e wythin litil time afterward ſhe ſo quikly reuiued yt none thē doubte yt ſhe ſhold lyue yt god graūted fulli deſire almyghti god fader mercy wylt yu thyn trewe ſeruaūt welbeloued child yu cōdeſcendiſt ſo benigly thyn ſynfull ſeruauntis mayſter reymound thenne aſked ſykernes wheder paſſyō tho woūdes contryned alway dede body anſwerd wiſe oure lord • hu hath herd prayer thefore tho woundes tourment body • yde rather comforte ſtrengthe loo maiden ye knowe evcellent grace holy maide hadde alſo ye mowe lerne oure lord vocheſaf ſynnes whan thry aſked ony thyng longeth ſowle helthe ¶ yet ſhall telle another merneylous thyng ſemeth paſſeth haue reherſed yet ſo ſhall make ende chapytre helpe god ¶ tyme lord hadde receyued ſoule blyſſyd wound ſyde ſhewed myſtery eſt gloryous trynyte thenne came glorious lady gloryous moder gloryous vyrgin marye fulfylled wyth gloryous mylke gloryous breſtes tetes came mary magdalene comynyd wyth ful homely reuelacions yt ſhe hadde whan ſhe deſert thyſe thre come togydre gaue many bleſſyd comfortable wordes yet wanted ſhe comforte ſaytes apperyng namely ſaynt poule appoſtle ſaynt johan theuangelyſt ſaint domynyke ſaint thomas dalquino oftetymes ſaint agnes ſhe hadde onys reuelacion ſholde felawe kyngdom heuen ſhall declared afterward helpe god ſhal telle two notable poyntes befyll hooly mayde whan ſhe hadde vyſyons ſaynt poule ye apoſtle befil ī ye feſt cō • ſaciō ſaīt poule yt holy mayde ſo merueylouſly rauyſſhed ſelf thought ſpyryt drawe vp heuen ſoo ferforth thre dayes thre nyghtes ſhe vnmeuable wythout bodly felyng ſoo ſemed ſhe fully dede ſomme vnderſtode better condycion ſayde ſuppoſed ſhe rauyſſhed wyth ſaint poule thirde heuen laſte thre dayes ende ſhe reforted bodly feling ſpyryte ſo comforted reuelacions ſhe ſtoode longe ▪tyme afterward ſhe hadde half ſlepe yet ſhe ſlepte mene whyle fryer thomas fyrſt confeſſour another felowe whiche called fryer donat flerence hadde deſyre goo vyſyte hooly myte deſerte fyrſt wente thei come holy mayde hou •• founde holy ſompnolente cauſe wolde excite aſked whether ſhe wolde go wyth thē deferte vyſyte holy man anſwerd theym ſame hooly ſlepe ſayde ye notwythſtondyng yt ſhe wyſt ſhe rauyſſhyg ſo longe ſhe wayled wepte vnceſſabyly yt ſy • e ſayd ſelf wycked woman haſt thou ſoo well bee feed wyth infinite goodnes god thou muſte make leſyng bee thyſe trenthe •• thou haſte lerned heuen ye doctryne thou art taught holy ghoſte make leſynges ¶ thenne wyſt thou ryght well thou woldeſte goo wyth tho fryer yete thou ſaydeſt thou woldeſt ſoo madeſt leſyng thyn confeſſour thyn ghoſtely faders meoſt wycked ſynne ce ye maydens meruaylous wayes maners lordis prouydence loo leſte reuelacyons ſholde haue cauſe pryde lorde ſuffred falle ſuche leſyng yf may callyd leſyng none • ye ¶ thenne ſhe procedyd forth many merueylous reuelacyons wythin whyle befyll yong brother called alſo bartylmeus went ſodenly ſhe caſte eye lytyll ſyde behylde brother left ſyght ſaynt domynyke bartylmewe prayed procede forth ſhe began ſhe migte ſobbyng vnnethe ſpeke one worde ¶ yet ſhe myght ſpeke ſhe ſayde ¶ wretche ſhall doo vengeaunce ſynnes ¶ fryer bertylmewe ſynne myght thēne ſhe ſayde sawe ye bowed awaye mynhede myn eyen beholde broder went ryght while lorde ſhe wed many merueylous thynges fryer bertyimewe ſay nay coude perceiue ſhe bowed ony wyſe hede eyen ſyde ¶ thenne ſhe • ion thene ſhe wente home chamber ſaynt poule appleryd ſhe de afterwarde confeſſour repreuyd ſharpely lokyng tyme whan ſhe tourned hede ſoo ſyde ſo ferforthe ſhe ſayd hadde leuer ſhamed worlde onys • herde mouthe •• myghty god fader thyſe wordes dere doughter haue brought forthe thyle chyldren one kyndely naturall beyng ſecond perſone intrynyte oder louyngly ſwetely adopcion thenne holy made hadde grete meruayle ſuche comparyſon twene ſone god ſaynte domynyke ¶ almyghty god fader put awaye grete meruayle expownyd thyſe wordes ſayde dere doughter ryght mynowne ſone brought forth naturally eternaly euer pertyghtly obedyent vnto dethe takyng vpon hym mā kynde ryght ſoo dedes domynyk myn ſone adopcyon euer wrought fro hys chyldehode enof hys bodely lyf reuled ¶ obedyence mȳ commaūde tys neuer brake onys ony maner precepte myn virgynyte ofthis body ſoule grace hys baptyme kepte euer vndefoylyd ¶ alſo ryght myn eternall naturall ſone endeles worlde mouthe tolde ſpake opē ly worlde badde hym ſay therto bare wyttenes trouthe ryght ſoo domynyke myn ſone adopcyon preche trouthe openly worlde welle amonges heretykes amonges faythfus peple onli bi hīſelf alſo bi hī only▪ whyles lyued erthe amonges alſo bi ſucceſſours bi yet precheth ſhalle preche ryght naturall eternall ſone ſente dyſcyples preche ryght ſoo domynyk myn ſone dopcion ſente fryer alſo ryght myn naturall ſone eternall myn word ryght domynyke myn ſone adopcion prechour aboute myn word wherfore myn ſynguler gyfte gyue hym fryer vuderſtonde trouthe min wordes paſſe therfro alſo ryght myn naturall ſone eternall ordeyned dyſpoſyd lyff dedes doctrynes enſample helthe mannys ſoule ryght domynyke myn ſone adopcion put beſynes delyuer ſoules ye ſorowe errour ſynne pryncipall entent whan began ordre ſay helthe ſoules therfore may well lyked min natural eternall ſone ſone iheſu criſte reuelacioy whiche ſhe comynyd fryer bertylmewe▪ whan ſodeyn caas lokyng aſyde byfyll reherſyd afore ſhall procede forth remenaunt lyf holy mayde reuelacions viſyons▪ fyrſt wolde ye knewe maydens grete haboundance greces open reuelacions viſyons gre • ene loue therwyth whiche holy maydes ſoule fulfylled ryght ſyke body euer encreſid ſekenes loue ſoo yt ſhe roo • nomore bedde laye ſtyll euer newyng loue ſpoſe ſeyng thus aſwete louely lord goddes ſone ſone mayden▪ wyth ſuche many louyng▪ wordes ſhe praiſed oure lorde ſpouſe beleft wythout bodely mete therto ſpouſe jheſu cryſte whiche gyuen fyre loue cauſe ſholde bren̄e ſtō gely apperyd ofte tymes ne ſayd ſhe hym ſo febyll fyre loue good louely lord yu ſuffereſt ſo longe abyde wretched body wylt take thyn endeles preſence haue none joye wretchid lyf myn ioye ſeke loue iheſu none wythout euer loue lord ther delayed ſoo longe▪ fro thyn endeles preſence ¶ ha ha mekeſt myldeſt lorde delyuer myn ſoule pryſon dedely lif thiſe wordes ſayd ſoo weylyngly oure lord anſwerd dere doughter whan liued erthe amonge men beſyed neuer fulfylle myn owne wyll myn faders albe deſyred ete laſte paſke wyth myn dyſciples wyth myn fader herd ofte tymes ſaye yet ſuffred paciently tyme ordeined myn fader ſoo muſt thou doo though yu deſyre feruently onyd perfightely bleſſe heuen yet thou muſte abyde tyme haue ordeyned theenne ſhe ſayd lord louely lord ſythe ſoo kynde yet paſſe lyff thyn wyl done fiat voluntas tua one thinge beſeche ye whyles lyue erthe yt ſythe may yet onyd yt ī blyſſe▪ graūte longe lyue lyf onyd ye ye bi parte taking thy bleſſyd paſſiō ye whiche graūted ¶ ſhe aſked ſoo ſhe hadde fro tyme forward ſhe hadde ſo moche experiens euery day herte īher body paſſions lorde ſhe tolde afterward preuyly maiſter reymoūd ſhe neuer felte ſuche ſoor wyſe ofte tymes ſhe wolde ſytte talke mayſter reymound teche hym paſſyon criſte affermyng myghtely lorde jheſu cryſte fro tyme gloryous concepcion tyme ende blyſſyd paſſyon bare euer croſſe deth hys ſoule▪ grete paſſyng deſyre hadde helthe mannys ſowle whan conceyued ful grace wyſdome charyte none nede hym encrece hym afterward perfyght ynow theym begynnyng therfore ſythe ſo loued ſo perfyghtly god fader mankynde herte ſeyng conſyderyng god fader trinite maner depryued honour alſo mankynde depryuyd f • bleſſyd ende ſoo tourmē ted wyth compaſſyon hym ſelf vnto tyme myght reſtore paſſyon dewe honour god fader • inyte endeles helthe mankynde▪ alſo ſhe ſayde affliction holy deſyre none lytyll payne grete payne thefore ſayde hys dyſcyples ſchherthurſday ſoper deſide • io deſideraui manducare vobiſcum hoc paſcha ¶ haue deſyred wyth grete deſyre longe afore thys tyme ete paſke cauſe gaue theym ſoper ſpeciall erneſt helthe whiche wolde werke er thenne purpoſed ete wyth theym eftſones therfore ſhe alleggid wordys ſauyour ſayth another place pater tranſfer calicem hūc fader put awaye paſſion fro ſhall drynke whiche wordes ſhe expownyd thus ſayde perfyght folke ſholde vnderſtonde thyſe wordes ſymple folke done ſauyour aſked fader put awaye remeue hye paynefull paſſiō thus fro begynnyng gloryous concepcton vnto tyme deth dranke euer paynfull paſſyon grete deſyre mannys helthe thenne drawe nere deth▪ gredyly deſyred drynke▪ aſked therfore ſhold ſoone fulfylled whiche hadde ſoo longe tyme deſyred helthe mannys ſoule dryke ye whiche hadde drunke ſoo longe afore ſholde thenne ended▪ thus aſke remeuyng awaye deth rader haſti ende deth whiche ſauyour declared full openly afterward whan ſayde juda quod facis fac cicius frend thou ſhalt doo doo anone ¶ neuertheles though ſoo forſayd paynes full drynke deſyre hym ryght greuous drynke yet ryght obedyent chylde fader ſayde thus veruntamen non ſicut ego volo ſed ſicut tu fader deſyre myn wyll fulfilled thy wyll offeryng hym ſelf redy th • ſe wordes ſuffre dayly payne full deſyre longe lyked hys fader ſoo fyrſt wordes ſayd tranſfer hunc calitem c fader voyde paynfull fro vnderſtode haue voyded paſſyon come paſſyon hys deſyre afore ſuffryng deth helthe mannes ſowle endyd thenne ſayd mayſter reymond moder comynly expoſicion doctours lord ſayd tho wordes veray mā hede hys choſen bothe f • eel ſtrong who ſenſualyte naturelly drede deth myght example bothe freel folk ſtrong folk dyſpeyre felte theyre ſenſualyt • e kyndely dredyng deth holy mayde anſwerd ſayd actes dedys ſauiour yf ben wyſely conſydered euery creature hys conſyderacyon may fynde ghoſtly felyng ſpedefull hys helthe therfore ſyth ſoo feble freall creature fynden tho wordes comfort ageynſt theyr febleneſſe ryght neceſſary thenne perfyt folk myghty ſhold fynde alſo ther jnne cōfyrmacyon theyr ſtrengthe whiche myght thys expoſycyon afore▪ therfore better yt expowned many maners ſo yt al may comforted ther thēne maner wyſe one maner folk allone whanne mayſter reymond herde helde hys pea meruayllyng hyr grete wyſdom grace ſhe de neuer expoſycyon afore ¶ another expoſycyon ſame wordes ſame holy mayde mayſter reymond founde wryten book hir fyrſt confeſſour wrote ben theſe tyme whan ſhe rauyſſhed ſhe lerned lord prayer whiche made fore hys paſſyon whan • watt bothe blood water ſeynge thus tranſfer hunc calicem • fader remoue peynfull paſſion fro prayed thenne whome ſawe afore wolde haue parte paſſion whiche peynfull paſſyon cauſe loued ryghtwyſneſſe put condycyon ſayd verūtamen non mea voluntas neutheleſſe fader wyll fulfylled thy wyll yf putto ſuche condycyon wolde haue folowed ther ſhe ſayd folk ſhold haue ſaued tyme thenne thus prayed herde ſaynte poule ſayd hys reuerence exauditus eſt ꝓpter ſuam reuerenciā expoſycion wordes ſaynt poule comynly doctours vnderſtonden ſame ellys meruaylle ſame ſone god ſholde haue herde alſo ſhe ſayd another tyme mayſter reymond taught hym paſſyons whiche lord god jheſu cryſt ray god man ſuffred helthe mankynde ſo myghty impoſſyble ony man erthe ſuffre ſholde dye poſſyble many tyme yf ſuffred ryght loue yt thenne hath yet mankynde vneſtymable vncomperable ryght ſo hys paſſyon ſuffred conſtreynyng loue allone vneſtymable wolde beleue thornes hys crowne ſholde peryſſhe brayne bone quyk man ſholde drawe theyre ioyntes ꝓphete ſayd lordes paſſyon thus dinumerauerūt omnia▪ oſſa mea tolde nombred bone body thenne may proued yt pryncypall cauſe hys paſſyon loue whiche ſhemed mankynde myght ſhewed conuenyently hys paſſyon ſemed naylles helde hym vpon croſſe hys loue onely ne ſtrengthe man ouercame hym • ot loue men ſo ſtronge holde hym worde hys mouthe fyll doune grounde whan came take hym suche hyghe wordes conuenyent wordes lordes paſſyon holy mayde cōmyne wyth mayſter reymond yet ſhe ſayd ſhe experyence hyr body ſom maner paſſyon cryſt ſuffred croſſe▪ ſhe wold ſay impoſſyble ony erthely creature ſpecyally cauſe grete loue ſhe lord paſſyon moſt peyne yt ſhe ſuffred hyr herte ſoo ſemed hyr whyle hyr herte braſte cutt ſondre fro one ende thys grete peyne loue ſhe oftymes dede mennys ſyght thys bare wytnes many one whiche preſente whanne ſhe dyed loue cryſtys paſſyon allone mayſter reymond grete doubte put awaye doubte thought comen wyth holy mayde ſerche ſothe hyr whether ſo whanne axed hyr grete wepyng coude gyue none anſwer long tyme gydre laſt ſhe ſayde fader wolde ye haue grete pyte compaſſyon ſowle delyuered derke pryſon lyght tyme ſee ſo mery lyght efteſones recluſed ageyn ſame derke pryſone ſame wretche thus happed ordynaunce god ſynnes ne mayſter reymond axed hir hir ſowle fully departed fro body whome ſhe anſwerd ſayd thus feruent fyre dyuyne loue ghooſtly deſyre ſo moche hyr herte lyue lord endeleſly ſhe loued though hyr herte hadde ſtone yren muſt nedys breſte therfore fader vnderſtondeth thys trouthe myn herte myn body thenne vndo opened fro ouermoſt partye nether onely ſtrengthe pure loue ſo ſemeth yet fele markys ſyſſure myn herte ye may knowe yt ſowle fully tyme deꝑted fro body ſette preſence god ſawe preuyt • e god vn • efull ſpeke ony man erthe ther ſpeche erthe expreſſe preuytees ony mānis tongue wote well ofte mater tourmented ſo gretly ſowle conſyderyng thenne tell ſorowe wyth wepynge ſobbyng thenne mayſter reymond prayed hyr tell began hyr anſwerd ſayde tyme fedde comforted wyth many vyſyons reuelacyons lordes mercy fell ſeek pure loue laye doun myn bedde prayed lorde jheſu wolde delyuer wretchyd worlde oned perfytely whiche tyme wolde graunte graūted therfore long lyued lyf ſhold partyner paſſyon aſmoche poſſyble dedly body ſuffre ſoo ſhe tolde hym reherſed afore ouer ſhe ſayd loo fader ſuche experyence hys paſſyon made ſo ſeke ſtrengthe loue ſowle deſyred thyng ellys delyuered world ſame fyre ſo encrecyd ſowle herte often tymes defayled departed ſonder ſoule vtterly delyuered body neuertheleſſe lytell tyme ſorowe ne efteſones mayſter reymond axed hir long tyme hyr ſowle body ſayd kepte hyr aboute haue beryed hyr foure houres thēne ſhe reuyued ageyn yet axed hyr ſhe ſawe tyme came ſoule ageyne body ſhe anſwerd thus fader tyme ſowle ſawe vnderſtode ioye bleſſyd ſowles peynes ſynners myn mynde wold ſuffre wordes wolde ſuffyce expreſſe ſhall tell ſowle ſawe diuyne eſſen cyall beyng god cauſe ſoo lothe vnpacyent lyue worlde loue hym loue cryſten people whiche ſowle reſtoryd body ageyne ſholde defaylled dyed ſorowe hygheſt comfort haue whan ſuffre ony dyſeaſe haue perfyte vyſyon god therfore trybulacyons ben heuyſom comfortable ye may knowe ben conuerſaunt wyth ſawe alſo peynes dampned ſowles peynes ſowles ben purgatory whiche expreſſe perfytely wyth maner wordes yf wretched ſynners ſawe leſte peyne leuer cheſe bodely deth hondred tymes yf poſſyble thēne ſuffre daye leſte peyne ſpecially ſawe hem ponyſ ſhed ſyngulerly ſynned matrymony whiche hadde kepte hem gyder honeſtly ſholde folowed dylectacions theyr luſtys mayſter reymond hir confeſ ſour axed hyr ſynne ſpecyall greuouſly punyſſhed thenne ſynnes ſyth ſo moſt greuous ſynne ſayd ſkylle ſoo grete conſcyence ſynne ne ſo grete contrycy ſynnes rather offended ſynne thenne ony ſynne whiche ſynner chargeth remoue penaū ce grete ſynne neuer ſoo lytell thenne holy mayde proceded forthe hyr mater ſayd thus alſo fader whāne ſeen thyſe ioyes thes peynes wenyng ſelf hadde fully delyuered body oure lorde ſayde ſeeſt thou doughter ioye lacke peyne haue offenden torne ageyn therfore thy body tell peple theyr errour theyr peryll wyth worde aſtonyed torne ageyne body ſore aferde thenne lord ſayd profyte mennys ſoules thou torne ageyne thou ſhalte lyue lyfe thou haſt lyued fore ne kepe ſolytarie allone chambre thou ſhalte goo brode wynne ſowles ſhall euer wyth goo wyth bothe goyng comyng thou ſhalte bere worſhyp name ghooſtly doctryne afore grete ſmale laye people clerkys fore relygyous folk alſo ſhall gyue bothe mouth wytte ſpeke none may wythſtande ſhall alſo bryng afore byſſhoppys curate ſowles confounde pryde whyles lorde ſpak thyſe wordes ſodeynly ſoule reſtored ageyne body whanne perceyued hadde grete ſorowe wepte thre dayes thre hyghtes gyders wythout ceſſyng yet wyſe abſteyne ne refreyne ther fro whanne cometh mynde ſodeynly come fro grete ioye vnto pryſone body wonder therfore fader though myn herte breſt euery day conſyderyng grete excellent ioye tyme hadde whiche ferre fro done ſowle hele therfore ther ſhall man meruayle though loue paſſyngly whome lord hath bede warne theyr ſynfull lyuyng haue lefte grete ioye certeyn tyme wote long therfore ſaynt poule ſeyth ben glorye crowne ioye thys ſaye fader putte youre hertes paſſyon grutchyng tyme comyng whan ſhall homely amonges men whan mayſter reymond herde vnderſtode grace gyue hym ꝑceyued hys herte incredulytee blyndnes men ſhe ſayde ſholde publyſſhed wherfore bade bothe freres ſuſtres whyle holy mayde lyued erthe ſholde pupplyſſhe matree perceyued alſo ſomme folowed fyrſt hyr doctryne wente backward coude ne myghte take hyr wordes leſte ſholde offende god yf hadde hydde hymſelf wythout wrytyng wrote perpetuell recorde hyr dyſſece whyle ſhe lyued maydens knowe veraly al ſothe ſhall tell wytnes recorde preſent wyth holy mayde whan thyſe thynges befyll hyr ſame tyme whan holy mayde drewe nye deth ſemed reherſed afore drewe aboute hyr wymmen ghooſtly doughters herys ſent hyr fyrſt confeſſour frere thomas preſent hyr paſſage prayer holy exercyſes commē dyng hyr ſowle god came thre freres wyth hym mo preſent att paſſyng holy mayde whan ſhe paſſyd ſemed one freres took ſo grete ſorowe therfore vyolence hys wepyng veyne hys breſt broſyd wyth caught coghe ſpatte gebettes blood thenne another ſorowe ſtode aboute bothe wepte holy mayde ſo paſſyd alſo hir brother whiche ſhappely lyue long payne thenne ſayde frere thomas hir fyrſt confeſſour ſeek frere wyth grete feyth truſt brother wote well holy mayde grete reputacyon afore god hyr good lyuyng therfore take hyr honde putte ſame place thy ſekenes doubte thou ſhalte hole anone forth wyth dyd ſo ſo hadde helthe whiche tolde afterward al wolde ther alſo ghooſtly doughter herys preſent thenne whiche called alyxa paſſyd worlde ſone afterward moother came inne ſee whether ſhe paſſed ther none coude ſuppoſe otherwyſe alſo two ſpecyall wytteneſſys aboute ordeyne body ſholde beryed bothe ſuſters penaunce saynt domynyk one called katheryne ſhe whiche hyr felawe longe tyme afore hyr coſyn lyſa thus make ende thys chapytre ¶ ſomme myracles wrought gracyouſly thys holy mayde aboute helthe ſowles capitulum vij yf ſholde reherce alle myracles lord ſhewed holy mayde myght rather make grete book comprehende hem oo chapytre cauſe wolde put awaye dulneſſe ſholde rede legende holy mayde aboute aſmoche may vnder fewe wordes comprehende one chapytre myghte knowe vnder fewe wordes grete ben whiche paſſe ouer lyghtely therfore moche ſowle paſſeth body worthyneſſe ſhall begynne tho myracles whiche ſhewed lord hyr aboute mennys ſowles bodyes touchyng fyrſt whan jamys jacob fader holy mayde perceyued hys doughter katheryne alle gyuen ſerue pleaſe lord reherſed fyrſte partye thys legende euer loued tretyd hyr reuerētly louyngly bedyng folk hys houſholde none ſoo hardy lette katheryne hys doughter ony maner wyſe euer ſhe wyll haue done thys grete cauſe doughter loued fader therfore ſhe commended ſpecyally hyr faders helthe oft tymes oure lord ſuche truſte hys doughters prayer ſuppoſed well ſhe myght haue god ſhe wold hys helthe sone fader ſykened laye doune hys bedde ſeek whan holy mayde hys doughter perceyued anone ſhe prayed oure lorde hyr ſpouſe helthe hyr fader anſwerd hyr lorde ende hys dayes worlde come ſpedefull hym abyde lenger lyf ne ſhe wente hyr fader vyſyted hym examyned hym dyſpoſed hys ſowle founde redy wylfully paſſe worlde hauyng luſte abyde lenger wherefor ſhe thanked lord hyghly thenne ſhe prayed lord efteſones ſyth ſo hadde gyuen hyr fader ſo grete grace paſſe worlde wythout ſynne wolde woucheſauf graunte hym alſo flee heuen wythout payne purgatory ſhe hadde anſwere wyſe ryghtwyſneſſe muſt nedys kepte therfore ryght impoſſyble ſowle haue clereneſſe endeles ioye wythout perfyte purgacyon fore thy fader hath ben hys dayes good lyuyng among alle wedded folke alſo many good thynges well pleaſed wyth ſpecyally touchyng yet neuertheleſſe may ſauyng ryghtwyſneſſe hys ſowle muſt purged fyre brenne duſte erthely conuerſacyon whiche hardened endured ſoule thenne ſayde holy mayde lord thus dere welbeloued lord may ſuffre yt fad ſowle haue ſo tenderly nouryſſhed haue ſo many cō fortes hys lyf tormented ſuche paynes praye lord goodneſſe euer thou ſhewdeſt mā kynde ſuffre hys ſowle goo hys body vnto ye tyme perfytly purged oo waye yt nede wyſe payne purgatory ſuche wordes lorde ſhewed hys mercy meruayllouſly though obeyed voyce hys mayden bodely ſtrengthes hir fader jamys beganne defaylle deth warde yet hys ſoule paſſed neuer body vnto tyme yt holy dyſputacion betwene lord alledgyng hym ryghtwyſneſſe holy made axyng grace mercy▪ laſte long dyſputacion holy mayde ſayd lord welbeloued lord yf thys grace may wyſe goten graunted without ſom maner ryghtwyſneſſe ſuffre ryghtwyſneſſe fall redy ſuffre al maner peyne euer thy goodneſſe wyll ordeyne delyueraūce fad ſowle thenne lord graunted hyr grace ſayd loo doughter loue yt thou haſt ſhall graunte thyne axyng ſhall delyuer thy faders ſoule fully payne thou ſhalbe ſuffre payne hym long thou lyueſt whiche ſhall aſſygne holy mayde thanked lord ſayde good bleſſyd lorde yu haſte ordeyned ſhe wente hyr fader laye deieng ſhe comforted hym meruayllouſly hys endeles helthe ryght ioyefull ſhe went hym vnto tyme paſſyd worlde whan ſowle paſſyd ye body anone forth wyth holy mayde payned wyth ſekenes ſyde whiche called ilica paſſyo neuer went hir tyme ſhe paſſyd worlde ther neuer tyme afterward ſhe ye payne ſhe ſayde bare recorde ofte tymes mayſter reymond vertue hyr pacyence wythout ony com • yſon paſſyd hyr ſekenes ſhall declare ye helpe god afterward laſt chapytre thrydde ꝑtye whan hyr faders ſoule delyuered body holy mayde ſmyled full manerly ſayd wold god ye ben tyme wepte ſhe ſhewed gladneſſe chere ſhe myght none wyſe ſhe ſawe hys bleſſyd ſowle whan paſſed ye body receyued endeleſſe blyſſe wythout ony taryeng whiche ſhe ryght gladde lytell afore ſhe exꝑyence ſame ioye reherſed chapytre afore see ye maydens wyſely prouydence lord wrought maydens fader lord myght yf wold haue purged ſoule many maner wyſes made hym able inough ioyes dyd thefe yt hynge hys ryght ſyde wold wythout ſom payne mayde ſholde ſuffre ſhe axed hir encrece hir ioye whiche payne euer afterward ſwete hyr hyr ſemed wythout cauſe ſhe wyſt well yt hir ſweteneſſe ſhold euer encrece aftward hyr grace blyſſe ioye therfore ſhe myght wyſe calle ye payne ilica paſſio ſwete peyne holy mayde tolde puely mayſter reymond yt long tyme aft hir fad deth ſoule appyred oftymes hir thākyng hir hir grace yt receyued hir alſo tolde hir many puy thinges gaue hir warnyng ye aſſaillyng hir enemy therto kepte hir al ghoſtly euelys ryght haue tolde maydens myracle ſhewed ryghtwyſmannys ſoule ſhall tell myracle ſhewed ſynfull mannes ſowle ¶ man dwellyng cyte sene whiche called andrewe full ryche man oute wordely thynges world full poure inwardly heuenly thynges vitioꝰ mā neyther dred ne loued god haſarder curſed blaſphemer ſwerer god ſayntes wythin afterward mā take wyth ſykenes lay done bedde ſoo ſeke euery man leche ſayde deed perceyued hys curat come hym comforte hym ſholde beſhryue take penaunce make teſtamēt maner countre whan hadde herdde preeſte counſeylled hym deſpyſed bothe hym coū ſeyll wyf conſydered hauynge zele loue ſoule ſhe wente maner relygyous folke men wymmen ſtere hym god yet counſeyll myght bowe hym confeſſion contrycion ſynnes neyther wyth thretinge endeles paynes ne wyth rewardes endeles ioyes thenne eftſones curate came hym dredyng leſt ſholde haue deyed defaulte counſeyll ſayde hym ſayd fyrſte addynge therto many holſom wordes yet alwaye wretched man diſpiſed hym afterward dyde afore bothe hym wordes ¶ laſt fyll deſpeyre ſynne hooly ghoſt▪ ſo drewe faſte deth afterward tolde frier thomas holy maydes fyrſt▪ confeſſour wente holy mayde hous purſuyng conſtrayne al vertu obedyens charyte praye lorde wolde vocheſaf ſocour ye wretched ſoule bee dampned wythouten ende ¶ whan came holy maides hous founde rauyſſhyd fro bodly wyttes longe ſhe ſo occupyed durſte occupye ne durſt long abyde hous cauſe yt myght drewe faſt vpon hym wherfore charged felowe here tyme wyth ye whiche called katheryn ſhe charge holy mayde goddes behalue whan ſhe reſtorid agayn bodely wyttes ſhe wolde praye ſuche mannys ſowle lyeth paſſyng ſhe ſayd ſhe wolde ſo whan holy mayde herde ſhe ſoo greate compaſſyon ſoule ſhe prayed lord▪ anone deuoutly beſechyng hym entyerly ſoule ſhold peryſſhe whiche boughte wyth precious blode lord anſwerd ſayde thus wyckednes hathe aſſerued payne horrybly blaſphemie hath blaſphemid myn ſayntes wyth mouth alſo hath throwen table ye fyre deſpyte whiche paynted ymage myn paſſyon ymage myn bleſſyd gloryous moder ſayntes therfore worthy ryghtwyſnes yt brenne endeles fyre ¶ thenne ſhe fyll downe proſtrate wepyng foot lorde ſayde lord yf thou wylt conſydere narowe ſynnes men may eſcape endeles dampnacion wherfore comeſt thou downe born gloryous mayde ſuffer tourment cruell deth wayte mennys ſynnes punyſſhe theym horrybly endeles payne telleſt thou ſynnes loſt man bareſt vppon thyn ſholders maner ſynnes whether come mercy ryghtwyſnes haue myn lord bleſfulle thou ſaydeſt whan yu putteſt forthe helthe many mennys ſowles haue none refreſſhinge lyf ſee myn neybours tourned alone ſuffer paciently thyn abſence yf thou gyue ioye ſhall doo good meke lord put awaye fro yelde myn brother graciouſly obſtynat herte ¶ thus ſhe prayed contynuelly fro begynnyng nyght vnto graye mornynge tyme wepyng wythout ony ſlepe dyſputyng wyth lorde alwaye helpe ſowle oure lord aledgyng ryghtwyſnes gyue hym vengeaunce ſynnes hooly mayde aſking mercy laſt lord endeles mercy gaue anſwere ſayde dere doughter ſhall ſhewe hym myn grace yu haſt prayed andrewe ſayde dere chylde whi wylt thou beſhreue ye treſ pa thou haſt done loke yu beſhryue redy forgyue thyn ſynnes thenne harde herte ſouple grace cryed wyth grete voyce meyny aboute hym ſayde ſende preſte wyll byſhryue lord jheſu criſt hath warned ſhold beſhryuen ¶ whan meynye perceyued anone went preſte preſte came perfyghtly confeſſyd hym made teſtament wyth greate contrycion paſſyd thys worlde lord iheſu cryſte ¶ fader endeles mercy mercy able ben thy werkes profounde ben thyn prouydence who gracyous werk ben vnſcrutable vnto man thou ſuffredeſt man hardyd hys ſynnes vnto laſte ende femyng thou haddeſt none torce hym yet laſte thou prouydeſt helthe thin ſeruaunt came hym ſtere hym grace yet al coū ſeylles myght auayle meke prayer thy meke mayde thou condeſcendyſt mekely mercyabyly gaue boldenes herte thou gaue fyre compaſſyon herte brother thou gaue meke teres bowed thy mercy tre wely none thou thou aryſſydyſt vp thy ſpouſe ſhe ſholde bowe lord thyſe ben thy werkes gloryfyeſt thyn ſaintes wyll coplued loue ſeyng thy mercy ſoo plentuous▪ loo maydens mercy lorde ſhewed meke teres yet ſhall telle merueylous myracle ¶ befyll alſo another tyme ſame cyte seene two famous thefes ryght peryllous whiche take brought byfore temporall juge bee dampned payne myſdedes ſoo thei put cruell tourmente called tourmente hote yron wyſe put carte tourmentours redy wyth hote yrous breune one place another body therto thefes ſoo obſtynat neyther pryſon ne pryſon myght none creature ſtere ſhryue take penaunce treſpaas ledde cyte make aferd blaſphemed god ſaintis ſpecyally whan felte brennynge curſed magnyfycence lorde ſoo ſemed thei payne temperall fyre drewe faſte endeles fyre thenne oure lorde iheſu endeles goodnes whiche wold none body dampned ſaued thought wolde lete tho wretched ſowlis medyacion ſpouſe katheryn dampnacion ſoo ordenaunce hym hooly mayde quyete ſame daye felawes hous ſhe loued vertuouſly whiche alixa who hous ſtood ſame waye dampned wretch ſhold paſſe sondenly morowe alyxa herde merueylous voyce comyng hous wyth ſhe loked wyndowe ſawe fyre two men whiche dampned hote yrens thenne ſhe wente agayne tolde holy mayde ſayde yren whan holy mayde herde ſhe wente wyndowe loked tourned agayn prayer ſhe ſawe ſhe ſayde afterward mayſter reymound confeſ ſour grete multytude wycked ſpirytes aboute theym brennyd ſowles wythin moche tourmentours dyde body wythout therfore ſhe ſtered double compaſſyon praye lord helpe wretched ſowles payne ſeyeng thus ha ha mekeſt lord iheſu ſetteſt thou ſoo lytyl thy creature thou madeſt thyn lykeneſſe boughteſt wyth thy precious blood aboue bodely torment thou ſuffreſt theym cruelly tormentyd ſpyrytes wythinforth ſowles whan thou illumynyſt ſoo graciouſly theef henge ryght ſyde al toke tourment croſſe wurthely hadde deſerued knowleched god mā tourmente appoſtles doubte wherfore deſerued thyn bleſſyd voyce whan thou ſaydeſt thus hodie mecum eris paradiſo is▪ daye thou ſhalt wyth paradyſe dedyſt thou lorde▪ trewely nothynge ellys yu woldeſt graunte forgyfnes ſuche lyke hym thou deſpyſyd mary magdalene grete ſynner thou dreweſt graciouſly thou putteſt fro puplycane ne woman cananye ne prince pupplycanis zacher rather thou calledeſt theym therfore thy mercy beſeche thou helpe mercyabyly ſoules ſynners lad tourment thenne oure lorde bowed mercy wretch graūt holy maide ſuche gra • e ſhe wente wyth theym ſpyryte wepyng weylyng ſtere ſhe anſwerd god wyll wyll therfore ſhal leue haue bygonne whan thyſe wretch outward att gate cyte lord iheſu cryſt appyred theym wyth blyſſyd blody woundes ſteryng theym tournyd therto byhete theym forgyfnes ſoo dyuyne light entryd hertes aſked apreſte wyth grete inſtaunce beſhryue tyme ſhryuen turnyd blaſphemynge prayſyng lord euer accuſyng theym ſelfe ſeyeng wurthy tho paynes gretter paynes ſoo wyth grete gladnes went deth hadde gon grete feſte conſyderyd tho ſtode merueylyng gretely changynge perceyuyng euermore grete deuociō ye tourmētours yt durſt nomore brenne thē thanked lord grete mercy none knewe wiſe bi who prayer mercy gyuen ¶ neuertheles deuout preſte whiche confeſſour commaund afterward wyth holy maydes confeſſour merueylynge grete mercy god ſo ſoone tourned theym grace then̄e confeſſour aſked afterward alixa holy maydes felawe thys holy mayde occupyed whan man ledde deth thenne alixa tolde hym proceſſe ſayd afore founde well record ſame hour katherin lefte hym euery day lyued werſe werſe ſuſter called shy nochya whiche fully gyuen vanyte world paſſyng outrage aray body albe ſhe mayde bodi moder • abes therof grete forowe leſt ſhold dampned ther myſbelyuyng ſhe wente foly mayde prayed ſhe wolde vocheſaf ſpeke ſomwhat ſoule hele wyth doughter fraciſca shynochya ſpecyally wyth ſhynochya holy mayde ſhe hadde euer ſowles grete compaſſyon graunted ryght deuoutely herde james jacob brother ye ſame tyme sene whanne ſuſtren torned came ye cyte ward wyth yong brother hys curſyng thretnyng wyth grete pryde tho excyted hys ſuſters abyte seynge cryeng wyth bolde ſpyryte wolde tere awaye abyte fro back breng theim hys hows dwelled whome hys yonger brother whiche came hym ſayd trewely james yf thou come sene thou ſhalt torned alſo ſhryuen thy ſynnes curſed hys brother bytterly ſayde leuer flee bothe freres preſtys thenne wolde ſhryuen ony hem chylde oftymes reherſed hys ꝓphecyes ofte curſed laſt entred cyte wood man forthe wente hys faders hows hym prayng hym wolde abyde tyll morow morow ſhe ſente holy maydes confeſſour frere thomas wolde woucheſauf come ſpeke hir ſone james counſeyll hym hys ſowle helthe came wyth hym felawe frere bartholomew ſpake hym ſpeche ſemed myght profyte ſame tyme holy mayde katheryne prayed lorde hys conuerſyon while frere bartholomew ſpak hym thenne ſodeynly oure lorde touched jamys herte contrycyon ſayde frere bartholomew well apayed hys ſuſter ſhe ſholde ſerue god alſo prayed hym confeſſyon wyth grete contrycyon myght ſhriuē hys ſynnes ſerue god alſo thenne ſo perfytely ſhreuen ſomme ſynnes whiche wold neuer knowe ne confeſſyd noo man confeſſyd hym soo wyth inne lytell tyme wolfe made lambe lyon whelpe folk knewe hym amerueylled hys ſodeyne tornyng moder rabes meruaylled alle hyr meyne exortacyons ghooſtly perellys whiche lorde hath meruayllouſly wrought hys ſpouſe holy made myght make many grete bokes coude telle many wretched ſynfull lyuers ſhe hath delyuered fendes bondys many obſtynate folke ſhe hath brought ageyne theyr owne knowleche many ſhe made forſake deſpyſed worlde many tempted folk fonle ſynnes ſhe hath delyuerd fendes daunger hyr prayer doctrynes neuertheleſſe ye ſhall ſaye ſaynt jerome ſayd comendyng lady myght ſay yf membrys lym̄ys body torned tongue ſholde ſuffyce tell fruyte ſoules holy mayde hath purpoſed heuen helpe almyghty god mayſter reymond bereth trewe recorde ſawe thouſand moo bothe men wymmen comyng doun fro mounteynes vyllages longyng ſhyre cyte sene comyng ſee holy mayde though hadde called inuyſyble trompe whiche onely hyr wordes alſo hyr lokyng ſtyred compunccyon confeſſyd theyr ſynnes wyth grete contricyon ſo theyr went two confeſſours whome mayſter reymond one ſeyth hym ſelf confeſſyd hyr ſynnes wyth ſo grete contrycion eche man myght well knowe grace gyuen god hertes onys ne twyes oftymes wherfore forſayd pope gregorye tyme hadde ſoo grete ioye delyte wynnyng ſoo many ſoules graūted bull mayſter reymond hys felawes thoo whiche wolde come vyſyte holy mayde deſyren ſhreuen ſholde aſſoylle moche byſſhop dyocyes myght therfore mayſter reymond bereth recorde ſeyth came many ſynfull wretch hym hys felawes whiche neuer ſhreuen fore ſynnes whiche ſhreuen hym ſtode ofte tymes faſtyng fro morow tyll euen cauſe grete concours people yet myght ſuffyce wold ſhryuen tyme holy mayde prayed thanked lord ioyefully fende hadde loſte hys prayer penne expreſſe ioye hir herte ſhe tyme wynnyng ſoules thus moche reherſed chapytre ghoſtly meruayllous thynges lord wrought hys ſpouſe holy mayde katheryne aboute helthe mannes ſoules ¶ ſhall tell next chapytre god wrought hyr aboute helthe bodyes ſo ſhall make ende next chapytre wytteneſſe nedeth reherſed ende chapytre ben reherſed fore ſame chapytre ſuffyceth ynough ¶ ſomme myracles done hyr lyfe hyr aboute lyf helthe mennys bodyes capitulum viij shall tell maydens wonder meruayllous thyng yette lyght eſye inough wyth whome founde none vnpoſſybylyte lapa holy maydes moder womman grete ſympteneſſe innocencye yet ſhe hadde tyme lytell affeccyon inuyſyble thynges therfore ſhe ſore aferde dye paſſe worlde caught bodely ſykenes encreced day day whan holy mayde vnderſtode prayed lord deuoutely hyr wold woucheſauf ſocour hyr moder wyth helthe brought hyr forth nouryſhed hyr hadde anſwer anone heuen beſte hyr paſſe worlde thenne ſhe haue aduerſytees ben come ſoone ſhe wyſte ſhe went hyr moder ſayde hyr wyttely ſuche ſwete wordes moder yf lord ſwete iheſu wyll calle hym worlde dyſpoſe confourmyd blyſſed wyll beth noo thyng ſory ¶ thenne moder deſyryng deye prayed hyr doughter praye hyr oure lorde wolde woucheſauf graunte hyr bodely hele ſpeke nomore hyr hyr deth thys holy mayde prayed thenne lord hertely feruentely wold woucheſauf take hir nought worlde tyme ſhe knewe hyr wylle confourmed hys wyll ¶ lorde graunted hyr hyr axynge ſuffred hyr moder ſeek tyme drawe paſſage deth thenne holy mayde made mene betwene god hyr moder praye one exhorte lord ſhe prayed wolde take hyr ageynſt hyr wyll hyr moder ſhe exorted admonyſſhed wyth ſwete wordes ſhe ſholde confourme hyr conſent wyll god neuertheleſſe though maner ſhe bowed lord hyr prayer yet ſhe myght enclyne hir moder wyll hyr exortacyons ¶ thenne lord ſpake hys ſpouſe katheryne ſayde telle thy moder ſhe hath nede paſſe worlde tyme ſhall come ſhe ſhall deſyre deye then̄e ſhe ſhal haue ſothe ¶ hyt befyll ſhe lyued grete age ſawe many aduerſytres hyr dayes well perſones theyr goody ſo moche ſhe ſayde ofte tymes heryng many folke ſuche wordes whether lord iheſu hath put ſoule body ſhall neuer delyuered then many chyldren doughters grete ſmale yong olde ben dede may deye ¶ ſhall ceſſe mater procede forthe fyrſt mater began lapa holy maydes moder ſo harde herte ſhe wolde wyſe dye ne confeſſyd ne thynke noo wyſe hyr ſoule hele ¶ thenne oure lorde appyre meruayllouſly hys ſpouſe katheryne denyed maner ſemed hys fyrſte graunte ſuffred lapa drawe faſt toward deth wythout confeſſyon whan holy mayde perceyued ſhe lyfte vp hyr eyen heuen wyth wypyng terys ſayd lord thus lord god ben thiſe thy beheſtys thou haſt graunted none faders houſhold ſhold peryſſhe thy mercyable byheſte ſaydeſt moder ſholde paſſe hen ageynſt hyr wyll ſee well ſhe ſhall dye wythout ſacramentys holy chyrche therfore beſeche alle thy mercyes thou ſuffre deceyued goo hen lyue vnto tyme thou haſte yolde moder reuyued ſoule body ¶ theſe wordes theſe meruayllous cauſe herde thre wimmen sene preſent ¶ whan hyr moder ſemed ſyghte felyng dede ſoo aboute go home ageyne theyr howſes leuyng lapa dede yf ben holy mayde prayed ſhe dyd therfore abode lenger maners theſe wymmen ſhall tell afterward ¶ thys holy mayde contynued long prayer ye laſt lord herde hyr prayer gracyouſly quyckened ſoule body ageyne lapa ſhe lyued afterward vnto ye tyme ſhe foure ſcore yere age nyne wyth grete torment herte many aduerſytres ſhe ſuffred prophecyed hyr afore hyr doughter holy mayde ¶ myracle wytneſſe one katheryne angelyna ſuſtres penaunce alſo lyſa holy maydes coſyn preſent whan lapa leyde forthe dede herden holy mayde prayed oure lorde thus lorde ben theſe thy beheſtys thou behote ſayd afore remeynaunt hyr age whan ſhe reſtoryd ageyne lyf bare wyttenes many one lo ye maydens may ye knowe meryte holy mayde wyth lord iheſu delyuered hyr faders ſoule purgatory reduced hyr moders ſoule hir body ageyne meruayllouſly ¶ another meruayllous thyng ſhall tell happened ther comyn peſtylence bocchys reygnyng cyte sene ſoo oppreſſyd bothe men wymmen yong olde deth comynly dyed wythin two dayes thre fertheſt whiche ſekenes feryd many man ¶ thenne mayſter reymond wente aboute vyſyte ſeek folke comforted god thyng chargyng infeccyon peſtylence touchyng hys bodely deth ſoo myght wynne ſoules whanne hadde ſo vyſyted werynes goyng aboute reſtyd hym chyrche lady hadde grete deuocyon namely perſone ſame chyrche bleſſyd lyuer well knowen wyth thys holy mayde katheryne whiche perſone called syr mathewe ¶ befyll fewe dayes mayſter reymond wente morowe vyſyte ſeek folke wonte came chyrche lady deuocyon hadde lady place alſo affeccyon hadde perſone ſyr mathewe wente loke ferde sodeynly whan entred chyrche ſawe ſyr mathewe bere vp hys chambre ſemynge hadde dede vyolence peſtylence hadde loſt bothe colour hys face ſtrengthe hys body alſo hys ſpeche ¶ thenne mayſter reymond axed aboute hym eyled anſwerde ſayd nyght afore aboute one mydnyght vppe vyſyte ſeek body wyth inne lytell tyme afterward take wyth peſtylence mayſter rymond ryght ſorye folowed hym vp chambre dyd ne ſatte doun hym wythin whyle whan layde hys bedde recouered ſpyrytes ageyne callyd mayſter reymond hym prayeng hym confeſſyon ſo ſhryuen clene hys ſynnes ofte wonte tyme aſſoylled mayſter reymound axed ſtode wyth hym anſwerd ſayd ageyne greued hym ſo ſore hys grynde flanke ſemed hym thygh wolde falle awaye onely thygh alſo ye hede fareth though departed foure partyes payne ache ſuffred ther inne thenne mayſter reymond touchyd taſtyd hys poūſe founde well hadde paſſyng feuer wherfore hys menye ſholde bere hys water lech ſo dyd mayſter reymound folowed ſoone knowe verayly lech wolde ſaye whome leche ſayde thus thys man take wyth peſtylence therfore drede hows lady ſhall wante lacke good perſone ¶ thenne axed mayſter reymond whether myght holpe ony maner remedye medycynes ſayd ſholde aſſaye hadde grete truſt noo medycynes cauſe ſykenes ryght greuous thus mayſter reymond departed hym wyth grete ſorowe euer prayeng waye lord hys ſoule wolde woucheſauf ſaue hys bodely lyf yet whyle hys example many ¶ mene whyle holy mayde herde ſaye ſyr mathewe ſeek whome ſhe loued tenderly hys vertuous lyuyng anone ſhe wente home hym ſoone ſhe ſawe hym ſhe cryed hym ſayd ¶ aryſe vp ſyr mathewe aryſe vp ſhame tyme lye bedde sodeynly thenne atte hyr callyng feuer bocche wente away fro hym though hadde neuer hadde hem thenne roos vp wythout ony taryeng goodly ſoo hys ryſyng ſayde ſmylyngly ioyefully vertue god reſtyd holy mayde ¶ thenne holy mayde wente awaye fledde preyſyng men ſhe went hows mette wyth mayſter reymond whome mayſter reymond ſayd full ſorowfully ¶ moder whether thou wylte ſuffre man dye ſo dere profytable v alle ſhe wyſt well ynough ſhe hadde done yette ſhe ſayde hym mekenes ſuche wordes fader wordes theſe whether ye wene god may delyuer men fro deth ¶ thenne ſayde mayſter reymond hyr ageyne wyth grete ſpyryte ſorowe hadde hys deth saye whome thou luſt tell ſuche thynges knoweth lorde dothe wyth knowe well euer thou axyſte god thou ſhalte haue ¶ thenne holy mayde bowed hyr hede hym ſmyled laſte ſhe loked vp wyth gladde chere vpon hym ſayd good chere fader ſhall dye thys tyme ¶ wyth mayſter reymound gladde knewe well god hadde gyue hyr grete grace ſoo departed hyr wente ſyr mathewe loke ferde whome founde ſyttyng hys bedde wyth gretr ioye reherſyng myracle holy mayde ¶ whome mayſter reymound ſayde confortynge hym holy mayde tolde hym syr mathew ſayd thenne mayſter reymond trowe ye ſhe hath ſayd wyſt ne • ſhe tolde worde therof syr mathew wyth yt aroos vp bedde ſat doune mayſter reymound tolde hym hole gladly holy mayde ſayde hym reherſed afore soone ſyr mathew ete dranke none ſeke mannis mete hole mā ny mete grete merueyle mercy gladde vnne myght ſpeke worde ſame daye morowe myracle wytneſſe one fryer nychol came wyth mayſter reymound preſtes clerkes hous glorious lady gloryous vyrgyn mary xx aboute praye maydens taketh hede infydelyte curyous hertes dyſceyue myracle somme wyll ſaye perauenture none greate merueyle though man helyd ſuche comyn ſekenes feueres peſtylence day ſuche thynge happeth may aſked agayn merueyle whan lord heled petre wyffes moder ye feuers al day happeth men ben delyuered feuers neuer ſoo greuous petris wyffes moder reherſed myracles goſpell taketh hede ye curyous vntrowyng hertes take hede whether whiche heled man mathewe heled petris wyffes moder helyng petre wyffes moder commaūded feuers ſholde goo fro ſoo dyde anone wythout ony taryeng▪ ſhe thenne aroſe vp myniſtred lord mete ¶ ryght ſoo miracle ſame lorde ſpak holy maydes breſte whiche heled petrys wyffes moder ſoo ſyr mathewe bothe fruers alſo peſtylence cauſe trowe trewely mynyſtracion ſholde ſhewe lorde tyme comynge wynnyng ſoules ſoo thenne entent folowyng cauſe miracle goth byfore therto made ſo perfyghtly hole ete forwyth hole mete mennys mete thought hadde ſeke afore ſythe haue tolde myracle done helthe bodyes ſhall telle nother helpe god ¶ lytyl beſide cyte sene deuoute woman one ſuſters penaunce ſaint domynyke whiche herd ſawe moche vertuous lyuyng holy mayde ſhe drewe moche afterward vnder coūſeyll holy mayde dyde reuerence moder befyll day deuout ſuſter hye ſolier houſ certayn thynges ſhe hadde ſodenly ſolyer fyll doune woman vndernethe ▪ alle raftre trey broſed ſo ſhe drawe halfe ded ſoone deed laſte helpe god ſhe broughte bedde began reuyue felte payne herte broſour complayned ſore wyth wepyng weylyng lech ſought beſynes hele her▪ yet lechecraf ſhe myght tourne bede without helpe whan ye holy mayde katheryn herde therof ſhe compaſſion herte ſuſter came comforted penaunce dyſeſe whan ſhe perteyued dyſeſe ſoo paſſyng payne touched place body paynefull though ſhe wolde anoynted theym wyth hondes whiche touchyng ſuſter 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page duplicate〉 well apayed ſuppoſyng faythfully mercy god ſholde bee grete eſe hadde ſo ſoone touched ſyde ſhe hole though ſhe hadde felt afore none payne thenne ſeke ſuſter prayed that▪ ſhe wolde touche oder ſyde ſhe dyde ye ſyde cauſe holy mayde thenne ſuppoſed eſe dyde ſoo ſhe badde ſame wyſe dyſeſe went waye place touchyng ſyde ſoo thenne laſte holy mayde touchyd ouer body ſhe felte dyſeſe dyſeſe clene voyded laſte whan ſhe alle hole ſhe tourned aboute ſelf wythouten ony helpe myght ſee verely token ſhe fully hole neuertheles yet ſhe helde pea tyll tfe hooly mayde goo leſte ſhe ſholde haue troubled mekenes yf ſhe hadde tolde ī preſence afterward ſhe told bothe lech neyghbours ſayde thus katheryne doughter lapa hath heled touchyng hadde rueyle therof thanked god hadde gyue ſuche gracious vertues holy mayde katheryne wyſte ryght well holynes might come god therfore thanked hym myracle mayſter reymound knewe tellyng ſhall tell anther yt mayſter reymound ſelf knewe ſawe ¶ tyme whan greate peſtylence contynued cyte sene reherſed afore holy recluſe cyte sene called scūs louyd whiche touched wyth ſame peſtylence whan holy mayde perceyued ſhe ordeyned ſholde brought hous gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn mary whiche called alſo ye hous mercy ſhe ſelf wyth felawes vyſyted hym ordeyned althynge nedefull hym ſekenes laſte ſhe came ſelf tolde hym preuyly hys ere ſayde thus fader drede thou ſhalt deye ſekeneſſe att tyme ſhe wolde telle thyng mayſter reymound felawes whiche prayed praye hym ſholde lyue ſemed ſhe doubte lyf well therfore ſhe ordeyned hym medycins heled wherfore mayſter reymaūd alle felawes ſory cauſe louyd holy man gode lyuyng thenne laſte ſekenes encreſed drewe faſte deth ſemed wherby al ſawe hym ſuppoſed ſhold deye prayed good paſſage ſoule alſo holy man wende ſholde haue deyed right anone ſame poynt deth holy mayde came rouned ere ſaide ye ſecond tyme fader drede yu ſhalt deye tyme ſekenes vnderſtod wel yt wyttes party dyſtrauȝt alienyd fro hym greuouſnes payne gaue credence wordes thenne dyde actuall payne deth ſo fyll afterward holy maydes wordes • came ye dedes kynde nature neuertheles contynued ſuche tranſite paſſyng ye comyn tyme mani dayes gyder ye laſt ye ſpirite paſſyng ſemed holy mayde came ſayde nowe ye thyrde tyme ſeke mannys ere thus charge ſpyryte name oure lorde theſu cryſt thou paſſe anon ſpyryte reſorted quycly agayn body thenne holy man toke ſtrengthe hym ro vp aſked mete ſoo wythin lytyll time hole lyued afterward holy mayde paſſyd world many yeres holy man yt called scūs bothe name dede tyme hole tolde maiſter reymound holy mayde ſayd hym tyme ſekenes preuyly ere felte myght vertuous wordes wherby ſpyryte called gayn poynt paſſyng afermed folke none naturall cauſe reſtoryd hym agayn lyf myght god ſhewed ſpouſe katheryn folke gaue credence cauſe lyued grete vertu holyneſſe knowen famous man cyte seene xxxvj yere gyder wythout ony repreue hys lyuyng ¶ ferthermore maydens ſhalle telle another myracle hooly mayde wrought mayſter reymound tyme grete peſtylēce ſoo breme cyte seene reherſed fore alle folke fledde cauſe ſoo infectyf soo men wymmen deyed wythout comforte counſeyll kepyng mayſter reymoūde bythought hym bounde loue mennis ſoule caſtyng none peryll one bodely dethe enfection peſtylence purpoſed hym goo aboute cyte vyſeted ſeke folke comforted theym dyde dede neuertheles cauſe alone party ſo grete cyte viſyte comforte ſeke vnethes myght haue tyme ſpace ete reſte ſoo ſente fro one hous another ¶ soone nyght befyll toke reſte wakyng certayn hour ſerue god felte greuaūce peſtilence hys grynde flancke fere durſt aryſe lay ſtyll thought hym paſſage worlde deſyred gretely hadde daye myght goo ſpeke wyth holy mayde katheryne thenne ſeke mene whyle hadde feuer hede ache maner peſtylence ſekenes ſoo gretely payned tourmentyd yet ſayde matyns myghte whan daye called hym hys felawe wente gyder myght holy maydes hous founde home ſhe vyſyte ſeke body ¶ mene whyle hym thought ſhe ſoo longe ſo ſeke myght thynge doo lay doune lytyll bedde prayeng tho ren hous ſholde ſende aſſone myght ſent came anone perceyued yt ſore ſeke ſhe knyled doune afore bedde croſſed hym forhede wyth honde thenne ſhe began praye ſhe wont done ſoule mayſter reymound behelde ſhe rauyſſhed fore hym hopynge ſom̄e ſynguler grate prouffyte ſoule body abode long ſemed within half houre afterward aboute felte body ſterid avomite wening yt ſholde haue caſte yet ſoo hym thought euery▪ parte body pulled wyth maner vyolence ſomme maner corrupcion ſo began wexe better eſe yet holy mayde fully reſtoryd agayn bodely wyttes hole ſaue lytyl fevylnes bylefte hym tyme thys holy mayde hadde purchaſed lord grace helthe ſhe ſe • yd rauyſhyng badde felawes ſhold ordeyne ſomme mete hym whan receyued mete holy hondes ſhe badde hym lye doun • eſte whyle dyde ſoo ſhe badde hym whā awoke ſtronge though hadde ſeke then̄e holy mayde ſayde vnto hym fader gooth laboureth helthe ſowles thanketh almyghty god hathe delyuered fro parylle went forthe cuſtumably beſynes thanked god hadde gyue ſuche vertu hys blyſſyd mayde suche lyke myracle lorde wrought holy mayde fryer bertylmewe time ſame peſtylence yet myracle ye bi cauſe long time waſ oppſſid ſekenes mayſter reymoūd cauſe wyſe lyke ellys therfore paſſe ouer reherce wolde ye vnderſtood may den holoy mayde ſhewed oonly dyuyne myracle curacion tyme peſtylence alſo tymes yet cyte sene alſo place therfore one ſhall declare tyme wherby ye may vnderſtonde yf ye take hede wytely therto ¶ befyll ſoone general peſt • lence whiche reherſed afore ye many folke men wymmen well relygyous ſeculer ſpecyally certayn mynchis cy •• • yſe herde famous name holy mayde katheryn deſyreden ſee ſpeke cauſe notlefull theym goo oute ſeke therfore prayed well lettres meſſengers ſhe wolde voucheſ • f come • yſe ſeyeng ſhe myght wynne many ſon meſſages thenne ſhe recource prayer ſhe wont done aſked lorde mekely declaracion doubte ſhe ſtode ſhe ſholde doo ſomme theym counſeyllers ſaide beſt goo ſom̄e ſayde nay wythin fewe dayes afterward ſhe anſwere lord ſhe beknewe afterward mayſter • eymound ſhe ſhold tarye algatys ſhe ſholde goo ſpeke wyth hys ſeruauntys ſpouſe dwellyng ſame cyte pyſe thenne • ewe obedyencer leue mayſter reymound confeſſour ſhe wente pyſe whome folowed afterward mayſter reymound wyth certeyn hys bredren confeſſyons many ther came whā herde ſpeke ſoo • eruent wordes loue ſteryd therby contrycion le • ſholde lette fro trewe conuerſacyō falle agayn fendes ſnares ſuche cōpuccion ſhe wold beidde theim go confeſſion ſhryue without ony taryeng cauſe confeſſyon ofte tymes delayed defaute confeſſours therfore ofte tymes ſhe deſyred ſhe myght haue confeſſours ſhe myght ſende ſuche repentaunce therfore maiſter reymound two felawes hadde power pope bull aſſoyle tho endu • ed confeſſyon holy mayde whā ſhe came pyſe ſhe receyued burgeys hous called gerardus whiche gerad vpon daye brought wyth hī yonge man xx yere age alle ſeke feuers holy mayde beſechinge ſhe wolde praye helthe tolde vexid xviij monethes gyders wyth feuers ſoo none daye hadde therto ſo myghty hadde brought hym ſoo lowe well ſene hys chekes hys body •• myght neuer none medecyn made hoole thenne holy mayde hadde grete compaſſyon herte yonge man ſhe aſked hym longe goo ſhryue hys ſynnes toke penaunce ſayd many yere therfore ſayde ſhe lord hath yeue • oorge thou haſt purged thy ſoule holy confeſſyon ſoo longe tyme therfore ſone goo forthe anone confeſſion caſt venim whiche enfecteth alle thy body whan confeſſyd • ame agayne ſhe put holy honde vpon ſholders ſayd hym thus goo ſone pee • lord • heſu cryſt wyll thou nomore vexed wyth tho feuers ſhe ſayd fro time forward vexed therwyth within fewe dayes came holy mayde thanked curacion ſayde openly afore • folke hadde neuer feuers ſythe ſhe voyded vertu lord • ff bereth wytnes mayſter reymound ſawe myracle wytneſſe ynow gerad childes moder many afterward yonge man puplychid miracle •• e contree ſuche another byfyll cyte seene moche more▪ merueylous cauſe ſikenes perylous ¶ ſuſter penaunce ſaynt domynyke ſame • yte seene called gemina whiche loued well holy mayde ſhe ſekenes hir throte whiche called ſ • ynce contynaunce tyme ſekenes encreſyd ſoo made throte ſoo ſtreyght vnethe ſhe might drawe brethe▪ almooſt ofte tymes ſtrangelyd thenne ſhe wente holy mayde prayed ſhe myght ſpeke ſeyenge thus moder ſhaldeye ye helpe holy maide hadde ſoo grete compaſſyon ſhe toke holy honde croſſed throte▪ ¶ anone wythout ony taryenge • e ſekenes avoyded ſoo ſhe come wyth grete ſorowe went home wyth grete gladneſſe tolde ſoone confeſſour cauſe ſomme haue tolde curacions done body holy mayde diuerſe perſones therfore ſhall telle grete notable myracle lorde wrought • bleſſyd holy mayde ¶ befyll holy mayde wente tyme fro pyſe auyoun wyth whome wente two good deuoute yonge men wrote lettres holy mayde wolde ſende one called neryus afterward • deuoute recluſe ca • led stephene afterward monke charterhous good vyrtuous lyuer therto ſame • yte auyoun wente alſ • mayſter reymoūd ¶ happed whan entred cyte auyoun forſayd neryus ſeke wyth merueylou • ſykenes bowellis myght haue none reſte neyther nyght ne daye cryed wayled ofte tymes might lye bedde creped hondes foot ſought reſte yet myght none fynde tolde holy maide ſhe badde mayſter reymound ſende afleches helpe hym comforte wolde ſhe none gyue mayſter reymoūd dyde ſoo none leche myght eſe rather payned trowe ende allone cauſe lord wolde worke myrarle ſpouſe katheryn laſt leche ſaid maiſter reymoūd yt myght prouffyte hym therfore hadde none truſte lyffe ¶ whan mayſter reymound hadde tolde companye ſatē mete stephene felowe neryus roos vp wyth grete ſpyryte went holy maydes chambre ſytyng doune knee prayed mekely ſhe wyll ſuffre felowe neryus deye ſuche ſtraunge contree holy mayde anſwerde thus ſone art thou heui thou ſholdeſt ſory thy felawe lorde wyll rewarde hym blyſſe pacyence ſufferyng ſekenes then̄e ſayd agayn dere moder yett myn prayer tyme helpe hym wote well ye may ye wyll thenne ſhe ſayd well ſone ſee well thou art conforme wil god haue tolde therfore ſythe ſee thou art ſoo tourmentyd hym come morowe whan go maſſe houſelyd reduce mater myn mynde ſhall ſende vp thyn prayer god thou ſhalt praye maye herde thenne ſtephen well apayed wyth vyheſte • erly morowe mette wyth holy mayde goyng maſſe aſſone aſpyed fyldoune knee prayed ſhe wolde forgete hym ſpake day afore tyme whan ſhe ho • elyd ſhe rauyſſhed bodely wyttes prayed lord ſeke man soone ſhe reſtoryd ayen bodely wyttes came ſame stephene ſmylyng whiche abode anſwere ſayde vnto hym thus sone thou haſt grace thou haſt aſked thenne aſked whether neryus ſhold deliuerd ſekenes ſayd ye wyth wente gladly felawe badde hym good ſhall hole ſoo full tendaunt aboute recouer hym tyme mynyſtracion aboute hī happed ſame stephene ſeke lay doune bedde paſſyng feuer whan holy mayde knewe ſhe hadde grete ſowwe went hym aſked hym ſekenes hadde ſhe perceyued touchynge hys ponſe vexed wyth ſtrong feuer anone wyth greate feruour •• ſpyryte ſhe ſayde thus charge feuer vertu obedyence tho • goo man thenne went feuer waye wos vp hole ony taryeng thanked oure lorde grete grace ſhewed hys ſpouſe katheryne another notable myracle ſhall telle ſuſter penaunce whiche called johan dwellyng cyte sene tyme holy fader pope gregory lyued tyme cyte sene byddyng holy fader gregorye holy mayde ſent florence make pee betwene hym rebell child florēce ye whiche mat longe tell mater ſhall hau • chapytre hit ſelf afterward ye helpe god whan ſhe come florence wyth hyr felawe here whiche called johan trete pee betwene oure holy fader rebell people people ſette lytell hyr wordes ſ • laundred hyr meruayllouſly ſet hyr nought ne ſhe counſeylled withdrawe hyr whyle vnto tyme ceſſyd theyr malyce dyd ſo yet ſhe ſayd ſhe wold neuer paſſe cyte tyme accorded pee cryed thorugh cyte florence ſhe ſayde ſo thenne ſhe wente ſyde lodgyd lytell beſyde cyte ſodeynly hir ſuſter johan ſeek hyr foot ſo hyr foot forſwo •
