lord helpe wold wouche • auf mercyably helpe hyr fel • whyle ſhe prayed hyr ſuſter ſlepe whan ſhe awoke ſhe hole though ſhe ſykenes anone ſhe aroſe vp went wyth holy mayde quykly euer ſhe dyd afore ¶ myracle many one thanked lord ſawe whiche wrought ſoo gracyouſly hys ſpouſe katheryne yette ſhall tell another meruayllous thynge lord wrought hyr cyte tholetane whan holy mayde entred cyte tholetane ſhe took hir inne anone ſhe wente hir chambre ſhe wonte ye whiche mayſter reymond come pope meſſage sodeynly thenne herde ſtretys cyte wymmen holy wommā come entred cyte ne ſoone cam men wymmen hyr inne axed thys holy mayde inne myght hyde hyr ſuffred wymmen onely goo hyr ſpeke wyth hyr thenne ther one wommen hadde lytell chylde who whombe meruayllouſly ſwolle prayed holy mayde ſhe wold take childe hyr armes begynnyng ſhe refuſed cauſe vayn glorye • aſt ſhe ouercome pyte dyd hyr ſoone ſhe took chylde hir hondes anone ye childe deliuered moche wynde ſo laſt hys bely aſwagyd ſmall euer ſoo chylde hole mayſter reymond ſawe myracle yet ther ſo open ſpeche therof cyte tholetane yt came byſſhopys ere ſent mayſter reymond prayed hym myght ſpeke wyth ye holy mayde childe neuewe vycary hys holy mayde came ſpake wyth byſſhop many vertuous mater many moomeruayls lord wrought holy mayde ben wryten book theſe fewe haue wryten maydens cauſe ye ſhall ſonner gyue credence lord jheſu cryſte dwellyd holy maydens ſoule whiche principally wrought thyſe meruayllous werkys wytnes tho mater ye whiche ben reherced chapytre ben reherced afore tho place theſe racles ſhewed thus endeth chapytre ¶ myracles wrought thys holy mayde boute delyueraunce whiche encombred vexyd wyth fendes capitulum lx owre lorde myghty iheſu ceſſyd ſhewe outward ye fertue gaue inwarde hys ſpouſe katheryne many meruayllous werkes vertue therfore lorde iheſu cryſt angmented ſo myghtly breſt holy mayde onely ſhewed ſeek bodyes reherced afore alſo ſhewed voydyng wycked ſpyrytes ſhall declared chapytre helpe god ther cyte sene man whiche called mychael vſed craft wrytyng whan paſſed yeres age conſent hys wyf purpoſe leue ye worlde ſerue lord ſpecyally thenne wonte alſo make two doughters hys mynchyns monaſterye ſame cyte sene endowed worſhyp ſaynt johan enange lyſt ſo hys lyſt fulfylled laſt pryue dome god one doughts whiche made myn called laurencyana vill yere age aboute vexed fende ſo yt monaſterye vnquyeted hyr vexacyon ye laſt comyn aſſent ſent hyr fader delyuered ageyne hys doughter wold nomore haue hyr monaſterye long ſhe ſo vexed whan ſhe take monaſterye fende ſpak wythin hir ye childys mouth many wondre thynges latyn wordes ſo many herde queſtyōs ther pupplyſſhed many pryue ſynnes ſclaunder many folke ye whiche myght well vnderſtond yt good ſpyryte vexacyon hyr fader moder hir frendes ryght ſory wente aboute dyuerſe relyques ſentes ſeke helpe grace doughter myght delyuerd ſpiryte ſpecyally truſted gretely relyques ſaynt ambroſe whiche frere prechour whome lord graunted ſynguler gyfte put awaye wycked ſpyrytes ſoo hys cope yf layde vpon ony creature vexed wyth wicked ſpiryte ſholde auoyded fore ſame chylde brought frere prechours leyde vpon tombe ſaint ambroſe hys clothes leyde childe fader mod prayed mene whyl helpe ef god ye ſente yt chylde myght ſocourre yet tyme herde ſynne euer dyd trowe cauſe yt ſyguler remedyes reſerued holy mayde thenne counſeylled fad mod preſente hyr doughter pratheryne holy mayde ſent ye holy mayde prayenge hyr yt ſhe wolde helpe theyre doughter ſhe ſent ageyn anſwer ſayd often tymes defayled departed ſonder ſoule vtterly delyuered body neuertheleſſe lytell tyme ſorowe ne efteſones mayſter reymond axed hir long tyme hyr ſowle body ſayd kepte hyr aboute haue beryed hyr foure houres thēne ſhe reuyued ageyn yet axed hyr ſhe ſawe tyme came ſoule ageyne body ſhe anſwerd thus fader tyme ſowle ſawe vnderſtode ioye bleſſyd ſowles peynes ſynners myn mynde wold ſuffre wordes wolde ſuffyce expreſſe ſhall tell ſowle ſawe diuyne eſſen cyall beyng god cauſe ſoo lothe vnpacyent lyue worlde loue hym loue cryſten people whiche ſowle reſtoryd body ageyne ſholde defaylled dyed ſorowe hygheſt comfort haue whan ſuffre ony dyſeaſe haue perfyte vyſyon god therfore trybulacyons ben heuyſom comfortable ye may knowe ben conuerſaunt wyth ſawe alſo peynes dampned ſowles peynes ſowles ben purgatory whiche expreſſe perfytely wyth maner wordes yf wretched ſynners ſawe leſte peyne leuer cheſe bodely deth hondred tymes yf poſſyble thēne ſuffre daye leſte peyne ſpecially ſawe hem ponyſſhed ſyngulerly ſynned matrymony whiche hadde kepte hem gyder honeſtly ſholde folowed dylectacions theyr luſtys mayſter reymond hir confeſſour axed hyr ſynne ſpecyall greuouſly punyſſhed thenne ther ſynnes ſyth ſo moſt greuous ſynne ſayd ſkylle ſoo grete conſcyence ſynne ne ſo grete contrycyon ſynnes rather offended ſynne thenne ony ſynne whiche ſynner chargeth remoue penaū ce grete ſynne neuer ſoo lytell thenne holy mayde proceded forthe hyr mater ſayd thus alſo fader whāne ſeen thyſe ioyes thes peynes wenyng ſelf hadde fully delyuered body oure lorde ſayde ſeeſt thou doughter ioye lacke peyne haue offenden torne ageyn therfore thy body tell peple theyr errour theyr peryll wyth worde aſtonyed torne ageyne body ſore aferde thenne ford ſayd profyte mennys ſoules thou torne ageyne thou ſhalte lyue lyfe thou haſt lyued whiche preſēt paſſyng enformed auctor boke whiche capitulum primum whan hooly mayde katherine sene ſente cyte florens holy fader gregory xj whiche tyme pope rome reherſed afore ſeconde party make pea betwyne oure hooly fader pope child florence ſhe founde theym vnobedyent rebell amonges ſhe ſuffred moche perſecucion ſoo moche yt one drewe ſwerde wolde haue ſmyten hede ſo woode wyth thought letted vertu glorious lord almighti god yet notwythſtondyng ſuche perſecucion ſhe wolde neuer goo then vnto tyme pea cryed thorugh cyte florence pope gregory dayes dyed ye mene tyme▪ pope vrbans tyme dayes ye whiche pope hym who tyme pea made tyme pope made ſhe went home agayne cyte seene bylefte owne hous ful dylygently aboute making certayn boke whiche ſwte gloryous holy ghoſte endyted mouth owne langage prayed wryters whiche wrote boke yt thei ſholde conſydere beſely ſhe telleth thē tyme rauyſſhyng ſoo ſhe bad theym wryte thenne ſhe wente prayed ſone ſhe rauyſſhed bodely wyttes rauiſſhyng ſhe ſpake many ſwehe wordes ye whiche wordes wryters wrote ſhe ſpake ſoo compyled boke full profytable ſentence ſwete gloryous almyghty god tolde whiche endytyng one ſpecial thynge merueylous ſhewed alle yt comprehended wryten boke endyted dyuerſe time tyme rauyſſhyng neuer ellys ſoo ſame tyme ſhe ſoo rauyſſhed ſhe ſawe none bodely ſyght wyth eyen ne herde wyth eeres ne ſwellyd wyth noſe ne none bodely wyttes neyther hadde bodely workynge tyme yt ſhe rauyſſhyng ye may cō ſydere vnderſtonde ye boke endyted none naturall kyndely wytte infuſyon ſwete gloryous holy ghoſte ne doubte tho whiche bee vnderſtondyng men dylygently ſerche ſentences ſhall rede boke boke ſhullen ſay ſame ſaye tyme ſhe made boke oure holy fader pope vrbane vj knewe holy mayde auyoun grete deuoucion wordes vertuous lyuyng ſent mayſter reymound confeſſour ſholde ſtere come rme vyſyte ſain •• ben mayſter reymounde dyde ſoo ſhe ſoo full dyſcrecion ſhe anſwerd agayn wyſe fader many cyte sene alſo owne ſuſters cauſe mingoyng aboute hider thyder • en ſklandred therby ſeyn ſemely relyous mayde go ſo aboute hope oure gloryous lorde almyghty god haue offedyd myn goyng aboute obedyence gloryous lord almyghty god vycar erther helthe ſoule wente thyder went therfore leeſt ben theym mater ſklander myn wyll purpos remeue cyte ¶ neuertheles yf gloryous louely cryſtis vicar wyll algatis come wyll done myn therto praye goo hym praye voucheſaf ſende worde wyll whiche ben ſo ſklandred min goyng aboute ye maye clerly knowe toke iorney vpon min wyll mayſter reymound wente tolde pope mater ſente agayn hym ſhe ſholde come ye vertu obedyens thenne aſſone ſhe herd com̄aūdement trewe douhter obediens ſhe ſpedde faſte came rome grete company men wym̄en many moo wolde haue come ſhe forbede thē ▪ whan oure holy fader ye pope ſaw glad ioyeful deſyred yt ſhe ſhold ſeye ſom̄e word exortaciō ye cardinalis yt preſent namely ſciſme ye whiche began ſame tyme ſo ſhe dyde full vertuouſly made eche ſtedfaſtly ſtronge wyth many ſwete wordes ſentences counſeylled ſholde drede nothynge notwythſtondynge ſciſme whiche began ſtand myghtely drede noman procede forth thynges yt longen gloryous lord mighty ynow mayntene theym whan ſhe made ende wordes holy fader pope gladde reherſed wordes tournyng hys cardynales ſayde loo brederen vnfeytfull reprouable ben ſyght gloryous lorde almyghty god woman hath ſhamed v ſhe ſholde rather aferd thā cauſe ſhe woman yet aferde ſhe aferde conforted v wyth good counſeyls certen ought aſhamed wherfor ſholde gloryous lord god iheſus cryſtus vicar aferd▪ trewele though ye worlde agaynſt hym gloryous lord god iheſus cryſte myghtyer thē ne poſſyble wil forſake chyrche wyth ſuche wordes many moo lyke thyſe holy fader pope comforted cardinalis commaunded holy mayde gloryous lord god graunted ſelfe frendes many ſpecial grace within fewe dayes afterward came hooly faders mynde ſholde ſende holy mayde katheryne wyth nother maide called katheryne one ghoſtely doughters ſaint brygytte ſwethe whiche ſaint brygytte canonyſed pope bonefas ix▪ dame johan quene cycely openly rebelled agaynſt hooly chyrche gaue greate fauour sciſmatykes two maydens ye whiche well knowen wyth quene cycely ſholde wythdrawe errour thenne holy maide katheryn seene herde ſhe wolde none wyſe wythdrawe fro holy obedyens oblyſſhed ſelf goon ¶ katheryn ſwethe noo wyſe wolde take iournaye vpon refuſed preſence mayſter reymound thenne mayſter reymound bythought hym fame holy maydens ryght tendre lytyll •• otte ſynne thought gylty therin ſklaunderous theym alſo thought ſhe thyſe maiden ſholde ſente myght counſeyll many aboute lye awayte ye waye thyſe maydens ſholde come preſens ſoo letted purpos alſo maydens myght eſcape wythout grete ſklander al myght gyltles thyſe thoughtes mayſter reyymound tolde holy fader holy fader anſwerd ſayde thus thou ſeyſt well mayſter reymoūde better goo goo tyme mayſter reymound wente tolde holy mayde anone ſhe tourned mayſter reymound ſayde thus wyth myghty voyce fader yf ſaint agnes ſaint margarete maydens ſholde haue thought thus ſhold neuer haue crowne martyrdome whether haue ſpouſe delyuer v hondes wycked men kepe clenneſſe amonges fylthy companye lecherous meyny ſuche thoughtes ben veyn thoughtes come rather defaute lytyll feythe thenne wyſdome yt mayſter reymound thus made aſhamed imperfection yet hadde grete gladnes perfeccion conſyderyng nothynge herte ſtedfaſteneſſe ſtabylnes faythe neuertheles cauſe holy fader ordyned tho two maydens ſholde go journay durſte noo meue hym mater ¶ loo maydens reherſed cauſe ye ſhold know ſtedfaſtly holy maydes foot ſet feyth perfecciō ¶ furthermore whan holy tader ordeyned theſe maydens ſholde nott go ordeyned mayſter reymonde ſholde goo fraunce suppoſyng myght torne kyng charles hys errour enbaſſatour bytwene yere myght kynges herte ſo enduratin malyce wolde torne beganne auctor begȳner ſcyſme tyme mayſter reymond knewe wyll entent tader came aſke counſeyll holy mayde beſt hym thenne yt ſhe lothe wante hys preſence yet ſhe gaue hȳ coun • eylitor obeye byddyng oure holy fader among thynges ſhe ſayde thus hym ¶ fader vnderſtondeth treuthe pope urbanis veray cryſtys vycarye tooke holy obedyence vpon hym latell fore went holy mayde cōmyned wyth hym tolde hym foure houres fyue g • d reuelacyons comfortes oure lorde ſhewed hyr lytell afore whan ſhe do▪ ſhe ſayde wordes ¶ fader goth lord ſpede trowe ſhal neuer lyf ſpeke ſo moche gyder haue nowe lyke ſhe ſayd ſo thenne mayſter reymonde came ageyne ſhe paſſed world furthermore cauſe ſhe wolde fully take hyr leue hym ſhe went ꝑſonally ſame place ſhold take hys galey ¶ whan began rowe ſhe kneiyd doune prayed afterward blyſſed galey wyth wepyng chere ſayd pryuely herde mayſter reymond ¶ thou lone ſhalt go ſaue croſſe ſhall kepe thou ſhalt neuer ſee thy moder lyf ¶ ſhe ꝓphecyed ſoo ther many enemyes • ee yet went ſaue awaye alſo mene tyme oute holy mayde paſſyd worlde ¶ fyrſt tell hyr blyſſed paſſyng world ſhall come home thys holy maydes paſſyng ſhe lyued longe ¶ ſeconde wytnes francyſca sene francyſca deuoute ſoule god holy mayde hertely loue wherfore whan hyr huſbounde dede ſhe toke abyte penaunce made ſyſter saynte domynyk ¶ thys francyſca enfourmed mayſter raymonde whan came home many folke maydes paſſyng thenne ſhe deyed ſoone allexe¶ thyrde wytnes lyſa hyr coſyn whiche wyll notte commende ſhe ryght trewe cauſe ſhe holy maydes brother wyf ſhold beholde ſuſpect wytnes amonge men ¶ many men hir paſſyng whiche beren trewe recorde othyr buſſed ende¶ foure ſpecyall thȳke reherſe ye whiche ryght vertuous men ¶ fyrſt called frere sanctus whiche bothe holy indede name holy man forſoke hys kynne came cyte ene lyued vertuouſly xxx yere ancheres lyfe ¶ herde ſpeke holy mayde ſtyred ſpeke wyth hyr ſo dyd enfourmed hyr ¶ laſt thout better walke oute cell wynne ſoules thenne ſo encloſed ſo dyd counſeyll went oute folowed thys holy mayde wan ſoules cryſte ſpecyally preſente wyth hyr hyr paſſyng¶ thys holy man enfourmed mayſter raymonde alſo whan came home paſſing holy mayd ſoone dyed ¶ ſeconde witnes men yong man age olde vertu whiche called barductyne ¶ thys yong man forſoke hys kynne folowed holy mayde hyr tyll ſhe paſſyd whome ſhe loued yettenderly cauſe mayde meruaylle ſemely oo mayde ſholde loue another ¶ whome holy mayde ſayd chargyd hym ſhold gouerned mayſter raymondis coū ſeyll ¶ cauſe trowe ſhe moche ſhe knewe well god ſholde long lyue hyr ſoo dyde teſyk fyrſte contynued longe therynne amended medycines laſt dyde theron cauſe mayſter raymonde drede hym ayre rome ſhol • e enfecte hym ſente hym sene paſſyd worlde bere wytnes yt hys paſſynge whan ſholde paſſe loked vp heuen began ſmyle ſoo wyth ſmylyng paſſyd tyme paſſyd token gladnes appyred hys face trowe therfore maydes wryters ye ſhe wrote bothe hyr letter ſhe ſente alſo hyrbook holy ghoſt endyted hyr whiche yong man holy mayde called hyr whan ſhe ſholde paſſe ſayd thus sone wyll god thou monke charterhous therfore charge yu ſo doo ſhe bad hym ſo dyd lyued euer afterward ꝑfyt lyf hadno felawe ꝑfeccyon relygyon aſſone profeſſyd made pryor ye ſame hous ſhorne inne ¶ afterward made pryour another place ſame ordre melayne viſitour ordre yong man stephen wrote certeyn thynges happed paſſyng holy mayde ētfourmed afterwarde mayſter raymonde ſame whan came home fourthe laſt wytneſſe men ye paſſyng holy hyr fyrſt men forſoke hys kynne folowed holy mayde cauſe knewe hyr vertuous lyuyng longe tyme therfore mayſter reymond called hym hym made hym ſpecyall wytnes makyng hyr legende felawe alſo stephen pryour charterhous theſe men theſe wymmen enfourmed mayſter reymond whan came home thynges whyche done hys abſence well tho thynges ſhe dyd ſhe paſte tho thynges ſhe ſhewed dyd hyr paſſyng thus endeth chapytre ¶ meruayllous thynges whyche befyll yere half fore ye deth holy mayden martyrdom ſhe ſuffred bodely wycked fendes atlaſt ſhe hadde hyr bodely deth capitulum ſecundum tyme ye mayſter reymond wente fro holy mayde reherſed afore byddyng holy fader pope ſhe belefte cyte rome lorde dede hyr ſhe deyed ſhewed holy lyuyng ſhe alſo ioye gaue hyr ſhe paſſyd worlde ſhall tell ¶ leue well maydens whan holy mayde perceyued ſo moche dyſeaſe encrecyd holy chyrche ſcyſme yt begonne perceyuyng alſo cryſtys vycarye ſuffred grete dyſeaſe ſhe wept day nyght prayed lord pee wold woucheſauf ſet pee holy chyrche thenne lord comforted hyr ſom maner wyſe yere afore half ſhe dyed oure lorde gaue double vyctorye holy chyrche cryſtys vycarye pope well caſtell saynt angell cyte rome whiche ſcyſmatykes hondes daye people helde caſtell name ſcyſmatykes ye ſame daye take caſtell yolde holy fader pope myght dwelle rome wonte cauſe enemyes caſtell saynt aungell knowe cam holy mayde axed hir counſeyll ſholde thenne ſhe gaue hym counſeyll ſhold go barfoot people rome wyth hym mynſter saynt peter thankynge lord god wyth good deuocyon grace benefetys whiche thus holy chyrche beganne quyken holy mayde hadde therof grete comfort ſoone hir ſorowe began encrece eftſonis fende myght ſtrayn gers aſſayed cyte rome made dyſoorde bytwene ye people cyte pope perceyued holy mayde ſhe prayed lord wolde woucheſauf put hys mercyable honde ſuffre curſyd ſynne done ſhe prayed ſhe ſawe cyte full fendes ſtyryng excytyng people kylle theyr ghooſtly fader cryed horrybly holy mayde whyle ſhe prayed ſeynge hyr thus thou curſed wretche thou arte aboute lette v therfore ſhall ſlee wyth horryble deth whome ſhe anſwerd worde prayed beſyly feruently axyng lord wold woucheſ auf worſhyp hys holy name remedye holy chyrche thenne ſtood grete meſhyef kepe hyr hys vycarye wythout harme ſuffre peple ſuche ſynne ſo put awaye fendes fro theyr purpoſe whiche ſteryng people ther hadde anſwere lord doughter ſuff • mekeſt myldeſt lord thou knoweſt well thy ſpouſe holy chyrche dyſeaſed tormented almoſt thorugh world routhe thou knoweſt well alſo ſewe helper defender ſhe hath therfore yf ſlee thy vy carye ben mercyable honde ceſſe myſhyef prayer ſhe contynued many dayes gyder ſhe wrote mayſter reymond letter euer lord alledgyng ryghtwyſnes ſhe axyng mercy tyme fendes cryed ho •• ybly vpon hir reherſed forthward grutchyng ceſſyd peopl • ly •• lytell hyr paſſyons encreced ſo ferforth ſerpentes hell power god • rmented hyr body cruely vncredyble man byleue yf hadde ſeen ſayden ſawe ther p • eſente whanne hyr body au • tyſhed ſawe ſerpentes fretted deuoured ſo maydens body therin lefte bone without ſkynne though ben conſumed waſted long lyeng erthe yet neuerthe ••• ſhe walked prayde ſhe wonte whiche many folke wonder thyng ſhe ſemed rather wonder thyng loke vpon ne naturell thyng hyr tormentes payne encreced contynually whyche ſhe conſumed yet ſhe ceſſyd prayer ſhe prayed • ore feruently len • er thenne ſhe wonte hyr ghooſtly chyldren ſhe hadde nouryſſhed vertue ſame tyme ſawe openly markes ſtrokes • endes helle gaue hyr hyr bodye myght therto remedy two ſkylles one wyſte well hit wyll god whome myght wythſtonde another cauſe ſawe hyr gladde ioyfull hyr paynes ſhe prayed hyr bodely payne yet wolde ſhe ceſſe therfore tormentours helle faylled cryed vpon hyr alle tyme ſayde hyr thus curſed wr • tche thou haſt euer ageynſt v therfore thy tyme come auenged vpon thou haſte putte v oft • tymes praye therfore ſhall neuer ceſſe vnto tyme thou arte oute thys • yf thys ſhe ſente whiche vpon ſondaye yere lord thouſand thre hondred foure ſ • ore whyche daye feſte saynt peter martyr ordre frece prechours ſolempnyſed holy chyrche ¶ many notable thynges wroughte thenne hyr paſſyng whiche ſhe mayde book generally ſhort • ly wryten book wyth ſame oryſon capitulum • ij whanne ende bodely lyf blyſſed mayde katheryn drewe faſte vpon hyr oure lorde ſhewed ioye hyr hyr paſſyng dyuers therfore purpoſe tranſlate none wyſe thenne ſhe ſayde worde worde tho two thynges theſe fyrſt recapytulacyon ſame book ſette ende whiche reherſed ſhortly tho thynges ben dyffuſely ſette book afore axe counſeyll mayſter reymond doubte euer hadde furthermore ſhe ſaye whan came home yt faylle ne aferde noo thyng ſhall falle euer contynue vertuouſly ſhe ſayd ſhe wolde wyth hym delyuer hym peryll whan doth ony thyng ſholde ſhall gyue hym warnyng ſhe ſayde amende thyſe wordes ſhe ſayd often tymes tha laſt ende hir paſſyng laſt worde ſhe ſayd domine manus tuas comnendo ſpiritum meum ſo blyſſed deuoute matrone vnderſtood better myght mene ſoo whens myght come whiche matrone ſhall tell ſame tyme whan holy mayde paſſyd worlde rome deuoute matrone called semya whiche hadde two men hyr ſones whome ſhe euery daye bothe moder ſeruant makyng theyr mete thys deuoute matrone tyme hyr huſbonde dede ſhe purpoſed euer ſerue god viſyte pylgrymage holy ſayntes rome ſhe continued many yeres hadde alſo cuſtome ryſe mydnyght praye afterward take lytell reſt ſyttyng lenyng wyth hyr hede ſhe myght quycker morowe erly go hyr ſtacyons rome befyll ſoone whan holy mayde katheryn come rome deuoute matrone took knowleche hyr often tymes edyfyed hyr good exhortacyons ſoo hadde good ghooſtly affeccyon hyr ofte tymes homely wyth hyr hyr hows almoſt euery daye neuertheles • ytell afore holy mayde hadde et • ſhe wente katherynes hous knockyd dore herde none anſwere ſayd hyr ye neyghboures yt ſhe walkyd vyſyte holy place yet treuthe hir ſuſters wythin waylyng wolde ſuffre none entre tyme hadde axyd counſeyll ſhold • body laſt determyned amonges morowe body ſhold ladde frere prechours ye ſeruyſe god wold ordeyne counſeyll ſo done ſoone body come ye chyrche ye people folowed touche hir fet • hir clothys ſo bothe ye freres alſo hir ſuſtres hir dyſciples aferde leſt ſholde haue borſte toren hyr clothys therfore ſette body wythin chauntell chapell endued worſhyp saynt domynyk fyll afterwarde pacyence ſhe hadde ꝑſecucyons gladde ſhe ther inne clerely declared fourthe chapytre fyrſt partye meruayllouſly vertuouſly alwaye ſhe ſtode purpoſe maydenhode yet ſerued houſholde wyth gladde chere neuer ſuche occupacyons pryuacyons hyr pure chambre ſhe ceſſyd fro prayer ghooſtly excercyſes vn tyme ſhe hadde ouercome bothe hyr perſecucyons hyr purſuers reherſed ſame fourthe chapytre yet ouermore whan fende ſtyred hyr moder lapa ſette holy mayde holy dyſcyplynes wakynges alſo herde lyggyng • thys holy mayde thenne wyth myghty pacyence meruayllous tempred ryght dyſcretely hyr moders heuynes ageynſt hyr yet neuertheleſſe kepte forthe hyr hardenes lyuyng declared vj chapytre fyrſt partye fully ynough moreouer impediment ſhe ſuffred hyr ſowle fende tyme prayer ghooſtly excercyſes tormentyng hyr fleſſhe almes dedes ſhe dyd openly ſhewed many dyuers chapytres thys legende afore ſhall declare fende beſyed hym myght fyrſt remeue thys holy mayde awaye hyr ſpouſe jheſu afterward wythdrawe hir fully hym ellys laſte lette hyr namely tyme ſhe wyth myghty feruour fyrſt ouerthrewe hyr enemye fende afterward wytte counſeyll holy ghooſt ouercome hym laſt wyth ſtedefaſt vertue ſhamed hym aboute moder full purpoſe marye hir hit ſhewed ſame chapytre thrydde tyme hym ſelfe puttyng hyr dyuers heuynes temptacyons dyuers illuſyons thenne ſhe receyued habyte penaunce reherſed vij chapytre fyrſt whiche illuſyon curyoſyte ſhe dyſpyſed blyſſed hyr torned hyr crucyfyxe fende vanyſſhed awaye yet lefte hyr mynde temptacyon curyoſytre clothyng thenne anone ſhe hadde myne hir purpoſe maydenhode ſpak lord wyſe dere lord ſwete ſpouſe thou knoweſt well deſyred neuer huſbonde therfore praye helpe may ouercome theſe temptacyons curyoſyte vertue thyne holy name axe lord thou ſholdeſt take awaye fro yt thou woucheſauf gyue vyctorye thy mercy ſoone ſhe hadde ſayde theſe wordes blyſſed lady quene maydens apperyd hyr ſyght ſemyng hyr ſyght ſhe took oute ryght fayre clothe hyr ſones ſyde wyth whiche clothe ſhe arrayed hyr afterward ſhe ſayde thys holy mayde thus▪ well wete doughter clothes whiche comen oute ſones ſyde paſſen clothes fayrnes beaute thenne alle hyr temptacyon wente awaye ſhe whan ſhe aboute lette hyr hyr penaunce doyng contynued afterwarde neuertheleſſe hyr penaunce ſhe began▪ alſo whan ſhe bare hir ſelf ſo wyſely hir confeſſour counſeyllours whiche counſeylled hyr leue hyr grete abſtynence lyue comyndyete declared fyfthe chapytre ſeconde partye alſo wyſely meruayllouſly ſhe peſyd hir ſoueraynes forbode hir go place thyder lorde ſente hyr yet ſhe fulfylled goddes byddynges eſely peſyd hyr ſoueraynes pacyence ſhe hadde werke ther noo tongue tell ne penne wryte furthermore fende ſaw myght noo whyle remeue ne wythdrawe thys holy mayde hir deuoute purpoſe beſyed namely certeyne tyme lette hyr onely hym ſelf dyuers perſones whiche ſhall tolde ſpecyally wythinne forthe fyrſt hyr owne moder lapa brought hyr bath bathed ſhe myght eſy bath wythdrawe tyme fro hyr ſharpe dyſciplynes hardeneſſe penaunce yet ſhe coude fynde ther ſharpe penaunce thenne hir owne chambre whan ſhe ſuffred hote brennyng water vpon hyr naked body • reherſed ſeuenthe chapytre fyrſt neuertheleſſe ſomme ſhall reherſe ſpecyall ben ſpoken ſame chapytre ſomme thynges may reherſed wythout ſhame ſom relygyous perſonys whiche cō trarye hyr holy purpoſe yet better reherſed thenne gyftes holy ghooſt hydde ye maydens may haue loue drede bothe ſuche treſpaſſes ſuche relygyous folke loue ſeyeng vertue pacyence holy mayde holy mayde katheryne tyme ſhe hadde ſauoure ſwetenes deuocyon ſhe fyfthe chapytre ſecounde partye yf ghooſtly lyuers quenche perfytely hyr propre wyll ſelf fall cruelly dyche enuye thenne fleſſhely lyuers putte exſample therof monkes holy abbotte pachamye grete abſtynence newe monke come amonges ſayd theywold goo momaſterye yf newe monke auoyded ryght ſo befyll wyth holy mayde alle ſuſters penaunce ſawe katheryne paſſyd alle hardenes lyuyng ſadnes vertue deuocion prayer contemplacyon anone ſerpente enuye entred ſtyred bacbyte holy mayde bothe pryuely alſo openly prelate ordre wyth grete boldenes yet holde moſte ſadde helde wyth ſayd myght ellys • ſhe wrought euer ſhe dyd belſabub prynce deuelys thys womman ſuche falſe ſuggeſtyon drewe vnto theyr errour many ſad folke bothe relygyous ſeculers ſoo theyr counſeyll thys holy mayde ofte tymes lette hyr confeſſyon hyr confeſſour alſo receyuyng blyſſed ſacrament ſhe ſuffred pacyently wythout ony grutchyng playnyng rather ſuppoſyng ſo lette hyr dyd holy entente helthe hyr ſoule fore hyr ſemed ſhe ye bounde praye hyr enemyes hyr ſpecyall frendes yet aboue whan ſhe whyle ſuffred houſelyd receyuyng ye blyſſed ſacrament aulter wolde ſuffre hyr afterward abyde long prayer ſhe wonte whiche hyr vnpoſſyble cauſe ſhe receyued wyth ſuche paſſyng feruour deuocyon ſoo euer ſoone hyr ſpyryte rauyſſhed fro hyr bodely wyttes ſo ſhe abode many houres gydre declared afore ſeconde laſte chapytre ſeconde partye ſoone ſhe aſpyed wyſe ſom dyſceyued forſayde ſuſters wolde come inne drawe hir chyrche ofte tymes ſhe ſholde lye ſonne whan moſt hoteſt aboute mydde daye long tyme gyders thenne ſhe ceſſyd hyr rauyſſhynge reſtored hyr bodely wyttes ther wyth wepyng waylyng ſomme▪ hir ſuſters vertuouſly ſtyred grace kepte hyr tyll ſhe reſtoryd alſo came another man came tyme founde hyr lye dede womman rauyſſhyng wyth grete angre wente hir ſporlyd hyr wyth hys foot whanne ſhe reſtoryd hyr bodely wyttes ageyne tolde hyr ſhe ferde wyth yet ſhe wolde neuer blame hem therfore rather excuſe hem whan ſpake euyll hem neuertheles punyſſhed lorde full harde grete ſorowe hyr ſaue ſhe durſt long ſtryue ageynſt hys ryghtwyſneſſe tyme lady hadde grete indygnacyon holy mayde whan ſhe ſawe hyr ſuche rauyſſhyng wherfore ſhe came hir ſporlyd hyr wyth hyr foot ſoone ſhe come home hyr owne place ſhe dyed wythout receyuyng ony ſacrament alſo another wretche ſporled hir ſame wyſe whā ſhe ſoo rauyſſhed alſo one tho one tyme bare hir chyrche whan ſhe ſoo rauyſſhed full vyolently punyſſhed afterward ferde tell thys wretchyd man ſoo enuyous ſoo odyous thys blyſſed mayde wythſtondyng alle formeſt curſed holy mayde vyrgyr aſked forgyuenes af curſed accuſacion ſhe ſhlaundred ſhe ſent tolde theym ſhe hadde falſely accuſed hooly mayde vyrgyn wherfore ſhe aſked theym forgyuenes thenne ſhe tolde theym ſhe wyth rightfully mercyfully ſhe worthy dampned paynes helle thenne lorde jheſu cryſte anſwered ſayde doughter ryghtuoſneſſe done god fader ſynnes ſatyſfaction fully made hym theym ryghtuouſneſſe aſketh yf thou haue offen dyd god wyth membrys thy body •• ormentyd membris body thyn man kindes ſynnes yf thou treſpaſed wyth honde wyth fete handy foot nayled croſſe wyth harde nayles▪ yf thou haue treſpaſed wyth thy eyen▪ myn eye blynfyld wyth clothe yf thou haue treſpaſed wyth thyn • erys myn • rys herde blaſphemes grete wronges yf yu haue treſpaſed wyth thyn herte herte perſed wyth ſpere yf thou haue offendyd wyth thy body body ſhorged ſoo ſole fote vnto tope hede apperyd noo ſtede hole ¶ therfore doughter thynke dew ſatyſfaccion thy ſynnes▪ doo full ryght wyſly god fader sothely • uffred paynes ſynfull wronges theym bare herte dyde ſynne ne gyle founden mouth ¶ another tyme whan elyſabeth goddes ſeruaunt prayeng sodenly ſhe ſawe wyth ghoſtely eyen full fayre honde hadde longe fyngers palme large brode myddes palme wounde redde blode ſoone ſhe vnderſtode honde cryſte wondrede ſoo ſmall ſoo longe alſo ne anſwerde her▪ ſo ſmall whiche cryſt lyued fleſſhe nyghtes prayed helde hondes ſtreyth forth dayes▪ • aueyled wyth hondes fete body tounes caſtellys prechynge kyngdome god ſhe herde voyce ſayeng elyſabeth loo thyrde tyme ſaye thy ſynnes ben fogyuen thou haſt grace whiche voyce ſhe anſwerde lord yf bee halowed thou ſayſte whero • maye wythholde offende thy mayeſte eche daye ſomme thynge voyce ſayde yf thou noo tyme offended thou ſholde ſo mocho mekyd folowed thou woldeſt loue ſoo moche thus thou ſholdeſt waxe worſe thenne fendes truſteth dredeth ¶ therfore haue ſoo haloweth ye thou maye ſynne▪ ſuffyſeth haue gyue ſoo moche grace wolde ſuffre thy ſelf ſlayne rather thenne thou ſholdeſt offēde dedely whan thys ſayd cryſt apperyd openly thought thyke lopred blode largely flowed oute hys ſyde wherfore ſhe beganne wonder cryſt ſayde doughter wonder whan hangyd croſſe membrys dyſioynyd ioynte vndone treſpaſſe myn entrayles broken veynes opened ¶ therfore ſoo haboundaunt thyke lopered b • ode folowed ſyde thyſe thinges ſayd sayn • elyſabeth boute endyng lyff whiche yere lorde cclxi affermyng ſhe hadde ſeyn herde aboue wryton ¶ ſhe ſayd ſhe hadde ſo grete certayne ſhe wolde rather ſuffre dethe thē ne doubte ony lytyll parte trewe ¶ endeth
